1|1|bismillāhir-raḥmānir-raḥīm
1|2|al-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbil-'ālamīn
1|3|ar-raḥmānir-raḥīm
1|4|māliki yaumid-dīn
1|5|iyyāka na'budu wa iyyāka nasta'īn
1|6|ihdinaṣ-ṣirāṭal-mustaqīm
1|7|ṣirāṭallażīna an'amta 'alaihim gairil-magḍụbi 'alaihim wa laḍ-ḍ<b>ā</b>llīn
2|1|alif l<b>ā</b>m m<b>ī</b>m
2|2|żālikal-kitābu lā raiba fīh, hudal lil-muttaqīn
2|3|allażīna yu`minụna bil-gaibi wa yuqīmụnaṣ-ṣalāta wa mimmā razaqnāhum yunfiqụn
2|4|wallażīna yu`minụna bim<b>ā</b> unzila ilaika wa m<b>ā</b> unzila ming qablik, wa bil-ākhirati hum yụqinụn
2|5|ul<b>ā</b>`ika 'alā hudam mir rabbihim wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-mufliḥụn
2|6|innallażīna kafarụ saw<b>ā</b>`un 'alaihim a anżartahum am lam tunżir-hum lā yu`minụn
2|7|khatamallāhu 'alā qulụbihim wa 'alā sam'ihim, wa 'al<b>ā</b> abṣārihim gisyāwatuw wa lahum 'ażābun 'aẓīm
2|8|wa minan-nāsi may yaqụlu āmannā billāhi wa bil-yaumil-ākhiri wa mā hum bimu`minīn
2|9|yukhādi'ụnallāha wallażīna āmanụ, wa mā yakhda'ụna ill<b>ā</b> anfusahum wa mā yasy'urụn
2|10|fī qulụbihim maraḍun fa zādahumullāhu maraḍā, wa lahum 'ażābun alīmum bimā kānụ yakżibụn
2|11|wa iżā qīla lahum lā tufsidụ fil arḍi qāl<b>ū</b> innamā naḥnu muṣliḥụn
2|12|al<b>ā</b> innahum humul-mufsidụna wa lākil lā yasy'urụn
2|13|wa iżā qīla lahum āminụ kam<b>ā</b> āmanan-nāsu qāl<b>ū</b> a nu`minu kam<b>ā</b> āmanas-sufah<b>ā</b>`, al<b>ā</b> innahum humus-sufah<b>ā</b>`u wa lākil lā ya'lamụn
2|14|wa iżā laqullażīna āmanụ qāl<b>ū</b> āmannā, wa iżā khalau ilā syayāṭīnihim qāl<b>ū</b> innā ma'akum innamā naḥnu mustahzi`ụn
2|15|allāhu yastahzi`u bihim wa yamudduhum fī ṭugyānihim ya'mahụn
2|16|ul<b>ā</b>`ikallażīnasytarawuḍ-ḍalālata bil-hudā fa mā rabiḥat tijāratuhum wa mā kānụ muhtadīn
2|17|maṡaluhum kamaṡalillażistauqada nārā, fa lamm<b>ā</b> aḍ<b>ā</b>`at mā ḥaulahụ żahaballāhu binụrihim wa tarakahum fī ẓulumātil lā yubṣirụn
2|18|ṣummum bukmun 'umyun fa hum lā yarji'ụn
2|19|au kaṣayyibim minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i fīhi ẓulumātuw wa ra'duw wa barq, yaj'alụna aṣābi'ahum f<b>ī</b> āżānihim minaṣ-ṣawā'iqi ḥażaral-maụt, wallāhu muḥīṭum bil-kāfirīn
2|20|yakādul-barqu yakhṭafu abṣārahum, kullam<b>ā</b> aḍ<b>ā</b>`a lahum masyau fīhi wa iż<b>ā</b> aẓlama 'alaihim qāmụ, walau sy<b>ā</b>`allāhu lażahaba bisam'ihim wa abṣārihim, innallāha 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
2|21|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsu'budụ rabbakumullażī khalaqakum wallażīna ming qablikum la'allakum tattaqụn
2|22|allażī ja'ala lakumul-arḍa firāsyaw was-sam<b>ā</b>`a bin<b>ā</b>`aw wa anzala minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i m<b>ā</b>`an fa akhraja bihī minaṡ-ṡamarāti rizqal lakum, fa lā taj'alụ lillāhi andādaw wa antum ta'lamụn
2|23|wa ing kuntum fī raibim mimmā nazzalnā 'alā 'abdinā fa`tụ bisụratim mim miṡlihī wad'ụ syuhad<b>ā</b>`akum min dụnillāhi ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
2|24|fa il lam taf'alụ wa lan taf'alụ fattaqun-nārallatī waqụduhan-nāsu wal-ḥijāratu u'iddat lil-kāfirīn
2|25|wa basysyirillażīna āmanụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāti anna lahum jannātin tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hār, kullamā ruziqụ min-hā min ṡamaratir rizqang qālụ hāżallażī ruziqnā ming qablu wa utụ bihī mutasyābihā, wa lahum fīh<b>ā</b> azwājum muṭahharatuw wa hum fīhā khālidụn
2|26|innallāha lā yastaḥy<b>ī</b> ay yaḍriba maṡalam mā ba'ụḍatan fa mā fauqahā, fa ammallażīna āmanụ fa ya'lamụna annahul-ḥaqqu mir rabbihim, wa ammallażīna kafarụ fa yaqụlụna māż<b>ā</b> arādallāhu bihāżā maṡalā, yuḍillu bihī kaṡīraw wa yahdī bihī kaṡīrā, wa mā yuḍillu bih<b>ī</b> illal-fāsiqīn
2|27|allażīna yangquḍụna 'ahdallāhi mim ba'di mīṡāqihī wa yaqṭa'ụna m<b>ā</b> amarallāhu bih<b>ī</b> ay yụṣala wa yufsidụna fil-arḍ, ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-khāsirụn
2|28|kaifa takfurụna billāhi wa kuntum amwātan fa aḥyākum, ṡumma yumītukum ṡumma yuḥyīkum ṡumma ilaihi turja'ụn
2|29|huwallażī khalaqa lakum mā fil-arḍi jamī'an ṡummastaw<b>ā</b> ilas-sam<b>ā</b>`i fa sawwāhunna sab'a samāwāt, wa huwa bikulli syai`in 'alīm
2|30|wa iż qāla rabbuka lil-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati innī jā'ilun fil-arḍi khalīfah, qāl<b>ū</b> a taj'alu fīhā may yufsidu fīhā wa yasfikud-dim<b>ā</b>`, wa naḥnu nusabbiḥu biḥamdika wa nuqaddisu lak, qāla inn<b>ī</b> a'lamu mā lā ta'lamụn
2|31|wa 'allama ādamal-asm<b>ā</b>`a kullahā ṡumma 'araḍahum 'alal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati fa qāla ambi`ụnī bi`asm<b>ā</b>`i h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`i ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
2|32|qālụ sub-ḥānaka lā 'ilma lan<b>ā</b> illā mā 'allamtanā, innaka antal-'alīmul-ḥakīm
2|33|qāla y<b>ā</b> ādamu ambi`hum bi`asm<b>ā</b>`ihim, fa lamm<b>ā</b> amba`ahum bi`asm<b>ā</b>`ihim qāla a lam aqul lakum inn<b>ī</b> a'lamu gaibas-samāwāti wal-arḍi wa a'lamu mā tubdụna wa mā kuntum taktumụn
2|34|wa iż qulnā lil-mal<b>ā</b>`ikatisjudụ li`ādama fa sajad<b>ū</b> ill<b>ā</b> iblīs, abā wastakbara wa kāna minal-kāfirīn
2|35|wa qulnā y<b>ā</b> ādamuskun anta wa zaujukal-jannata wa kulā min-hā ragadan ḥaiṡu syi`tumā wa lā taqrabā hāżihisy-syajarata fa takụnā minaẓ-ẓālimīn
2|36|fa azallahumasy-syaiṭānu 'an-hā fa akhrajahumā mimmā kānā fīhi wa qulnahbiṭụ ba'ḍukum liba'ḍin 'aduww, wa lakum fil-arḍi mustaqarruw wa matā'un ilā ḥīn
2|37|fa talaqq<b>ā</b> ādamu mir rabbihī kalimātin fa tāba 'alaīh, innahụ huwat-tawwābur-raḥīm
2|38|qulnahbiṭụ min-hā jamī'ā, fa immā ya`tiyannakum minnī hudan fa man tabi'a hudāya fa lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
2|39|wallażīna kafarụ wa każżabụ bi`āyātin<b>ā</b> ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
2|40|yā ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īlażkurụ ni'matiyallat<b>ī</b> an'amtu 'alaikum wa aufụ bi'ahd<b>ī</b> ụfi bi'ahdikum, wa iyyāya far-habụn
2|41|wa āminụ bim<b>ā</b> anzaltu muṣaddiqal limā ma'akum wa lā takụn<b>ū</b> awwala kāfirim bihī wa lā tasytarụ bi`āyātī ṡamanang qalīlaw wa iyyāya fattaqụn
2|42|wa lā talbisul-ḥaqqa bil-bāṭili wa taktumul-ḥaqqa wa antum ta'lamụn
2|43|wa aqīmuṣ-ṣalāta wa ātuz-zakāta warka'ụ ma'ar-rāki'īn
2|44|a ta`murụnan-nāsa bil-birri wa tansauna anfusakum wa antum tatlụnal-kitāb, a fa lā ta'qilụn
2|45|wasta'īnụ biṣ-ṣabri waṣ-ṣalāh, wa innahā lakabīratun illā 'alal-khāsyi'īn
2|46|allażīna yaẓunnụna annahum mulāqụ rabbihim wa annahum ilaihi rāji'ụn
2|47|yā ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īlażkurụ ni'matiyallat<b>ī</b> an'amtu 'alaikum wa annī faḍḍaltukum 'alal-'ālamīn
2|48|wattaqụ yaumal lā tajzī nafsun 'an nafsin syai`aw wa lā yuqbalu min-hā syafā'atuw wa lā yu`khażu min-hā 'adluw wa lā hum yunṣarụn
2|49|wa iż najjainākum min āli fir'auna yasụmụnakum s<b>ū</b>`al-'ażābi yużabbiḥụna abn<b>ā</b>`akum wa yastaḥyụna nis<b>ā</b>`akum, wa fī żālikum bal<b>ā</b>`um mir rabbikum 'aẓīm
2|50|wa iż faraqnā bikumul-baḥra fa anjainākum wa agraqn<b>ā</b> āla fir'auna wa antum tanẓurụn
2|51|wa iż wā'adnā mụs<b>ā</b> arba'īna lailatan ṡummattakhażtumul-'ijla mim ba'dihī wa antum ẓālimụn
2|52|ṡumma 'afaunā 'angkum mim ba'di żālika la'allakum tasykurụn
2|53|wa iż ātainā mụsal-kitāba wal-furqāna la'allakum tahtadụn
2|54|wa iż qāla mụsā liqaumihī yā qaumi innakum ẓalamtum anfusakum bittikhāżikumul-'ijla fa tụb<b>ū</b> ilā bāri`ikum faqtul<b>ū</b> anfusakum, żālikum khairul lakum 'inda bāri`ikum, fa tāba 'alaikum, innahụ huwat-tawwābur-raḥīm
2|55|wa iż qultum yā mụsā lan nu`mina laka ḥattā narallāha jahratan fa akhażatkumuṣ-ṣā'iqatu wa antum tanẓurụn
2|56|ṡumma ba'aṡnākum mim ba'di mautikum la'allakum tasykurụn
2|57|wa ẓallalnā 'alaikumul-gamāma wa anzalnā 'alaikumul-manna was-salwā, kulụ min ṭayyibāti mā razaqnākum, wa mā ẓalamụnā wa lāking kān<b>ū</b> anfusahum yaẓlimụn
2|58|wa iż qulnadkhulụ hāżihil-qaryata fa kulụ min-hā ḥaiṡu syi`tum ragadaw wadkhulul-bāba sujjadaw wa qụlụ ḥiṭṭatun nagfir lakum khaṭāyākum, wa sanazīdul-muḥsinīn
2|59|fa baddalallażīna ẓalamụ qaulan gairallażī qīla lahum fa anzalnā 'alallażīna ẓalamụ rijzam minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i bimā kānụ yafsuqụn
2|60|wa iżistasqā mụsā liqaumihī fa qulnaḍrib bi'aṣākal-ḥajar, fanfajarat min-huṡnatā 'asyrata 'ainā, qad 'alima kullu unāsim masyrabahum, kulụ wasyrabụ mir rizqillāhi wa lā ta'ṡau fil-arḍi mufsidīn
2|61|wa iż qultum yā mụsā lan naṣbira 'alā ṭa'āmiw wāḥidin fad'u lanā rabbaka yukhrij lanā mimmā tumbitul-arḍu mim baqlihā wa qiṡṡ<b>ā</b>`ihā wa fụmihā wa 'adasihā wa baṣalihā, qāla a tastabdilụnallażī huwa adnā billażī huwa khaīr, ihbiṭụ miṣran fa inna lakum mā sa`altum, wa ḍuribat 'alaihimuż-żillatu wal-maskanatu wa b<b>ā</b>`ụ bigaḍabim minallāh, żālika bi`annahum kānụ yakfurụna bi`āyātillāhi wa yaqtulụnan-nabiyyīna bigairil-ḥaqq, żālika bimā 'aṣaw wa kānụ ya'tadụn
2|62|innallażīna āmanụ wallażīna hādụ wan-naṣārā waṣ-ṣābi`īna man āmana billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri wa 'amila ṣāliḥan fa lahum ajruhum 'inda rabbihim, wa lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
2|63|wa iż akhażnā mīṡāqakum wa rafa'nā fauqakumuṭ-ṭụr, khużụ m<b>ā</b> ātainākum biquwwatiw ważkurụ mā fīhi la'allakum tattaqụn
2|64|ṡumma tawallaitum mim ba'di żālika falau lā faḍlullāhi 'alaikum wa raḥmatuhụ lakuntum minal-khāsirīn
2|65|wa laqad 'alimtumullażīna'tadau mingkum fis-sabti fa qulnā lahum kụnụ qiradatan khāsi`īn
2|66|fa ja'alnāhā nakālal limā baina yadaihā wa mā khalfahā wa mau'iẓatal lil-muttaqīn
2|67|wa iż qāla mụsā liqaumih<b>ī</b> innallāha ya`murukum an tażbaḥụ baqarah, qāl<b>ū</b> a tattakhiżunā huzuwā, qāla a'ụżu billāhi an akụna minal-jāhilīn
2|68|qālud'u lanā rabbaka yubayyil lanā mā hiy, qāla innahụ yaqụlu innahā baqaratul lā fāriḍuw wa lā bikr, 'awānum baina żālik, faf'alụ mā tu`marụn
2|69|qālud'u lanā rabbaka yubayyil lanā mā launuhā, qāla innahụ yaqụlu innahā baqaratun ṣafr<b>ā</b>`u fāqi'ul launuhā tasurrun-nāẓirīn
2|70|qālud'u lanā rabbaka yubayyil lanā mā hiya innal-baqara tasyābaha 'alainā, wa inn<b>ā</b> in sy<b>ā</b>`allāhu lamuhtadụn
2|71|qāla innahụ yaqụlu innahā baqaratul lā żalụlun tuṡīrul-arḍa wa lā tasqil-ḥarṡ, musallamatul lā syiyata fīhā, qālul-āna ji`ta bil-ḥaqqi fa żabaḥụhā wa mā kādụ yaf'alụn
2|72|wa iż qataltum nafsan faddāra'tum fīhā, wallāhu mukhrijum mā kuntum taktumụn
2|73|fa qulnaḍribụhu biba'ḍihā, każālika yuḥyillāhul-mautā wa yurīkum āyātihī la'allakum ta'qilụn
2|74|ṡumma qasat qulụbukum mim ba'di żālika fa hiya kal-ḥijārati au asyaddu qaswah, wa inna minal-ḥijārati lamā yatafajjaru min-hul-an-hār, wa inna min-hā lamā yasysyaqqaqu fa yakhruju min-hul-m<b>ā</b>`, wa inna min-hā lamā yahbiṭu min khasy-yatillāh, wa mallāhu bigāfilin 'ammā ta'malụn
2|75|a fa taṭma'ụna ay yu`minụ lakum wa qad kāna farīqum min-hum yasma'ụna kalāmallāhi ṡumma yuḥarrifụnahụ mim ba'di mā 'aqalụhu wa hum ya'lamụn
2|76|wa iżā laqullażīna āmanụ qāl<b>ū</b> āmannā, wa iżā khalā ba'ḍuhum ilā ba'ḍing qāl<b>ū</b> a tuḥaddiṡụnahum bimā fataḥallāhu 'alaikum liyuḥ<b>ā</b>jjụkum bihī 'inda rabbikum, a fa lā ta'qilụn
2|77|a wa lā ya'lamụna annallāha ya'lamu mā yusirrụna wa mā yu'linụn
2|78|wa min-hum ummiyyụna lā ya'lamụnal-kitāba ill<b>ā</b> amāniyya wa in hum illā yaẓunnụn
2|79|fa wailul lillażīna yaktubụnal-kitāba bi`aidīhim ṡumma yaqụlụna hāżā min 'indillāhi liyasytarụ bihī ṡamanang qalīlā, fa wailul lahum mimmā katabat aidīhim wa wailul lahum mimmā yaksibụn
2|80|wa qālụ lan tamassanan-nāru ill<b>ā</b> ayyāmam ma'dụdah, qul attakhażtum 'indallāhi 'ahdan fa lay yukhlifallāhu 'ahdah<b>ū</b> am taqụlụna 'alallāhi mā lā ta'lamụn
2|81|balā mang kasaba sayyi`ataw wa `aḥāṭat bihī khaṭ<b>ī</b>`atuhụ fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
2|82|wallażīna āmanụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāti ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābul-jannah, hum fīhā khālidụn
2|83|wa iż akhażnā mīṡāqa ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla lā ta'budụna illallāha wa bil-wālidaini iḥsānaw wa żil-qurbā wal-yatāmā wal-masākīni wa qụlụ lin-nāsi ḥusnaw wa aqīmuṣ-ṣalāta wa ātuz-zakāh, ṡumma tawallaitum illā qalīlam mingkum wa antum mu'riḍụn
2|84|wa iż akhażnā mīṡāqakum lā tasfikụna dim<b>ā</b>`akum wa lā tukhrijụna anfusakum min diyārikum ṡumma aqrartum wa antum tasy-hadụn
2|85|ṡumma antum h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`i taqtulụna anfusakum wa tukhrijụna farīqam mingkum min diyārihim taẓāharụna 'alaihim bil-iṡmi wal-'udwān, wa iy ya`tụkum usārā tufādụhum wa huwa muḥarramun 'alaikum ikhrājuhum, a fa tu`minụna biba'ḍil-kitābi wa takfurụna biba'ḍ, fa mā jaz<b>ā</b>`u may yaf'alu żālika mingkum illā khizyun fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā, wa yaumal-qiyāmati yuraddụna il<b>ā</b> asyaddil-'ażāb, wa mallāhu bigāfilin 'ammā ta'malụn
2|86|ul<b>ā</b>`ikallażīnasytarawul-ḥayātad-dun-yā bil-ākhirati fa lā yukhaffafu 'an-humul-'ażābu wa lā hum yunṣarụn
2|87|wa laqad ātainā mụsal-kitāba wa qaffainā mim ba'dihī bir-rusuli wa ātainā 'īsabna maryamal-bayyināti wa ayyadnāhu birụḥil-qudus, a fa kullamā j<b>ā</b>`akum rasụlum bimā lā tahw<b>ā</b> anfusukumustakbartum, fa farīqang każżabtum wa farīqan taqtulụn
2|88|wa qālụ qulụbunā gulf, bal la'anahumullāhu bikufrihim fa qalīlam mā yu`minụn
2|89|wa lammā j<b>ā</b>`ahum kitābum min 'indillāhi muṣaddiqul limā ma'ahum wa kānụ ming qablu yastaftiḥụna 'alallażīna kafarụ, fa lammā j<b>ā</b>`ahum mā 'arafụ kafarụ bihī fa la'natullāhi 'alal-kāfirīn
2|90|bi`samasytarau bih<b>ī</b> anfusahum ay yakfurụ bim<b>ā</b> anzalallāhu bagyan ay yunazzilallāhu min faḍlihī 'alā may yasy<b>ā</b>`u min 'ibādih, fa b<b>ā</b>`ụ bigaḍabin 'alā gaḍab, wa lil-kāfirīna 'ażābum muhīn
2|91|wa iżā qīla lahum āminụ bim<b>ā</b> anzalallāhu qālụ nu`minu bim<b>ā</b> unzila 'alainā wa yakfurụna bimā war<b>ā</b>`ahụ wa huwal-ḥaqqu muṣaddiqal limā ma'ahum, qul fa lima taqtulụna ambiy<b>ā</b>`allāhi ming qablu ing kuntum mu`minīn
2|92|wa laqad j<b>ā</b>`akum mụsā bil-bayyināti ṡummattakhażtumul-'ijla mim ba'dihī wa antum ẓālimụn
2|93|wa iż akhażnā mīṡāqakum wa rafa'nā fauqakumuṭ-ṭụr, khużụ m<b>ā</b> ātainākum biquwwatiw wasma'ụ, qālụ sami'nā wa 'aṣainā wa usyribụ fī qulụbihimul-'ijla bikufrihim, qul bi`samā ya`murukum bih<b>ī</b> īmānukum ing kuntum mu`minīn
2|94|qul ing kānat lakumud-dārul-ākhiratu 'indallāhi khāliṣatam min dụnin-nāsi fa tamannawul-mauta ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
2|95|wa lay yatamannauhu abadam bimā qaddamat aidīhim, wallāhu 'alīmum biẓ-ẓālimīn
2|96|wa latajidannahum aḥraṣan-nāsi 'alā ḥayāh, wa minallażīna asyrakụ yawaddu aḥaduhum lau yu'ammaru alfa sanah, wa mā huwa bimuzaḥziḥihī minal-'ażābi ay yu'ammar, wallāhu baṣīrum bimā ya'malụn
2|97|qul mang kāna 'aduwwal lijibrīla fa innahụ nazzalahụ 'alā qalbika bi`iżnillāhi muṣaddiqal limā baina yadaihi wa hudaw wa busyrā lil-mu`minīn
2|98|mang kāna 'aduwwal lillāhi wa mal<b>ā</b>`ikatihī wa rusulihī wa jibrīla wa mīkāla fa innallāha 'aduwwul lil-kāfirīn
2|99|wa laqad anzaln<b>ā</b> ilaika āyātim bayyināt, wa mā yakfuru bih<b>ā</b> illal-fāsiqụn
2|100|a wa kullamā 'āhadụ 'ahdan nabażahụ farīqum min-hum, bal akṡaruhum lā yu`minụn
2|101|wa lammā j<b>ā</b>`ahum rasụlum min 'indillāhi muṣaddiqul limā ma'ahum nabaża farīqum minallażīna ụtul-kitāba kitāballāhi war<b>ā</b>`a ẓuhụrihim ka`annahum lā ya'lamụn
2|102|wattaba'ụ mā tatlusy-syayāṭīnu 'alā mulki sulaimān, wa mā kafara sulaimānu wa lākinnasy-syayāṭīna kafarụ yu'allimụnan-nāsas-siḥra wa m<b>ā</b> unzila 'alal-malakaini bibābila hārụta wa mārụt, wa mā yu'allimāni min aḥadin ḥattā yaqụl<b>ā</b> innamā naḥnu fitnatun fa lā takfur, fa yata'allamụna min-humā mā yufarriqụna bihī bainal-mar'i wa zaujih, wa mā hum biḍ<b>ā</b>rrīna bihī min aḥadin illā bi`iżnillāh, wa yata'allamụna mā yaḍurruhum wa lā yanfa'uhum, wa laqad 'alimụ lamanisytarāhu mā lahụ fil-ākhirati min khalāq, wa labi`sa mā syarau bih<b>ī</b> anfusahum, lau kānụ ya'lamụn
2|103|walau annahum āmanụ wattaqau lamaṡụbatum min 'indillāhi khaīr, lau kānụ ya'lamụn
2|104|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ lā taqụlụ rā'inā wa qụlunẓurnā wasma'ụ wa lil-kāfirīna 'ażābun alīm
2|105|mā yawaddullażīna kafarụ min ahlil-kitābi wa lal-musyrikīna ay yunazzala 'alaikum min khairim mir rabbikum, wallāhu yakhtaṣṣu biraḥmatihī may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu żul-faḍlil-'aẓīm
2|106|mā nansakh min āyatin au nunsihā na`ti bikhairim min-h<b>ā</b> au miṡlihā, a lam ta'lam annallāha 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
2|107|a lam ta'lam annallāha lahụ mulkus-samāwāti wal-arḍ, wa mā lakum min dụnillāhi miw waliyyiw wa lā naṣīr
2|108|am turīdụna an tas`alụ rasụlakum kamā su`ila mụsā ming qabl, wa may yatabaddalil-kufra bil-īmāni fa qad ḍalla saw<b>ā</b>`as-sabīl
2|109|wadda kaṡīrum min ahlil-kitābi lau yaruddụnakum mim ba'di īmānikum kuffārā, ḥasadam min 'indi anfusihim mim ba'di mā tabayyana lahumul-ḥaqq, fa'fụ waṣfaḥụ ḥattā ya`tiyallāhu bi`amrih, innallāha 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
2|110|wa aqīmuṣ-ṣalāta wa ātuz-zakāh, wa mā tuqaddimụ li`anfusikum min khairin tajidụhu 'indallāh, innallāha bimā ta'malụna baṣīr
2|111|wa qālụ lay yadkhulal-jannata illā mang kāna hụdan au naṣārā, tilka amāniyyuhum, qul hātụ bur-hānakum ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
2|112|balā man aslama waj-hahụ lillāhi wa huwa muḥsinun fa lah<b>ū</b> ajruhụ 'inda rabbihī wa lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
2|113|wa qālatil-yahụdu laisatin-naṣārā 'alā syai`iw wa qālatin-naṣārā laisatil-yahụdu 'alā syai`iw wa hum yatlụnal-kitāb, każālika qālallażīna lā ya'lamụna miṡla qaulihim, fallāhu yaḥkumu bainahum yaumal-qiyāmati fīmā kānụ fīhi yakhtalifụn
2|114|wa man aẓlamu mim mam mana'a masājidallāhi ay yużkara fīhasmuhụ wa sa'ā fī kharābihā, ul<b>ā</b>`ika mā kāna lahum ay yadkhulụh<b>ā</b> illā kh<b>ā</b>`ifīn, lahum fid-dun-yā khizyuw wa lahum fil-ākhirati 'ażābun 'aẓīm
2|115|wa lillāhil-masyriqu wal-magribu fa ainamā tuwallụ fa ṡamma waj-hullāh, innallāha wāsi'un 'alīm
2|116|wa qāluttakhażallāhu waladan sub-ḥānah, bal lahụ mā fis-samāwāti wal-arḍ, kullul lahụ qānitụn
2|117|badī'us-samāwāti wal-arḍ, wa iżā qaḍ<b>ā</b> amran fa innamā yaqụlu lahụ kun fa yakụn
2|118|wa qālallażīna lā ya'lamụna lau lā yukallimunallāhu au ta`tīn<b>ā</b> āyah, każālika qālallażīna ming qablihim miṡla qaulihim, tasyābahat qulụbuhum, qad bayyannal-āyāti liqaumiy yụqinụn
2|119|inn<b>ā</b> arsalnāka bil-ḥaqqi basyīraw wa nażīraw wa lā tus`alu 'an aṣ-ḥābil-jaḥīm
2|120|wa lan tarḍā 'angkal-yahụdu wa lan-naṣārā ḥattā tattabi'a millatahum, qul inna hudallāhi huwal-hudā, wa la`inittaba'ta ahw<b>ā</b>`ahum ba'dallażī j<b>ā</b>`aka minal-'ilmi mā laka minallāhi miw waliyyiw wa lā naṣīr
2|121|allażīna ātaināhumul-kitāba yatlụnahụ ḥaqqa tilāwatih, ul<b>ā</b>`ika yu`minụna bih, wa may yakfur bihī fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-khāsirụn
2|122|yā ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īlażkurụ ni'matiyallat<b>ī</b> an'amtu 'alaikum wa annī faḍḍaltukum 'alal-'ālamīn
2|123|wattaqụ yaumal lā tajzī nafsun 'an nafsin syai`aw wa lā yuqbalu min-hā 'adluw wa lā tanfa'uhā syafā'atuw wa lā hum yunṣarụn
2|124|wa iżibtal<b>ā</b> ibrāhīma rabbuhụ bikalimātin fa atammahunn, qāla innī jā'iluka lin-nāsi imāmā, qāla wa min żurriyyatī, qāla lā yanālu 'ahdiẓ-ẓālimīn
2|125|wa iż ja'alnal-baita maṡābatal lin-nāsi wa amnā, wattakhiżụ mim maqāmi ibrāhīma muṣallā, wa 'ahidn<b>ā</b> il<b>ā</b> ibrāhīma wa ismā'īla an ṭahhirā baitiya liṭ-ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifīna wal-'ākifīna war-rukka'is-sujụd
2|126|wa iż qāla ibrāhīmu rabbij'al hāżā baladan āminaw warzuq ahlahụ minaṡ-ṡamarāti man āmana min-hum billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhir, qāla wa mang kafara fa umatti'uhụ qalīlan ṡumma aḍṭarruh<b>ū</b> ilā 'ażābin-nār, wa bi`sal-maṣīr
2|127|wa iż yarfa'u ibrāhīmul-qawā'ida minal-baiti wa ismā'īl, rabbanā taqabbal minnā, innaka antas-samī'ul-'alīm
2|128|rabbanā waj'alnā muslimaini laka wa min żurriyyatin<b>ā</b> ummatam muslimatal laka wa arinā manāsikanā wa tub 'alainā, innaka antat-tawwābur-raḥīm
2|129|rabbanā wab'aṡ fīhim rasụlam min-hum yatlụ 'alaihim āyātika wa yu'allimuhumul-kitāba wal-ḥikmata wa yuzakkīhim, innaka antal-'azīzul-ḥakīm
2|130|wa may yargabu 'am millati ibrāhīma illā man safiha nafsah, wa laqadiṣṭafaināhu fid-dun-yā, wa innahụ fil-ākhirati laminaṣ-ṣāliḥīn
2|131|iż qāla lahụ rabbuh<b>ū</b> aslim qāla aslamtu lirabbil-'ālamīn
2|132|wa waṣṣā bih<b>ā</b> ibrāhīmu banīhi wa ya'qụb, yā baniyya innallāhaṣṭafā lakumud-dīna fa lā tamụtunna illā wa antum muslimụn
2|133|am kuntum syuhad<b>ā</b>`a iż ḥaḍara ya'qụbal-mautu iż qāla libanīhi mā ta'budụna mim ba'dī, qālụ na'budu ilāhaka wa ilāha āb<b>ā</b>`ika ibrāhīma wa ismā'īla wa is-ḥāqa ilāhaw wāḥidā, wa naḥnu lahụ muslimụn
2|134|tilka ummatung qad khalat, lahā mā kasabat wa lakum mā kasabtum, wa lā tus`alụna 'ammā kānụ ya'malụn
2|135|wa qālụ kụnụ hụdan au naṣārā tahtadụ, qul bal millata ibrāhīma ḥanīfā, wa mā kāna minal-musyrikīn
2|136|qụl<b>ū</b> āmannā billāhi wa m<b>ā</b> unzila ilainā wa m<b>ā</b> unzila il<b>ā</b> ibrāhīma wa ismā'īla wa is-ḥāqa wa ya'qụba wal-asbāṭi wa m<b>ā</b> ụtiya mụsā wa 'īsā wa m<b>ā</b> ụtiyan-nabiyyụna mir rabbihim, lā nufarriqu baina aḥadim min-hum wa naḥnu lahụ muslimụn
2|137|fa in āmanụ bimiṡli m<b>ā</b> āmantum bihī fa qadihtadau, wa in tawallau fa innamā hum fī syiqāq, fa sayakfīkahumullāh, wa huwas-samī'ul-'alīm
2|138|ṣibgatallāh, wa man aḥsanu minallāhi ṣibgataw wa naḥnu lahụ 'ābidụn
2|139|qul a tuḥ<b>ā</b>jjụnanā fillāhi wa huwa rabbunā wa rabbukum, wa lan<b>ā</b> a'mālunā wa lakum a'mālukum, wa naḥnu lahụ mukhliṣụn
2|140|am taqụlụna inna ibrāhīma wa ismā'īla wa is-ḥāqa wa ya'qụba wal-asbāṭa kānụ hụdan au naṣārā, qul a antum a'lamu amillāh, wa man aẓlamu mim mang katama syahādatan 'indahụ minallāh, wa mallāhu bigāfilin 'ammā ta'malụn
2|141|tilka ummatung qad khalat, lahā mā kasabat wa lakum mā kasabtum, wa lā tus`alụna 'ammā kānụ ya'malụn
2|142|sayaqụlus-sufah<b>ā</b>`u minan-nāsi mā wallāhum 'ang qiblatihimullatī kānụ 'alaihā, qul lillāhil-masyriqu wal-magrib, yahdī may yasy<b>ā</b>`u ilā ṣirāṭim mustaqīm
2|143|wa każālika ja'alnākum ummataw wasaṭal litakụnụ syuhad<b>ā</b>`a 'alan-nāsi wa yakụnar-rasụlu 'alaikum syahīdā, wa mā ja'alnal-qiblatallatī kunta 'alaih<b>ā</b> illā lina'lama may yattabi'ur-rasụla mim may yangqalibu 'alā 'aqibaīh, wa ing kānat lakabīratan illā 'alallażīna hadallāh, wa mā kānallāhu liyuḍī'a īmānakum, innallāha bin-nāsi lara`ụfur raḥīm
2|144|qad narā taqalluba waj-hika fis-sam<b>ā</b>`, fa lanuwalliyannaka qiblatan tarḍāhā fa walli waj-haka syaṭral-masjidil-ḥarām, wa ḥaiṡu mā kuntum fa wallụ wujụhakum syaṭrah, wa innallażīna ụtul-kitāba laya'lamụna annahul-ḥaqqu mir rabbihim, wa mallāhu bigāfilin 'ammā ya'malụn
2|145|wa la`in ataitallażīna ụtul-kitāba bikulli āyatim mā tabi'ụ qiblatak, wa m<b>ā</b> anta bitābi'ing qiblatahum, wa mā ba'ḍuhum bitābi'ing qiblata ba'ḍ, wa la`inittaba'ta ahw<b>ā</b>`ahum mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`aka minal-'ilmi innaka iżal laminaẓ-ẓālimīn
2|146|allażīna ātaināhumul-kitāba ya'rifụnahụ kamā ya'rifụna abn<b>ā</b>`ahum, wa inna farīqam min-hum layaktumụnal-ḥaqqa wa hum ya'lamụn
2|147|al-ḥaqqu mir rabbika fa lā takụnanna minal-mumtarīn
2|148|wa likulliw wij-hatun huwa muwallīhā fastabiqul-khairāt, aina mā takụnụ ya`ti bikumullāhu jamī'ā, innallāha 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
2|149|wa min ḥaiṡu kharajta fa walli waj-haka syaṭral-masjidil-ḥarām, wa innahụ lal-ḥaqqu mir rabbik, wa mallāhu bigāfilin 'ammā ta'malụn
2|150|wa min ḥaiṡu kharajta fa walli waj-haka syaṭral-masjidil-ḥarām, wa ḥaiṡu mā kuntum fa wallụ wujụhakum syaṭrahụ li`allā yakụna lin-nāsi 'alaikum ḥujjatun illallażīna ẓalamụ min-hum fa lā takhsyauhum wakhsyaunī wa li`utimma ni'matī 'alaikum wa la'allakum tahtadụn
2|151|kam<b>ā</b> arsalnā fīkum rasụlam mingkum yatlụ 'alaikum āyātinā wa yuzakkīkum wa yu'allimukumul-kitāba wal-ḥikmata wa yu'allimukum mā lam takụnụ ta'lamụn
2|152|fażkurụn<b>ī</b> ażkurkum wasykurụ lī wa lā takfurụn
2|153|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanusta'īnụ biṣ-ṣabri waṣ-ṣalāh, innallāha ma'aṣ-ṣābirīn
2|154|wa lā taqụlụ limay yuqtalu fī sabīlillāhi amwāt, bal aḥy<b>ā</b>`uw wa lākil lā tasy'urụn
2|155|wa lanabluwannakum bisyai`im minal-khaufi wal-jụ'i wa naqṣim minal-amwāli wal-anfusi waṡ-ṡamarāt, wa basysyiriṣ-ṣābirīn
2|156|allażīna iż<b>ā</b> aṣābat-hum muṣībah, qāl<b>ū</b> innā lillāhi wa inn<b>ā</b> ilaihi rāji'ụn
2|157|ul<b>ā</b>`ika 'alaihim ṣalawātum mir rabbihim wa raḥmah, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-muhtadụn
2|158|innaṣ-ṣafā wal-marwata min sya'<b>ā</b>`irillāh, fa man ḥajjal-baita awi'tamara fa lā junāḥa 'alaihi ay yaṭṭawwafa bihimā, wa man taṭawwa'a khairan fa innallāha syākirun 'alīm
2|159|innallażīna yaktumụna m<b>ā</b> anzalnā minal-bayyināti wal-hudā mim ba'di mā bayyannāhu lin-nāsi fil-kitābi ul<b>ā</b>`ika yal'anuhumullāhu wa yal'anuhumul-lā'inụn
2|160|illallażīna tābụ wa aṣlaḥụ wa bayyanụ fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika atụbu 'alaihim, wa anat-tawwābur-raḥīm
2|161|innallażīna kafarụ wa mātụ wa hum kuffārun ul<b>ā</b>`ika 'alaihim la'natullāhi wal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati wan-nāsi ajma'īn
2|162|khālidīna fīhā, lā yukhaffafu 'an-humul-'ażābu wa lā hum yunẓarụn
2|163|wa ilāhukum ilāhuw wāḥid, l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huwar-raḥmānur-raḥīm
2|164|inna fī khalqis-samāwāti wal-arḍi wakhtilāfil-laili wan-nahāri wal-fulkillatī tajrī fil-baḥri bimā yanfa'un-nāsa wa m<b>ā</b> anzalallāhu minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i mim m<b>ā</b>`in fa aḥyā bihil-arḍa ba'da mautihā wa baṡṡa fīhā ming kulli d<b>ā</b>bbatiw wa taṣrīfir-riyāḥi was-saḥābil-musakhkhari bainas-sam<b>ā</b>`i wal-arḍi la`āyātil liqaumiy ya'qilụn
2|165|wa minan-nāsi may yattakhiżu min dụnillāhi andāday yuḥibbụnahum kaḥubbillāh, wallażīna āman<b>ū</b> asyaddu ḥubbal lillāhi walau yarallażīna ẓalam<b>ū</b> iż yaraunal-'ażāba annal-quwwata lillāhi jamī'aw wa annallāha syadīdul-'ażāb
2|166|iż tabarra`allażīnattubi'ụ minallażīnattaba'ụ wa ra`awul-'ażāba wa taqaṭṭa'at bihimul-asbāb
2|167|wa qālallażīnattaba'ụ lau anna lanā karratan fa natabarra`a min-hum, kamā tabarra`ụ minnā, każālika yurīhimullāhu a'mālahum ḥasarātin 'alaihim, wa mā hum bikhārijīna minan-nār
2|168|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsu kulụ mimmā fil-arḍi ḥalālan ṭayyibaw wa lā tattabi'ụ khuṭuwātisy-syaiṭān, innahụ lakum 'aduwwum mubīn
2|169|innamā ya`murukum bis-s<b>ū</b>`i wal-faḥsy<b>ā</b>`i wa an taqụlụ 'alallāhi mā lā ta'lamụn
2|170|wa iżā qīla lahumuttabi'ụ m<b>ā</b> anzalallāhu qālụ bal nattabi'u m<b>ā</b> alfainā 'alaihi āb<b>ā</b>`anā, a walau kāna āb<b>ā</b>`uhum lā ya'qilụna syai`aw wa lā yahtadụn
2|171|wa maṡalullażīna kafarụ kamaṡalillażī yan'iqu bimā lā yasma'u illā du'<b>ā</b>`aw wa nid<b>ā</b>`ā, ṣummum bukmun 'umyun fa hum lā ya'qilụn
2|172|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ kulụ min ṭayyibāti mā razaqnākum wasykurụ lillāhi ing kuntum iyyāhu ta'budụn
2|173|innamā ḥarrama 'alaikumul-maitata wad-dama wa laḥmal-khinzīri wa m<b>ā</b> uhilla bihī ligairillāh, fa maniḍṭurra gaira bāgiw wa lā 'ādin fa l<b>ā</b> iṡma 'alaīh, innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
2|174|innallażīna yaktumụna m<b>ā</b> anzalallāhu minal-kitābi wa yasytarụna bihī ṡamanang qalīlan ul<b>ā</b>`ika mā ya`kulụna fī buṭụnihim illan-nāra wa lā yukallimuhumullāhu yaumal-qiyāmati wa lā yuzakkīhim, wa lahum 'ażābun alīm
2|175|ul<b>ā</b>`ikallażīnasytarawuḍ-ḍalālata bil-hudā wal-'ażāba bil-magfirah, fa m<b>ā</b> aṣbarahum 'alan-nār
2|176|żālika bi`annallāha nazzalal-kitāba bil-ḥaqq, wa innallażīnakhtalafụ fil-kitābi lafī syiqāqim ba'īd
2|177|laisal-birra an tuwallụ wujụhakum qibalal-masyriqi wal-magribi wa lākinnal-birra man āmana billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri wal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati wal-kitābi wan-nabiyyīn, wa ātal-māla 'alā ḥubbihī żawil-qurbā wal-yatāmā wal-masākīna wabnas-sabīli was-s<b>ā</b>`ilīna wa fir-riqāb, wa aqāmaṣ-ṣalāta wa ātaz-zakāh, wal-mụfụna bi'ahdihim iżā 'āhadụ, waṣ-ṣābirīna fil-ba`s<b>ā</b>`i waḍ-ḍarr<b>ā</b>`i wa ḥīnal-ba`s, ul<b>ā</b>`ikallażīna ṣadaqụ, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-muttaqụn
2|178|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ kutiba 'alaikumul-qiṣāṣu fil-qatlā, al-ḥurru bil-ḥurri wal-'abdu bil-'abdi wal-unṡā bil-unṡā, fa man 'ufiya lahụ min akhīhi syai`un fattibā'um bil-ma'rụfi wa ad<b>ā</b>`un ilaihi bi`iḥsān, żālika takhfīfum mir rabbikum wa raḥmah, fa mani'tadā ba'da żālika fa lahụ 'ażābun alīm
2|179|wa lakum fil-qiṣāṣi ḥayātuy y<b>ā</b> ulil-albābi la'allakum tattaqụn
2|180|kutiba 'alaikum iżā ḥaḍara aḥadakumul-mautu in taraka khairanil-waṣiyyatu lil-wālidaini wal-aqrabīna bil-ma'rụf, ḥaqqan 'alal-muttaqīn
2|181|fa mam baddalahụ ba'da mā sami'ahụ fa innam<b>ā</b> iṡmuhụ 'alallażīna yubaddilụnah, innallāha samī'un 'alīm
2|182|fa man khāfa mim mụṣin janafan au iṡman fa aṣlaḥa bainahum fa l<b>ā</b> iṡma 'alaīh, innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
2|183|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ kutiba 'alaikumuṣ-ṣiyāmu kamā kutiba 'alallażīna ming qablikum la'allakum tattaqụn
2|184|ayyāmam ma'dụdāt, fa mang kāna mingkum marīḍan au 'alā safarin fa 'iddatum min ayyāmin ukhar, wa 'alallażīna yuṭīqụnahụ fidyatun ṭa'āmu miskīn, fa man taṭawwa'a khairan fa huwa khairul lah, wa an taṣụmụ khairul lakum ing kuntum ta'lamụn
2|185|syahru ramaḍānallaż<b>ī</b> unzila fīhil-qur`ānu hudal lin-nāsi wa bayyinātim minal-hudā wal-furqān, fa man syahida mingkumusy-syahra falyaṣum-h, wa mang kāna marīḍan au 'alā safarin fa 'iddatum min ayyāmin ukhar, yurīdullāhu bikumul-yusra wa lā yurīdu bikumul-'usra wa litukmilul-'iddata wa litukabbirullāha 'alā mā hadākum wa la'allakum tasykurụn
2|186|wa iżā sa`alaka 'ibādī 'annī fa innī qarīb, ujību da'watad-dā'i iżā da'āni falyastajībụ lī walyu`minụ bī la'allahum yarsyudụn
2|187|uḥilla lakum lailataṣ-ṣiyāmir-rafaṡu ilā nis<b>ā</b>`ikum, hunna libāsul lakum wa antum libāsul lahunn, 'alimallāhu annakum kuntum takhtānụna anfusakum fa tāba 'alaikum wa 'afā 'angkum, fal-āna bāsyirụhunna wabtagụ mā kataballāhu lakum, wa kulụ wasyrabụ ḥattā yatabayyana lakumul-khaiṭul-abyaḍu minal-khaiṭil-aswadi minal-fajr, ṡumma atimmuṣ-ṣiyāma ilal-laīl, wa lā tubāsyirụhunna wa antum 'ākifụna fil-masājid, tilka ḥudụdullāhi fa lā taqrabụhā, każālika yubayyinullāhu āyātihī lin-nāsi la'allahum yattaqụn
2|188|wa lā ta`kul<b>ū</b> amwālakum bainakum bil-bāṭili wa tudlụ bih<b>ā</b> ilal-ḥukkāmi lita`kulụ farīqam min amwālin-nāsi bil-iṡmi wa antum ta'lamụn
2|189|yas`alụnaka 'anil-ahillah, qul hiya mawāqītu lin-nāsi wal-ḥajj, wa laisal-birru bi`an ta`tul-buyụta min ẓuhụrihā wa lākinnal-birra manittaqā, wa`tul-buyụta min abwābihā wattaqullāha la'allakum tufliḥụn
2|190|wa qātilụ fī sabīlillāhillażīna yuqātilụnakum wa lā ta'tadụ, innallāha lā yuḥibbul-mu'tadīn
2|191|waqtulụhum ḥaiṡu ṡaqiftumụhum wa akhrijụhum min ḥaiṡu akhrajụkum wal-fitnatu asyaddu minal-qatl, wa lā tuqātilụhum 'indal-masjidil-ḥarāmi ḥattā yuqātilụkum fīh, fa ing qātalụkum faqtulụhum, każālika jaz<b>ā</b>`ul-kāfirīn
2|192|fa inintahau fa innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
2|193|wa qātilụhum ḥattā lā takụna fitnatuw wa yakụnad-dīnu lillāh, fa inintahau fa lā 'udwāna illā 'alaẓ-ẓālimīn
2|194|asy-syahrul-ḥarāmu bisy-syahril-ḥarāmi wal-ḥurumātu qiṣāṣ, fa mani'tadā 'alaikum fa'tadụ 'alaihi bimiṡli ma'tadā 'alaikum wattaqullāha wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha ma'al-muttaqīn
2|195|wa anfiqụ fī sabīlillāhi wa lā tulqụ bi`aidīkum ilat-tahlukati wa aḥsinụ, innallāha yuḥibbul-muḥsinīn
2|196|wa atimmul-ḥajja wal-'umrata lillāh, fa in uḥṣirtum fa mastaisara minal-hady, wa lā taḥliqụ ru`ụsakum ḥattā yablugal-hadyu maḥillah, fa mang kāna mingkum marīḍan au bih<b>ī</b> ażam mir ra`sihī fa fidyatum min ṣiyāmin au ṣadaqatin au nusuk, fa iż<b>ā</b> amintum, fa man tamatta'a bil-'umrati ilal-ḥajji fa mastaisara minal-hady, fa mal lam yajid fa ṣiyāmu ṡalāṡati ayyāmin fil-ḥajji wa sab'atin iżā raja'tum, tilka 'asyaratung kāmilah, żālika limal lam yakun ahluhụ ḥāḍiril-masjidil-ḥarām, wattaqullāha wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha syadīdul-'iqāb
2|197|al-ḥajju asy-hurum ma'lụmāt, fa man faraḍa fīhinnal-ḥajja fa lā rafaṡa wa lā fusụqa wa lā jidāla fil-ḥajj, wa mā taf'alụ min khairiy ya'lam-hullāh, wa tazawwadụ fa inna khairaz-zādit-taqwā wattaqụni y<b>ā</b> ulil-albāb
2|198|laisa 'alaikum junāḥun an tabtagụ faḍlam mir rabbikum, fa iż<b>ā</b> afaḍtum min 'arafātin fażkurullāha 'indal-masy'aril-ḥarāmi ważkurụhu kamā hadākum, wa ing kuntum ming qablihī laminaḍ-ḍ<b>ā</b>llīn
2|199|ṡumma afīḍụ min ḥaiṡu afāḍan-nāsu wastagfirullāh, innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
2|200|fa iżā qaḍaitum manasikakum fażkurullāha każikrikum āb<b>ā</b>`akum au asyadda żikrā, fa minan-nāsi may yaqụlu rabban<b>ā</b> ātinā fid-dun-yā wa mā lahụ fil-ākhirati min khalāq
2|201|wa min-hum may yaqụlu rabban<b>ā</b> ātinā fid-dun-yā ḥasanataw wa fil-ākhirati ḥasanataw wa qinā 'ażāban-nār
2|202|ul<b>ā</b>`ika lahum naṣībum mimmā kasabụ, wallāhu sarī'ul-ḥisāb
2|203|ważkurullāha f<b>ī</b> ayyāmim ma'dụdāt, fa man ta'ajjala fī yaumaini fa l<b>ā</b> iṡma 'alaīh, wa man ta`akhkhara fa l<b>ā</b> iṡma 'alaihi limanittaqā, wattaqullāha wa'lam<b>ū</b> annakum ilaihi tuḥsyarụn
2|204|wa minan-nāsi may yu'jibuka qauluhụ fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā wa yusy-hidullāha 'alā mā fī qalbihī wa huwa aladdul-khiṣām
2|205|wa iżā tawallā sa'ā fil-arḍi liyufsida fīhā wa yuhlikal-ḥarṡa wan-nasl, wallāhu lā yuḥibbul-fasād
2|206|wa iżā qīla lahuttaqillāha akhażat-hul-'izzatu bil-iṡmi fa ḥasbuhụ jahannam, wa labi`sal-mihād
2|207|wa minan-nāsi may yasyrī nafsahubtig<b>ā</b>`a marḍātillāh, wallāhu ra`ụfum bil-'ibād
2|208|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanudkhulụ fis-silmi k<b>ā</b>ffataw wa lā tattabi'ụ khuṭuwātisy-syaiṭān, innahụ lakum 'aduwwum mubīn
2|209|fa in zalaltum mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`atkumul-bayyinātu fa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha 'azīzun ḥakīm
2|210|hal yanẓurụna ill<b>ā</b> ay ya`tiyahumullāhu fī ẓulalim minal-gamāmi wal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikatu wa quḍiyal-amr, wa ilallāhi turja'ul-umụr
2|211|sal ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla kam ātaināhum min āyatim bayyinah, wa may yubaddil ni'matallāhi mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`at-hu fa innallāha syadīdul-'iqāb
2|212|zuyyina lillażīna kafarul-ḥayātud-dun-yā wa yaskharụna minallażīna āmanụ, wallażīnattaqau fauqahum yaumal-qiyāmah, wallāhu yarzuqu may yasy<b>ā</b>`u bigairi ḥisāb
2|213|kānan-nāsu ummataw wāḥidah, fa ba'aṡallāhun-nabiyyīna mubasysyirīna wa munżirīna wa anzala ma'ahumul-kitāba bil-ḥaqqi liyaḥkuma bainan-nāsi fīmakhtalafụ fīh, wa makhtalafa fīhi illallażīna ụtụhu mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`at-humul-bayyinātu bagyam bainahum, fa hadallāhullażīna āmanụ limakhtalafụ fīhi minal-ḥaqqi bi`iżnih, wallāhu yahdī may yasy<b>ā</b>`u ilā ṣirāṭim mustaqīm
2|214|am ḥasibtum an tadkhulul-jannata wa lammā ya`tikum maṡalullażīna khalau ming qablikum, massat-humul-ba`s<b>ā</b>`u waḍ-ḍarr<b>ā</b>`u wa zulzilụ ḥattā yaqụlar-rasụlu wallażīna āmanụ ma'ahụ matā naṣrullāh, al<b>ā</b> inna naṣrallāhi qarīb
2|215|yas`alụnaka māżā yunfiqụn, qul m<b>ā</b> anfaqtum ming kairin fa lil-wālidaini wal-aqrabīna wal-yatāmā wal-masākīni wabnis-sabīl, wa mā taf'alụ min khairin fa innallāha bihī 'alīm
2|216|kutiba 'alaikumul-qitālu wa huwa kur-hul lakum, wa 'as<b>ā</b> an takrahụ syai`aw wa huwa khairul lakum, wa 'as<b>ā</b> an tuḥibbụ syai`aw wa huwa syarrul lakum, wallāhu ya'lamu wa antum lā ta'lamụn
2|217|yas`alụnaka 'anisy-syahril-ḥarāmi qitālin fīh, qul qitālun fīhi kabīr, wa ṣaddun 'an sabīlillāhi wa kufrum bihī wal-masjidil-ḥarāmi wa ikhrāju ahlihī min-hu akbaru 'indallāh, wal-fitnatu akbaru minal-qatl, wa lā yazālụna yuqātilụnakum ḥattā yaruddụkum 'an dīnikum inistaṭā'ụ, wa may yartadid mingkum 'an dīnihī fa yamut wa huwa kāfirun fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika ḥabiṭat a'māluhum fid-dun-yā wal-ākhirah, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
2|218|innallażīna āmanụ wallażīna hājarụ wa jāhadụ fī sabīlillāhi ul<b>ā</b>`ika yarjụna raḥmatallāh, wallāhu gafụrur raḥīm
2|219|yas`alụnaka 'anil-khamri wal-maisir, qul fīhim<b>ā</b> iṡmung kabīruw wa manafi'u lin-nāsi wa iṡmuhum<b>ā</b> akbaru min-naf'ihimā, wa yas`alụnaka māżā yunfiqụn, qulil-'afw, każālika yubayyinullāhu lakumul-āyāti la'allakum tatafakkarụn
2|220|fid-dun-yā wal-ākhirah, wa yas`alụnaka 'anil-yatāmā, qul iṣlāḥul lahum khaīr, wa in tukhāliṭụhum fa ikhwānukum, wallāhu ya'lamul-mufsida minal-muṣliḥ, walau sy<b>ā</b>`allāhu la`a'natakum, innallāha 'azīzun ḥakīm
2|221|wa lā tangkiḥul-musyrikāti ḥattā yu`minn, wa la`amatum mu`minatun khairum mim musyrikatiw walau a'jabatkum, wa lā tungkiḥul-musyrikīna ḥattā yu`minụ, wa la'abdum mu`minun khairum mim musyrikiw walau a'jabakum, ul<b>ā</b>`ika yad'ụna ilan-nāri wallāhu yad'<b>ū</b> ilal-jannati wal-magfirati bi`iżnih, wa yubayyinu āyātihī lin-nāsi la'allahum yatażakkarụn
2|222|wa yas`alụnaka 'anil-maḥīḍ, qul huwa ażan fa'tazilun-nis<b>ā</b>`a fil-maḥīḍi wa lā taqrabụhunna ḥattā yaṭ-hurn, fa iżā taṭahharna fa`tụhunna min ḥaiṡu amarakumullāh, innallāha yuḥibbut-tawwābīna wa yuḥibbul-mutaṭahhirīn
2|223|nis<b>ā</b>`ukum ḥarṡul lakum fa`tụ ḥarṡakum annā syi`tum wa qaddimụ li`anfusikum, wattaqullāha wa'lam<b>ū</b> annakum mulāqụh, wa basysyiril-mu`minīn
2|224|wa lā taj'alullāha 'urḍatal li`aimānikum an tabarrụ wa tattaqụ wa tuṣliḥụ bainan-nās, wallāhu samī'un 'alīm
2|225|lā yu`ākhiżukumullāhu bil-lagwi f<b>ī</b> aimānikum wa lākiy yu`ākhiżukum bimā kasabat qulụbukum, wallāhu gafụrun ḥalīm
2|226|lillażīna yu`lụna min nis<b>ā</b>`ihim tarabbuṣu arba'ati asy-hur, fa in f<b>ā</b>`ụ fa innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
2|227|wa in 'azamuṭ-ṭalāqa fa innallāha samī'un 'alīm
2|228|wal-muṭallaqātu yatarabbaṣna bi`anfusihinna ṡalāṡata qur<b>ū</b>`, wa lā yaḥillu lahunna ay yaktumna mā khalaqallāhu f<b>ī</b> ar-ḥāmihinna ing kunna yu`minna billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhir, wa bu'ụlatuhunna aḥaqqu biraddihinna fī żālika in arād<b>ū</b> iṣlāḥā, wa lahunna miṡlullażī 'alaihinna bil-ma'rụfi wa lir-rijāli 'alaihinna darajah, wallāhu 'azīzun ḥakīm
2|229|aṭ-ṭalāqu marratāni fa imsākum bima'rụfin au tasrīḥum bi`iḥsān, wa lā yaḥillu lakum an ta`khużụ mimm<b>ā</b> ātaitumụhunna syai`an ill<b>ā</b> ay yakhāf<b>ā</b> allā yuqīmā ḥudụdallāh, fa in khiftum allā yuqīmā ḥudụdallāhi fa lā junāḥa 'alaihimā fīmaftadat bih, tilka ḥudụdullāhi fa lā ta'tadụhā, wa may yata'adda ḥudụdallāhi fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humuẓ-ẓālimụn
2|230|fa in ṭallaqahā fa lā taḥillu lahụ mim ba'du ḥattā tangkiḥa zaujan gairah, fa in ṭallaqahā fa lā junāḥa 'alaihim<b>ā</b> ay yatarāja'<b>ā</b> in ẓann<b>ā</b> ay yuqīmā ḥudụdallāh, wa tilka ḥudụdullāhi yubayyinuhā liqaumiy ya'lamụn
2|231|wa iżā ṭallaqtumun-nis<b>ā</b>`a fa balagna ajalahunna fa amsikụhunna bima'rụfin au sarriḥụhunna bima'rụf, wa lā tumsikụhunna ḍirāral lita'tadụ, wa may yaf'al żālika fa qad ẓalama nafsah, wa lā tattakhiż<b>ū</b> āyātillāhi huzuwaw ważkurụ ni'matallāhi 'alaikum wa m<b>ā</b> anzala 'alaikum minal-kitābi wal-ḥikmati ya'iẓukum bih, wattaqullāha wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha bikulli syai`in 'alīm
2|232|wa iżā ṭallaqtumun-nis<b>ā</b>`a fa balagna ajalahunna fa lā ta'ḍulụhunna ay yangkiḥna azwājahunna iżā tarāḍau bainahum bil-ma'rụf, żālika yụ'aẓu bihī mang kāna mingkum yu`minu billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhir, żālikum azkā lakum wa aṭ-har, wallāhu ya'lamu wa antum lā ta'lamụn
2|233|wal-wālidātu yurḍi'na aulādahunna ḥaulaini kāmilaini liman arāda ay yutimmar-raḍā'ah, wa 'alal-maulụdi lahụ rizquhunna wa kiswatuhunna bil-ma'rụf, lā tukallafu nafsun illā wus'ahā, lā tuḍ<b>ā</b>rra wālidatum biwaladihā wa lā maulụdul lahụ biwaladihī wa 'alal-wāriṡi miṡlu żālik, fa in arādā fiṣālan 'an tarāḍim min-humā wa tasyāwurin fa lā junāḥa 'alaihimā, wa in arattum an tastarḍi'<b>ū</b> aulādakum fa lā junāḥa 'alaikum iżā sallamtum m<b>ā</b> ātaitum bil-ma'rụf, wattaqullāha wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha bimā ta'malụna baṣīr
2|234|wallażīna yutawaffauna mingkum wa yażarụna azwājay yatarabbaṣna bi`anfusihinna arba'ata asy-huriw wa 'asyrā, fa iżā balagna ajalahunna fa lā junāḥa 'alaikum fīmā fa'alna f<b>ī</b> anfusihinna bil-ma'rụf, wallāhu bimā ta'malụna khabīr
2|235|wa lā junāḥa 'alaikum fīmā 'arraḍtum bihī min khiṭbatin-nis<b>ā</b>`i au aknantum f<b>ī</b> anfusikum, 'alimallāhu annakum satażkurụnahunna wa lākil lā tuwā'idụhunna sirran ill<b>ā</b> an taqụlụ qaulam ma'rụfā, wa lā ta'zimụ 'uqdatan-nikāḥi ḥattā yablugal-kitābu ajalah, wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha ya'lamu mā f<b>ī</b> anfusikum faḥżarụh, wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha gafụrun ḥalīm
2|236|lā junāḥa 'alaikum in ṭallaqtumun-nis<b>ā</b>`a mā lam tamassụhunna au tafriḍụ lahunna farīḍataw wa matti'ụhunna 'alal-mụsi'i qadaruhụ wa 'alal-muqtiri qadaruh, matā'am bil-ma'rụf, ḥaqqan 'alal-muḥsinīn
2|237|wa in ṭallaqtumụhunna ming qabli an tamassụhunna wa qad faraḍtum lahunna farīḍatan fa niṣfu mā faraḍtum ill<b>ā</b> ay ya'fụna au ya'fuwallażī biyadihī 'uqdatun-nikāḥ, wa an ta'f<b>ū</b> aqrabu lit-taqwā, wa lā tansawul-faḍla bainakum, innallāha bimā ta'malụna baṣīr
2|238|ḥāfiẓụ 'alaṣ-ṣalawāti waṣ-ṣalātil-wusṭā wa qụmụ lillāhi qānitīn
2|239|fa in khiftum fa rijālan au rukbānā, fa iż<b>ā</b> amintum fażkurullāha kamā 'allamakum mā lam takụnụ ta'lamụn
2|240|wallażīna yutawaffauna mingkum wa yażarụna azwājaw waṣiyyatal li`azwājihim matā'an ilal-ḥauli gaira ikhrāj, fa in kharajna fa lā junāḥa 'alaikum fī mā fa'alna f<b>ī</b> anfusihinna mim ma'rụf, wallāhu 'azīzun ḥakīm
2|241|wa lil-muṭallaqāti matā'um bil-ma'rụf, ḥaqqan 'alal-muttaqīn
2|242|każālika yubayyinullāhu lakum āyātihī la'allakum ta'qilụn
2|243|a lam tara ilallażīna kharajụ min diyārihim wa hum ulụfun ḥażaral-mauti fa qāla lahumullāhu mụtụ, ṡumma aḥyāhum, innallāha lażụ faḍlin 'alan-nāsi wa lākinna akṡaran-nāsi lā yasykurụn
2|244|wa qātilụ fī sabīlillāhi wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha samī'un 'alīm
2|245|man żallażī yuqriḍullāha qarḍan ḥasanan fa yuḍā'ifahụ lah<b>ū</b> aḍ'āfang kaṡīrah, wallāhu yaqbiḍu wa yabṣuṭu wa ilaihi turja'ụn
2|246|a lam tara ilal-mala`i mim ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla mim ba'di mụsā, iż qālụ linabiyyil lahumub'aṡ lanā malikan-nuqātil fī sabīlillāh, qāla hal 'asaitum ing kutiba 'alaikumul-qitālu allā tuqātilụ, qālụ wa mā lan<b>ā</b> allā nuqātila fī sabīlillāhi wa qad ukhrijnā min diyārinā wa abn<b>ā</b>`inā, fa lammā kutiba 'alaihimul-qitālu tawallau illā qalīlam min-hum, wallāhu 'alīmum biẓ-ẓālimīn
2|247|wa qāla lahum nabiyyuhum innallāha qad ba'aṡa lakum ṭālụta malikā, qāl<b>ū</b> annā yakụnu lahul-mulku 'alainā wa naḥnu aḥaqqu bil-mulki min-hu wa lam yu`ta sa'atam minal-māl, qāla innallāhaṣṭafāhu 'alaikum wa zādahụ basṭatan fil 'ilmi wal-jism, wallāhu yu`tī mulkahụ may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu wāsi'un 'alīm
2|248|wa qāla lahum nabiyyuhum inna āyata mulkih<b>ī</b> ay ya`tiyakumut-tābụtu fīhi sakīnatum mir rabbikum wa baqiyyatum mimmā taraka ālu mụsā wa ālu hārụna taḥmiluhul-mal<b>ā</b>`ikah, inna fī żālika la`āyatal lakum ing kuntum mu`minīn
2|249|fa lammā faṣala ṭālụtu bil-junụdi qāla innallāha mubtalīkum binahar, fa man syariba min-hu fa laisa minnī, wa mal lam yaṭ'am-hu fa innahụ minn<b>ī</b> illā manigtarafa gurfatam biyadih, fa syaribụ min-hu illā qalīlam min-hum, fa lammā jāwazahụ huwa wallażīna āmanụ ma'ahụ qālụ lā ṭāqata lanal-yauma bijālụta wa junụdih, qālallażīna yaẓunnụna annahum mulāqullāhi kam min fi`ating qalīlatin galabat fi`atang kaṡīratam bi`iżnillāh, wallāhu ma'aṣ-ṣābirīn
2|250|wa lammā barazụ lijālụta wa junụdihī qālụ rabban<b>ā</b> afrig 'alainā ṣabraw wa ṡabbit aqdāmanā wanṣurnā 'alal-qaumil-kāfirīn
2|251|fa hazamụhum bi`iżnillāh, wa qatala dāwụdu jālụta wa ātāhullāhul-mulka wal-ḥikmata wa 'allamahụ mimmā yasy<b>ā</b>`, walau lā daf'ullāhin-nāsa ba'ḍahum biba'ḍil lafasadatil-arḍu wa lākinnallāha żụ faḍlin 'alal-'ālamīn
2|252|tilka āyātullāhi natlụhā 'alaika bil-ḥaqq, wa innaka laminal-mursalīn
2|253|tilkar-rusulu faḍḍalnā ba'ḍahum 'alā ba'ḍ, min-hum mang kallamallāhu wa rafa'a ba'ḍahum darajāt, wa ātainā 'īsabna maryamal-bayyināti wa ayyadnāhu birụḥil-qudus, walau sy<b>ā</b>`allāhu maqtatalallażīna mim ba'dihim mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`at-humul-bayyinātu wa lākinikhtalafụ fa min-hum man āmana wa min-hum mang kafar, walau sy<b>ā</b>`allāhu maqtatalụ, wa lākinnallāha yaf'alu mā yurīd
2|254|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> anfiqụ mimmā razaqnākum ming qabli ay ya`tiya yaumul lā bai'un fīhi wa lā khullatuw wa lā syafā'ah, wal-kāfirụna humuẓ-ẓālimụn
2|255|allāhu l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huw, al-ḥayyul-qayyụm, lā ta`khużuhụ sinatuw wa lā na`ụm, lahụ mā fis-samāwāti wa mā fil-arḍ, man żallażī yasyfa'u 'indah<b>ū</b> illā bi`iżnih, ya'lamu mā baina aidīhim wa mā khalfahum, wa lā yuḥīṭụna bisyai`im min 'ilmih<b>ī</b> illā bimā sy<b>ā</b>`, wasi'a kursiyyuhus-samāwāti wal-arḍ, wa lā ya`ụduhụ ḥifẓuhumā, wa huwal-'aliyyul-'aẓīm
2|256|l<b>ā</b> ikrāha fid-dīn, qat tabayyanar-rusydu minal-gayy, fa may yakfur biṭ-ṭāgụti wa yu`mim billāhi fa qadistamsaka bil-'urwatil-wuṡqā lanfiṣāma lahā, wallāhu samī'un 'alīm
2|257|allāhu waliyyullażīna āmanụ yukhrijuhum minaẓ-ẓulumāti ilan-nụr, wallażīna kafar<b>ū</b> auliy<b>ā</b>`uhumuṭ-ṭāgụtu yukhrijụnahum minan-nụri ilaẓ-ẓulumāt, ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
2|258|a lam tara ilallażī ḥ<b>ā</b>jja ibrāhīma fī rabbih<b>ī</b> an ātāhullāhul-mulk, iż qāla ibrāhīmu rabbiyallażī yuḥyī wa yumītu qāla ana uḥyī wa umīt, qāla ibrāhīmu fa innallāha ya`tī bisy-syamsi minal-masyriqi fa`ti bihā minal-magribi fa buhitallażī kafar, wallāhu lā yahdil-qaumaẓ-ẓālimīn
2|259|au kallażī marra 'alā qaryatiw wa hiya khāwiyatun 'alā 'urụsyihā, qāla annā yuḥyī hāżihillāhu ba'da mautihā, fa amātahullāhu mi`ata 'āmin ṡumma ba'aṡah, qāla kam labiṡt, qāla labiṡtu yauman au ba'ḍa yaụm, qāla bal labiṡta mi`ata 'āmin fanẓur ilā ṭa'āmika wa syarābika lam yatasannah, wanẓur ilā ḥimārik, wa linaj'alaka āyatal lin-nāsi wanẓur ilal-'iẓāmi kaifa nunsyizuhā ṡumma naksụhā laḥmā, fa lammā tabayyana lahụ qāla a'lamu annallāha 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
2|260|wa iż qāla ibrāhīmu rabbi arinī kaifa tuḥyil-mautā, qāla a wa lam tu`min, qāla balā wa lākil liyaṭma`inna qalbī, qāla fakhuż arba'atam minaṭ-ṭairi fa ṣur-hunna ilaika ṡummaj'al 'alā kulli jabalim min-hunna juz`an ṡummad'uhunna ya`tīnaka sa'yā, wa'lam annallāha 'azīzun ḥakīm
2|261|maṡalullażīna yunfiqụna amwālahum fī sabīlillāhi kamaṡali ḥabbatin ambatat sab'a sanābila fī kulli sumbulatim mi`atu ḥabbah, wallāhu yuḍā'ifu limay yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu wāsi'un 'alīm
2|262|allażīna yunfiqụna amwālahum fī sabīlillāhi ṡumma lā yutbi'ụna m<b>ā</b> anfaqụ mannaw wa l<b>ā</b> ażal lahum ajruhum 'inda rabbihim, wa lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
2|263|qaulum ma'rụfuw wa magfiratun khairum min ṣadaqatiy yatba'uh<b>ā</b> ażā, wallāhu ganiyyun ḥalīm
2|264|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ lā tubṭilụ ṣadaqātikum bil-manni wal-ażā kallażī yunfiqu mālahụ ri`<b>ā</b>`an-nāsi wa lā yu`minu billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhir, fa maṡaluhụ kamaṡali ṣafwānin 'alaihi turābun fa aṣābahụ wābilun fa tarakahụ ṣaldā, lā yaqdirụna 'alā syai`im mimmā kasabụ, wallāhu lā yahdil-qaumal-kāfirīn
2|265|wa maṡalullażīna yunfiqụna amwālahumubtig<b>ā</b>`a marḍātillāhi wa taṡbītam min anfusihim kamaṡali jannatim birabwatin aṣābahā wābilun fa ātat ukulahā ḍi'faīn, fa il lam yuṣib-hā wābilun fa ṭall, wallāhu bimā ta'malụna baṣīr
2|266|a yawaddu aḥadukum an takụna lahụ jannatum min nakhīliw wa a'nābin tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hāru lahụ fīhā ming kulliṡ-ṡamarāti wa aṣābahul-kibaru wa lahụ żurriyyatun ḍu'af<b>ā</b>`, fa aṣābah<b>ā</b> i'ṣārun fīhi nārun faḥtaraqat, każālika yubayyinullāhu lakumul-āyāti la'allakum tatafakkarụn
2|267|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> anfiqụ min ṭayyibāti mā kasabtum wa mimm<b>ā</b> akhrajnā lakum minal-arḍ, wa lā tayammamul-khabīṡa min-hu tunfiqụna wa lastum bi`ākhiżīhi ill<b>ā</b> an tugmiḍụ fīh, wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha ganiyyun ḥamīd
2|268|asy-syaiṭānu ya'idukumul-faqra wa ya`murukum bil-faḥsy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu ya'idukum magfiratam min-hu wa faḍlā, wallāhu wāsi'un 'alīm
2|269|yu`til-ḥikmata may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wa may yu`tal-ḥikmata fa qad ụtiya khairang kaṡīrā, wa mā yażżakkaru ill<b>ā</b> ulul-albāb
2|270|wa m<b>ā</b> anfaqtum min nafaqatin au nażartum min nażrin fa innallāha ya'lamuh, wa mā liẓ-ẓālimīna min anṣār
2|271|in tubduṣ-ṣadaqāti fa ni'immā hiy, wa in tukhfụhā wa tu`tụhal-fuqar<b>ā</b>`a fa huwa khairul lakum, wa yukaffiru 'angkum min sayyi`ātikum, wallāhu bimā ta'malụna khabīr
2|272|laisa 'alaika hudāhum wa lākinnallāha yahdī may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wa mā tunfiqụ min khairin fa li`anfusikum, wa mā tunfiqụna illabtig<b>ā</b>`a waj-hillāh, wa mā tunfiqụ min khairiy yuwaffa ilaikum wa antum lā tuẓlamụn
2|273|lil-fuqar<b>ā</b>`illażīna uḥṣirụ fī sabīlillāhi lā yastaṭī'ụna ḍarban fil-arḍi yaḥsabuhumul-jāhilu agniy<b>ā</b>`a minat-ta'affuf, ta'rifuhum bisīmāhum, lā yas`alụnan-nāsa il-ḥāfā, wa mā tunfiqụ min khairin fa innallāha bihī 'alīm
2|274|allażīna yunfiqụna amwālahum bil-laili wan-nahāri sirraw wa 'alāniyatan fa lahum ajruhum 'inda rabbihim, wa lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
2|275|allażīna ya`kulụnar-ribā lā yaqụmụna illā kamā yaqụmullażī yatakhabbaṭuhusy-syaiṭānu minal-mass, żālika bi`annahum qāl<b>ū</b> innamal-bai'u miṡlur-ribā, wa aḥallallāhul-bai'a wa ḥarramar-ribā, fa man j<b>ā</b>`ahụ mau'iẓatum mir rabbihī fantahā fa lahụ mā salaf, wa amruh<b>ū</b> ilallāh, wa man 'āda fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
2|276|yam-ḥaqullāhur-ribā wa yurbiṣ-ṣadaqāt, wallāhu lā yuḥibbu kulla kaffārin aṡīm
2|277|innallażīna āmanụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāti wa aqāmuṣ-ṣalāta wa ātawuz-zakāta lahum ajruhum 'inda rabbihim, wa lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
2|278|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanuttaqullāha wa żarụ mā baqiya minar-rib<b>ā</b> ing kuntum mu`minīn
2|279|fa il lam taf'alụ fa`żanụ biḥarbim minallāhi wa rasụlih, wa in tubtum fa lakum ru`ụsu amwālikum, lā taẓlimụna wa lā tuẓlamụn
2|280|wa ing kāna żụ 'usratin fa naẓiratun ilā maisarah, wa an taṣaddaqụ khairul lakum ing kuntum ta'lamụn
2|281|wattaqụ yauman turja'ụna fīhi ilallāh, ṡumma tuwaffā kullu nafsim mā kasabat wa hum lā yuẓlamụn
2|282|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> iżā tadāyantum bidainin il<b>ā</b> ajalim musamman faktubụh, walyaktub bainakum kātibum bil-'adli wa lā ya`ba kātibun ay yaktuba kamā 'allamahullāhu falyaktub, walyumlilillażī 'alaihil-ḥaqqu walyattaqillāha rabbahụ wa lā yabkhas min-hu syai`ā, fa ing kānallażī 'alaihil-ḥaqqu safīhan au ḍa'īfan au lā yastaṭī'u ay yumilla huwa falyumlil waliyyuhụ bil-'adl, wastasy-hidụ syahīdaini mir rijālikum, fa il lam yakụnā rajulaini fa rajuluw wamra`atāni mim man tarḍauna minasy-syuhad<b>ā</b>`i an taḍilla iḥdāhumā fa tużakkira iḥdāhumal-ukhrā, wa lā ya`basy-syuhad<b>ā</b>`u iżā mā du'ụ, wa lā tas`am<b>ū</b> an taktubụhu ṣagīran au kabīran il<b>ā</b> ajalih, żālikum aqsaṭu 'indallāhi wa aqwamu lisy-syahādati wa adn<b>ā</b> allā tartāb<b>ū</b> ill<b>ā</b> an takụna tijāratan ḥāḍiratan tudīrụnahā bainakum fa laisa 'alaikum junāḥun allā taktubụhā, wa asy-hid<b>ū</b> iżā tabāya'tum wa lā yuḍ<b>ā</b>rra kātibuw wa lā syahīd, wa in taf'alụ fa innahụ fusụqum bikum, wattaqullāh, wa yu'allimukumullāh, wallāhu bikulli syai`in 'alīm
2|283|wa ing kuntum 'alā safariw wa lam tajidụ kātiban fa rihānum maqbụḍah, fa in amina ba'ḍukum ba'ḍan falyu`addillażi`tumina amānatahụ walyattaqillāha rabbah, wa lā taktumusy-syahādah, wa may yaktum-hā fa innah<b>ū</b> āṡimung qalbuh, wallāhu bimā ta'malụna 'alīm
2|284|lillāhi mā fis-samāwāti wa mā fil-arḍ, wa in tubdụ mā f<b>ī</b> anfusikum au tukhfụhu yuḥāsibkum bihillāh, fa yagfiru limay yasy<b>ā</b>`u wa yu'ażżibu may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
2|285|āmanar-rasụlu bim<b>ā</b> unzila ilaihi mir rabbihī wal-mu`minụn, kullun āmana billāhi wa mal<b>ā</b>`ikatihī wa kutubihī wa rusulih, lā nufarriqu baina aḥadim mir rusulih, wa qālụ sami'nā wa aṭa'nā gufrānaka rabbanā wa ilaikal-maṣīr
2|286|lā yukallifullāhu nafsan illā wus'ahā, lahā mā kasabat wa 'alaihā maktasabat, rabbanā lā tu`ākhiżn<b>ā</b> in nasīn<b>ā</b> au akhṭa`nā, rabbanā wa lā taḥmil 'alain<b>ā</b> iṣrang kamā ḥamaltahụ 'alallażīna ming qablinā, rabbanā wa lā tuḥammilnā mā lā ṭāqata lanā bih, wa'fu 'annā, wagfir lanā, war-ḥamnā, anta maulānā fanṣurnā 'alal-qaumil-kāfirīn
3|1|alif l<b>ā</b>m m<b>ī</b>m
3|2|allāhu l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huwal-ḥayyul-qayyụm
3|3|nazzala 'alaikal-kitāba bil-ḥaqqi muṣaddiqal limā baina yadaihi wa anzalat-taurāta wal-injīl
3|4|ming qablu hudal lin-nāsi wa anzalal-furqān, innallażīna kafarụ bi`āyātillāhi lahum 'ażābun syadīd, wallāhu 'azīzun żuntiqām
3|5|innallāha lā yakhfā 'alaihi syai`un fil-arḍi wa lā fis-sam<b>ā</b>`
3|6|huwallażī yuṣawwirukum fil-ar-ḥāmi kaifa yasy<b>ā</b>`, l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huwal-'azīzul-ḥakīm
3|7|huwallaż<b>ī</b> anzala 'alaikal-kitāba min-hu āyātum muḥkamātun hunna ummul-kitābi wa ukharu mutasyābihāt, fa ammallażīna fī qulụbihim zaigun fayattabi'ụna mā tasyābaha min-hubtig<b>ā</b>`al-fitnati wabtig<b>ā</b>`a ta`wīlih, wa mā ya'lamu ta`wīlah<b>ū</b> illallāh, war-rāsikhụna fil-'ilmi yaqụlụna āmannā bihī kullum min 'indi rabbinā, wa mā yażżakkaru ill<b>ā</b> ulul-albāb
3|8|rabbanā lā tuzig qulụbanā ba'da iż hadaitanā wa hab lanā mil ladungka raḥmah, innaka antal-wahhāb
3|9|rabban<b>ā</b> innaka jāmi'un-nāsi liyaumil lā raiba fīh, innallāha lā yukhliful-mī'ād
3|10|innallażīna kafarụ lan tugniya 'an-hum amwāluhum wa l<b>ā</b> aulāduhum minallāhi syai`ā, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika hum waqụdun-nār
3|11|kada`bi āli fir'auna wallażīna ming qablihim, każżabụ bi`āyātinā, fa akhażahumullāhu biżunụbihim, wallāhu syadīdul-'iqāb
3|12|qul lillażīna kafarụ satuglabụna wa tuḥsyarụna ilā jahannam, wa bi`sal-mihād
3|13|qad kāna lakum āyatun fī fi`atainiltaqatā, fi`atun tuqātilu fī sabīlillāhi wa ukhrā kāfiratuy yaraunahum miṡlaihim ra`yal-'aīn, wallāhu yu`ayyidu binaṣrihī may yasy<b>ā</b>`, inna fī żālika la'ibratal li`ulil-abṣār
3|14|zuyyina lin-nāsi ḥubbusy-syahawāti minan-nis<b>ā</b>`i wal-banīna wal-qanaṭīril-muqanṭarati minaż-żahabi wal-fiḍḍati wal-khailil-musawwamati wal-an'āmi wal-ḥarṡ, żālika matā'ul-ḥayātid-dun-yā, wallāhu 'indahụ ḥusnul-ma`āb
3|15|qul a unabbi`ukum bikhairim min żālikum, lillażīnattaqau 'inda rabbihim jannātun tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hāru khālidīna fīhā wa azwājum muṭahharatuw wa riḍwānum minallāh, wallāhu baṣīrum bil-'ibād
3|16|allażīna yaqụlụna rabban<b>ā</b> innan<b>ā</b> āmannā fagfir lanā żunụbanā wa qinā 'ażāban-nār

3|18|syahidallāhu annahụ l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huwa wal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikatu wa ulul-'ilmi q<b>ā</b>`imam bil-qisṭ, l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huwal-'azīzul-ḥakīm
3|19|innad-dīna 'indallāhil-islām, wa makhtalafallażīna ụtul-kitāba illā mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`ahumul-'ilmu bagyam bainahum, wa may yakfur bi`āyātillāhi fa innallāha sarī'ul-ḥisāb
3|20|fa in ḥ<b>ā</b>jjụka fa qul aslamtu waj-hiya lillāhi wa manittaba'an, wa qul lillażīna ụtul-kitāba wal-ummiyyīna a aslamtum, fa in aslamụ fa qadihtadau, wa in tawallau fa innamā 'alaikal-balāg, wallāhu baṣīrum bil-'ibād
3|21|innallażīna yakfurụna bi`āyātillāhi wa yaqtulụnan-nabiyyīna bigairi ḥaqqiw wa yaqtulụnallażīna ya`murụna bil-qisṭi minan-nāsi fa basysyir-hum bi'ażābin alīm
3|22|ul<b>ā</b>`ikallażīna ḥabiṭat a'māluhum fid-dun-yā wal-ākhirati wa mā lahum min nāṣirīn
3|23|a lam tara ilallażīna ụtụ naṣībam minal-kitābi yud'auna ilā kitābillāhi liyaḥkuma bainahum ṡumma yatawallā farīqum min-hum wa hum mu'riḍụn
3|24|żālika bi`annahum qālụ lan tamassanan-nāru ill<b>ā</b> ayyāmam ma'dụdātiw wa garrahum fī dīnihim mā kānụ yaftarụn
3|25|fa kaifa iżā jama'nāhum liyaumil lā raiba fīh, wa wuffiyat kullu nafsim mā kasabat wa hum lā yuẓlamụn
3|26|qulillāhumma mālikal-mulki tu`til-mulka man tasy<b>ā</b>`u wa tanzi'ul-mulka mim man tasy<b>ā</b>`u wa tu'izzu man tasy<b>ā</b>`u wa tużillu man tasy<b>ā</b>`, biyadikal-khaīr, innaka 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
3|27|tụlijul-laila fin-nahāri wa tụlijun-nahāra fil-laili wa tukhrijul-ḥayya minal-mayyiti wa tukhrijul-mayyita minal-ḥayyi wa tarzuqu man tasy<b>ā</b>`u bigairi ḥisāb
3|28|lā yattakhiżil-mu`minụnal-kāfirīna auliy<b>ā</b>`a min dụnil-mu`minīn, wa may yaf'al żālika fa laisa minallāhi fī syai`in ill<b>ā</b> an tattaqụ min-hum tuqāh, wa yuḥażżirukumullāhu nafsah, wa ilallāhil-maṣīr
3|29|qul in tukhfụ mā fī ṣudụrikum au tubdụhu ya'lam-hullāh, wa ya'lamu mā fis-samāwāti wa mā fil-arḍ, wallāhu 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
3|30|yauma tajidu kullu nafsim mā 'amilat min khairim muḥḍaraw wa mā 'amilat min s<b>ū</b>`, tawaddu lau anna bainahā wa bainah<b>ū</b> amadam ba'īdā, wa yuḥażżirukumullāhu nafsah, wallāhu ra`ụfum bil-'ibād
3|31|qul ing kuntum tuḥibbụnallāha fattabi'ụnī yuḥbibkumullāhu wa yagfir lakum żunụbakum, wallāhu gafụrur raḥīm
3|32|qul aṭī'ullāha war-rasụl, fa in tawallau fa innallāha lā yuḥibbul-kāfirīn
3|33|innallāhaṣṭaf<b>ā</b> ādama wa nụḥaw wa āla ibrāhīma wa āla 'imrāna 'alal-'ālamīn
3|34|żurriyyatam ba'ḍuhā mim ba'ḍ, wallāhu samī'un 'alīm
3|35|iż qālatimra`atu 'imrāna rabbi innī nażartu laka mā fī baṭnī muḥarraran fa taqabbal minnī, innaka antas-samī'ul-'alīm
3|36|fa lammā waḍa'at-hā qālat rabbi innī waḍa'tuh<b>ā</b> unṡā, wallāhu a'lamu bimā waḍa'at, wa laisaż-żakaru kal-unṡā, wa innī sammaituhā maryama wa inn<b>ī</b> u'īżuhā bika wa żurriyyatahā minasy-syaiṭānir-rajīm
3|37|fa taqabbalahā rabbuhā biqabụlin ḥasaniw wa ambatahā nabātan ḥasanaw wa kaffalahā zakariyyā, kullamā dakhala 'alaihā zakariyyal-miḥrāba wajada 'indahā rizqā, qāla yā maryamu annā laki hāżā, qālat huwa min 'indillāh, innallāha yarzuqu may yasy<b>ā</b>`u bigairi ḥisāb
3|38|hunālika da'ā zakariyyā rabbah, qāla rabbi hab lī mil ladungka żurriyyatan ṭayyibah, innaka samī'ud-du'<b>ā</b>`
3|39|fa nādat-hul-mal<b>ā</b>`ikatu wa huwa q<b>ā</b>`imuy yuṣallī fil-miḥrābi annallāha yubasysyiruka biyaḥyā muṣaddiqam bikalimatim minallāhi wa sayyidaw wa ḥaṣụraw wa nabiyyam minaṣ-ṣāliḥīn
3|40|qāla rabbi annā yakụnu lī gulāmuw wa qad balaganiyal-kibaru wamra`atī 'āqir, qāla każālikallāhu yaf'alu mā yasy<b>ā</b>`
3|41|qāla rabbij'al l<b>ī</b> āyah, qāla āyatuka allā tukalliman-nāsa ṡalāṡata ayyāmin illā ramzā, ważkur rabbaka kaṡīraw wa sabbiḥ bil-'asyiyyi wal-ibkār
3|42|wa iż qālatil-mal<b>ā</b>`ikatu yā maryamu innallāhaṣṭafāki wa ṭahharaki waṣṭafāki 'alā nis<b>ā</b>`il-'ālamīn
3|43|yā maryamuqnutī lirabbiki wasjudī warka'ī ma'ar-rāki'īn
3|44|żālika min amb<b>ā</b>`il-gaibi nụḥīhi ilaīk, wa mā kunta ladaihim iż yulqụna aqlāmahum ayyuhum yakfulu maryama wa mā kunta ladaihim iż yakhtaṣimụn
3|45|iż qālatil-mal<b>ā</b>`ikatu yā maryamu innallāha yubasysyiruki bikalimatim min-husmuhul-masīḥu 'īsabnu maryama wajīhan fid-dun-yā wal-ākhirati wa minal-muqarrabīn
3|46|wa yukallimun-nāsa fil-mahdi wa kahlaw wa minaṣ-ṣāliḥīn
3|47|qālat rabbi annā yakụnu lī waladuw wa lam yamsasnī basyar, qāla każālikillāhu yakhluqu mā yasy<b>ā</b>`, iżā qaḍ<b>ā</b> amran fa innamā yaqụlu lahụ kun fa yakụn
3|48|wa yu'allimuhul-kitāba wal-ḥikmata wat-taurāta wal-injīl
3|49|wa rasụlan ilā ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla annī qad ji`tukum bi`āyatim mir rabbikum ann<b>ī</b> akhluqu lakum minaṭ-ṭīni kahai`atiṭ-ṭairi fa anfukhu fīhi fa yakụnu ṭairam bi`iżnillāh, wa ubri`ul-akmaha wal-abraṣa wa uḥyil-mautā bi`iżnillāh, wa unabbi`ukum bimā ta`kulụna wa mā taddakhirụna fī buyụtikum, inna fī żālika la`āyatal lakum ing kuntum mu`minīn
3|50|wa muṣaddiqal limā baina yadayya minat-taurāti wa li`uḥilla lakum ba'ḍallażī ḥurrima 'alaikum wa ji`tukum bi`āyatim mir rabbikum, fattaqullāha wa aṭī'ụn
3|51|innallāha rabbī wa rabbukum fa'budụh, hāżā ṣirāṭum mustaqīm
3|52|fa lamm<b>ā</b> aḥassa 'īsā min-humul-kufra qāla man anṣār<b>ī</b> ilallāh, qālal-ḥawāriyyụna naḥnu anṣārullāh, āmannā billāh, wasy-had bi`annā muslimụn
3|53|rabban<b>ā</b> āmannā bim<b>ā</b> anzalta wattaba'nar-rasụla faktubnā ma'asy-syāhidīn
3|54|wa makarụ wa makarallāh, wallāhu khairul-mākirīn
3|55|iż qālallāhu yā 'īs<b>ā</b> innī mutawaffīka wa rāfi'uka ilayya wa muṭahhiruka minallażīna kafarụ wa jā'ilullażīnattaba'ụka fauqallażīna kafar<b>ū</b> ilā yaumil-qiyāmah, ṡumma ilayya marji'ukum fa aḥkumu bainakum fīmā kuntum fīhi takhtalifụn
3|56|fa ammallażīna kafarụ fa u'ażżibuhum 'ażāban syadīdan fid-dun-yā wal-ākhirati wa mā lahum min nāṣirīn
3|57|wa ammallażīna āmanụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāti fa yuwaffīhim ujụrahum, wallāhu lā yuḥibbuẓ-ẓālimīn
3|58|żālika natlụhu 'alaika minal-āyāti waż-żikril-ḥakīm
3|59|inna maṡala 'īsā 'indallāhi kamaṡali ādam, khalaqahụ min turābin ṡumma qāla lahụ kun fa yakụn
3|60|al-ḥaqqu mir rabbika fa lā takum minal-mumtarīn
3|61|fa man ḥ<b>ā</b>jjaka fīhi mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`aka minal-'ilmi fa qul ta'ālau nad'u abn<b>ā</b>`anā wa abn<b>ā</b>`akum wa nis<b>ā</b>`anā wa nis<b>ā</b>`akum wa anfusanā wa anfusakum, ṡumma nabtahil fa naj'al la'natallāhi 'alal-kāżibīn
3|62|inna hāżā lahuwal-qaṣaṣul-ḥaqq, wa mā min ilāhin illallāh, wa innallāha lahuwal-'azīzul-ḥakīm
3|63|fa in tawallau fa innallāha 'alīmum bil-mufsidīn
3|64|qul y<b>ā</b> ahlal-kitābi ta'ālau ilā kalimatin saw<b>ā</b>`im bainanā wa bainakum allā na'buda illallāha wa lā nusyrika bihī syai`aw wa lā yattakhiża ba'ḍunā ba'ḍan arbābam min dụnillāh, fa in tawallau fa qụlusy-hadụ bi`annā muslimụn
3|65|y<b>ā</b> ahlal-kitābi lima tuḥ<b>ā</b>jjụna f<b>ī</b> ibrāhīma wa m<b>ā</b> unzilatit-taurātu wal-injīlu illā mim ba'dih, a fa lā ta'qilụn
3|66|h<b>ā</b>`antum h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`i ḥājajtum fīmā lakum bihī 'ilmun fa lima tuḥ<b>ā</b>jjụna fīmā laisa lakum bihī 'ilm, wallāhu ya'lamu wa antum lā ta'lamụn
3|67|mā kāna ibrāhīmu yahụdiyyaw wa lā naṣrāniyyaw wa lāking kāna ḥanīfam muslimā, wa mā kāna minal-musyrikīn
3|68|inna aulan-nāsi bi`ibrāhīma lallażīnattaba'ụhu wa hāżan-nabiyyu wallażīna āmanụ, wallāhu waliyyul-mu`minīn
3|69|waddaṭ ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatum min ahlil-kitābi lau yuḍillụnakum, wa mā yuḍillụna ill<b>ā</b> anfusahum wa mā yasy'urụn
3|70|y<b>ā</b> ahlal-kitābi lima takfurụna bi`āyātillāhi wa antum tasy-hadụn
3|71|y<b>ā</b> ahlal-kitābi lima talbisụnal-ḥaqqa bil-bāṭili wa taktumụnal-ḥaqqa wa antum ta'lamụn
3|72|wa qālaṭ ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatum min ahlil-kitābi āminụ billaż<b>ī</b> unzila 'alallażīna āmanụ waj-han-nahāri wakfur<b>ū</b> ākhirahụ la'allahum yarji'ụn
3|73|wa lā tu`min<b>ū</b> illā liman tabi'a dīnakum, qul innal-hudā hudallāhi ay yu`t<b>ā</b> aḥadum miṡla m<b>ā</b> ụtītum au yuḥ<b>ā</b>jjụkum 'inda rabbikum, qul innal-faḍla biyadillāh, yu`tīhi may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu wāsi'un 'alīm
3|74|yakhtaṣṣu biraḥmatihī may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu żul-faḍlil-'aẓīm
3|75|wa min ahlil-kitābi man in ta`man-hu biqinṭāriy yu`addih<b>ī</b> ilaīk, wa min-hum man in ta`man-hu bidīnāril lā yu`addih<b>ī</b> ilaika illā mā dumta 'alaihi q<b>ā</b>`imā, żālika bi`annahum qālụ laisa 'alainā fil-ummiyyīna sabīl, wa yaqụlụna 'alallāhil-każiba wa hum ya'lamụn
3|76|balā man aufā bi'ahdihī wattaqā fa innallāha yuḥibbul-muttaqīn
3|77|innallażīna yasytarụna bi'ahdillāhi wa aimānihim ṡamanang qalīlan ul<b>ā</b>`ika lā khalāqa lahum fil-ākhirati wa lā yukallimuhumullāhu wa lā yanẓuru ilaihim yaumal-qiyāmati wa lā yuzakkīhim wa lahum 'ażābun alīm
3|78|wa inna min-hum lafarīqay yalwụna alsinatahum bil-kitābi litaḥsabụhu minal-kitābi wa mā huwa minal-kitāb, wa yaqụlụna huwa min 'indillāhi wa mā huwa min 'indillāh, wa yaqụlụna 'alallāhil-każiba wa hum ya'lamụn
3|79|mā kāna libasyarin ay yu`tiyahullāhul-kitāba wal-ḥukma wan-nubuwwata ṡumma yaqụla lin-nāsi kụnụ 'ibādal lī min dụnillāhi wa lāking kụnụ rabbāniyyīna bimā kuntum tu'allimụnal-kitāba wa bimā kuntum tadrusụn
3|80|wa lā ya`murakum an tattakhiżul-mal<b>ā</b>`ikata wan-nabiyyīna arbābā, a ya`murukum bil-kufri ba'da iż antum muslimụn
3|81|wa iż akhażallāhu mīṡāqan-nabiyyīna lam<b>ā</b> ātaitukum ming kitābiw wa ḥikmatin ṡumma j<b>ā</b>`akum rasụlum muṣaddiqul limā ma'akum latu`minunna bihī wa latanṣurunnah, qāla a aqrartum wa akhażtum 'alā żālikum iṣrī, qāl<b>ū</b> aqrarnā, qāla fasy-hadụ wa ana ma'akum minasy-syāhidīn
3|82|fa man tawallā ba'da żālika fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-fāsiqụn
3|83|a fa gaira dīnillāhi yabgụna wa lah<b>ū</b> aslama man fis-samāwāti wal-arḍi ṭau'aw wa kar-haw wa ilaihi yurja'ụn
3|84|qul āmannā billāhi wa m<b>ā</b> unzila 'alainā wa m<b>ā</b> unzila 'al<b>ā</b> ibrāhīma wa ismā'īla wa is-ḥāqa wa ya'qụba wal-asbāṭi wa m<b>ā</b> ụtiya mụsā wa 'īsā wan-nabiyyụna mir rabbihim lā nufarriqu baina aḥadim min-hum wa naḥnu lahụ muslimụn
3|85|wa may yabtagi gairal-islāmi dīnan fa lay yuqbala min-h, wa huwa fil-ākhirati minal-khāsirīn
3|86|kaifa yahdillāhu qaumang kafarụ ba'da īmānihim wa syahid<b>ū</b> annar-rasụla ḥaqquw wa j<b>ā</b>`ahumul-bayyināt, wallāhu lā yahdil-qaumaẓ-ẓālimīn
3|87|ul<b>ā</b>`ika jaz<b>ā</b>`uhum anna 'alaihim la'natallāhi wal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati wan-nāsi ajma'īn
3|88|khālidīna fīhā, lā yukhaffafu 'an-humul-'ażābu wa lā hum yunẓarụn
3|89|illallażīna tābụ mim ba'di żālika wa aṣlaḥụ, fa innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
3|90|innallażīna kafarụ ba'da īmānihim ṡummazdādụ kufral lan tuqbala taubatuhum, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humuḍ-ḍ<b>ā</b>llụn
3|91|innallażīna kafarụ wa mātụ wa hum kuffārun fa lay yuqbala min aḥadihim mil`ul-arḍi żahabaw wa lawiftadā bih, ul<b>ā</b>`ika lahum 'ażābun alīmuw wa mā lahum min nāṣirīn
3|92|lan tanālul-birra ḥattā tunfiqụ mimmā tuḥibbụn, wa mā tunfiqụ min syai`in fa innallāha bihī 'alīm
3|93|kulluṭ-ṭa'āmi kāna ḥillal liban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla illā mā ḥarrama isr<b>ā</b>`īlu 'alā nafsihī ming qabli an tunazzalat-taurāh, qul fa`tụ bit-taurāti fatlụh<b>ā</b> ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
3|94|fa maniftarā 'alallāhil-każiba mim ba'di żālika fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humuẓ-ẓālimụn
3|95|qul ṣadaqallāh, fattabi'ụ millata ibrāhīma ḥanīfā, wa mā kāna minal-musyrikīn
3|96|inna awwala baitiw wuḍi'a lin-nāsi lallażī bibakkata mubārakaw wa hudal lil-'ālamīn
3|97|fīhi āyātum bayyinātum maqāmu ibrāhīm, wa man dakhalahụ kāna āminā, wa lillāhi 'alan-nāsi ḥijjul-baiti manistaṭā'a ilaihi sabīlā, wa mang kafara fa innallāha ganiyyun 'anil-'ālamīn
3|98|qul y<b>ā</b> ahlal-kitābi lima takfurụna bi`āyātillāhi wallāhu syahīdun 'alā mā ta'malụn
3|99|qul y<b>ā</b> ahlal-kitābi lima taṣuddụna 'an sabīlillāhi man āmana tabgụnahā 'iwajaw wa antum syuhad<b>ā</b>`, wa mallāhu bigāfilin 'ammā ta'malụn
3|100|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> in tuṭī'ụ farīqam minallażīna ụtul-kitāba yaruddụkum ba'da īmānikum kāfirīn
3|101|wa kaifa takfurụna wa antum tutlā 'alaikum āyātullāhi wa fīkum rasụluh, wa may ya'taṣim billāhi fa qad hudiya ilā ṣirāṭim mustaqīm
3|102|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanuttaqullāha ḥaqqa tuqātihī wa lā tamụtunna illā wa antum muslimụn
3|103|wa'taṣimụ biḥablillāhi jamī'aw wa lā tafarraqụ ważkurụ ni'matallāhi 'alaikum iż kuntum a'd<b>ā</b>`an fa allafa baina qulụbikum fa aṣbaḥtum bini'matih<b>ī</b> ikhwānā, wa kuntum 'alā syafā ḥufratim minan-nāri fa angqażakum min-hā, każālika yubayyinullāhu lakum āyātihī la'allakum tahtadụn
3|104|waltakum mingkum ummatuy yad'ụna ilal-khairi wa ya`murụna bil-ma'rụfi wa yan-hauna 'anil-mungkar, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-mufliḥụn
3|105|wa lā takụnụ kallażīna tafarraqụ wakhtalafụ mim ba'di mā j<b>ā</b>`ahumul-bayyināt, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika lahum 'ażābun 'aẓīm
3|106|yauma tabyaḍḍu wujụhuw wa taswaddu wujụh, fa ammallażīnaswaddat wujụhuhum, a kafartum ba'da īmānikum fa żụqul-'ażāba bimā kuntum takfurụn
3|107|wa ammallażīnabyaḍḍat wujụhuhum fa fī raḥmatillāh, hum fīhā khālidụn
3|108|tilka āyātullāhi natlụhā 'alaika bil-ḥaqq, wa mallāhu yurīdu ẓulmal lil-'ālamīn
3|109|wa lillāhi mā fis-samāwāti wa mā fil-arḍ, wa ilallāhi turja'ul-umụr
3|110|kuntum khaira ummatin ukhrijat lin-nāsi ta`murụna bil-ma'rụfi wa tan-hauna 'anil-mungkari wa tu`minụna billāh, walau āmana ahlul-kitābi lakāna khairal lahum, min-humul-mu`minụna wa akṡaruhumul-fāsiqụn
3|111|lay yaḍurrụkum ill<b>ā</b> ażā, wa iy yuqātilụkum yuwallụkumul-adbār, ṡumma lā yunṣarụn
3|112|ḍuribat 'alaihimuż-żillatu aina mā ṡuqif<b>ū</b> illā biḥablim minallāhi wa ḥablim minan-nāsi wa b<b>ā</b>`ụ bigaḍabim minallāhi wa ḍuribat 'alaihimul-maskanah, żālika bi`annahum kānụ yakfurụna bi`āyātillāhi wa yaqtulụnal-ambiy<b>ā</b>`a bigairi ḥaqq, żālika bimā 'aṣaw wa kānụ ya'tadụn
3|113|laisụ saw<b>ā</b>`ā, min ahlil-kitābi ummatung q<b>ā</b>`imatuy yatlụna āyātillāhi ān<b>ā</b>`al-laili wa hum yasjudụn
3|114|yu`minụna billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri wa ya`murụna bil-ma'rụfi wa yan-hauna 'anil-mungkari wa yusāri'ụna fil-khairāt, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika minaṣ-ṣāliḥīn
3|115|wa mā yaf'alụ min khairin fa lay yukfarụh, wallāhu 'alīmum bil-muttaqīn
3|116|innallażīna kafarụ lan tugniya 'an-hum amwāluhum wa l<b>ā</b> aulāduhum minallāhi syai`ā, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
3|117|maṡalu mā yunfiqụna fī hāżihil-ḥayātid-dun-yā kamaṡali rīḥin fīhā ṣirrun aṣābat ḥarṡa qaumin ẓalam<b>ū</b> anfusahum fa ahlakat-h, wa mā ẓalamahumullāhu wa lākin anfusahum yaẓlimụn
3|118|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ lā tattakhiżụ biṭānatam min dụnikum lā ya`lụnakum khabālā, waddụ mā 'anittum, qad badatil-bagḍ<b>ā</b>`u min afwāhihim wa mā tukhfī ṣudụruhum akbar, qad bayyannā lakumul-āyāti ing kuntum ta'qilụn
3|119|h<b>ā</b>`antum ul<b>ā</b>`i tuḥibbụnahum wa lā yuḥibbụnakum wa tu`minụna bil-kitābi kullih, wa iżā laqụkum qāl<b>ū</b> āmannā wa iżā khalau 'aḍḍụ 'alaikumul-anāmila minal-gaīẓ, qul mụtụ bigaiẓikum, innallāha 'alīmum biżātiṣ-ṣudụr
3|120|in tamsaskum ḥasanatun tasu`hum wa in tuṣibkum sayyi`atuy yafraḥụ bihā, wa in taṣbirụ wa tattaqụ lā yaḍurrukum kaiduhum syai`ā, innallāha bimā ya'malụna muḥīṭ
3|121|wa iż gadauta min ahlika tubawwi`ul-mu`minīna maqā'ida lil-qitāl, wallāhu samī'un 'alīm
3|122|iż hammaṭ ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatāni mingkum an tafsyalā wallāhu waliyyuhumā, wa 'alallāhi falyatawakkalil-mu`minụn
3|123|wa laqad naṣarakumullāhu bibadriw wa antum ażillah, fattaqullāha la'allakum tasykurụn
3|124|iż taqụlu lil-mu`minīna a lay yakfiyakum ay yumiddakum rabbukum biṡalāṡati ālāfim minal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati munzalīn
3|125|bal<b>ā</b> in taṣbirụ wa tattaqụ wa ya`tụkum min faurihim hāżā yumdidkum rabbukum bikhamsati ālāfim minal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati musawwimīn
3|126|wa mā ja'alahullāhu illā busyrā lakum wa litaṭma`inna qulụbukum bih, wa man-naṣru illā min 'indillāhil-'azīzil-ḥakīm
3|127|liyaqṭa'a ṭarafam minallażīna kafar<b>ū</b> au yakbitahum fa yangqalibụ kh<b>ā</b>`ibīn
3|128|laisa laka minal-amri syai`un au yatụba 'alaihim au yu'ażżibahum fa innahum ẓālimụn
3|129|wa lillāhi mā fis-samāwāti wa mā fil-arḍ, yagfiru limay yasy<b>ā</b>`u wa yu'ażżibu may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu gafụrur raḥīm
3|130|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ lā ta`kulur-rib<b>ā</b> aḍ'āfam muḍā'afataw wattaqullāha la'allakum tufliḥụn
3|131|wattaqun-nārallat<b>ī</b> u'iddat lil-kāfirīn
3|132|wa aṭī'ullāha war-rasụla la'allakum tur-ḥamụn
3|133|wa sāri'<b>ū</b> ilā magfiratim mir rabbikum wa jannatin 'arḍuhas-samāwātu wal-arḍu u'iddat lil-muttaqīn
3|134|allażīna yunfiqụna fis-sarr<b>ā</b>`i waḍ-ḍarr<b>ā</b>`i wal-kāẓimīnal-gaiẓa wal-'āfīna 'anin-nās, wallāhu yuḥibbul-muḥsinīn
3|135|wallażīna iżā fa'alụ fāḥisyatan au ẓalam<b>ū</b> anfusahum żakarullāha fastagfarụ liżunụbihim, wa may yagfiruż-żunụba illallāh, wa lam yuṣirrụ 'alā mā fa'alụ wa hum ya'lamụn
3|136|ul<b>ā</b>`ika jaz<b>ā</b>`uhum magfiratum mir rabbihim wa jannātun tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hāru khālidīna fīhā, wa ni'ma ajrul-'āmilīn
3|137|qad khalat ming qablikum sunanun fa sīrụ fil-arḍi fanẓurụ kaifa kāna 'āqibatul-mukażżibīn
3|138|hāżā bayānul lin-nāsi wa hudaw wa mau'iẓatul lil-muttaqīn
3|139|wa lā tahinụ wa lā taḥzanụ wa antumul-a'launa ing kuntum mu`minīn
3|140|iy yamsaskum qar-ḥun fa qad massal-qauma qar-ḥum miṡluh, wa tilkal-ayyāmu nudāwiluhā bainan-nās, wa liya'lamallāhullażīna āmanụ wa yattakhiża mingkum syuhad<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu lā yuḥibbuẓ-ẓālimīn
3|141|wa liyumaḥḥiṣallāhullażīna āmanụ wa yam-ḥaqal-kāfirīn
3|142|am ḥasibtum an tadkhulul-jannata wa lammā ya'lamillāhullażīna jāhadụ mingkum wa ya'lamaṣ-ṣābirīn
3|143|wa laqad kuntum tamannaunal-mauta ming qabli an talqauhu fa qad ra`aitumụhu wa antum tanẓurụn
3|144|wa mā muḥammadun illā rasụl, qad khalat ming qablihir-rusul, a fa im māta au qutilangqalabtum 'al<b>ā</b> a'qābikum, wa may yangqalib 'alā 'aqibaihi fa lay yaḍurrallāha syai`ā, wa sayajzillāhusy-syākirīn
3|145|wa mā kāna linafsin an tamụta illā bi`iżnillāhi kitābam mu`ajjalā, wa may yurid ṡawābad-dun-yā nu`tihī min-hā, wa may yurid ṡawābal-ākhirati nu`tihī min-hā, wa sanajzisy-syākirīn
3|146|wa ka`ayyim min nabiyying qātala ma'ahụ ribbiyyụna kaṡīr, fa mā wahanụ lim<b>ā</b> aṣābahum fī sabīlillāhi wa mā ḍa'ufụ wa mastakānụ, wallāhu yuḥibbuṣ-ṣābirīn
3|147|wa mā kāna qaulahum ill<b>ā</b> ang qālụ rabbanagfir lanā żunụbanā wa isrāfanā f<b>ī</b> amrinā wa ṡabbit aqdāmanā wanṣurnā 'alal-qaumil-kāfirīn
3|148|fa ātāhumullāhu ṡawābad-dun-yā wa ḥusna ṡawābil-ākhirah, wallāhu yuḥibbul-muḥsinīn
3|149|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> in tuṭī'ullażīna kafarụ yaruddụkum 'al<b>ā</b> a'qābikum fa tangqalibụ khāsirīn
3|150|balillāhu maulākum, wa huwa khairun nāṣirīn
3|151|sanulqī fī qulụbillażīna kafarur-ru'ba bim<b>ā</b> asyrakụ billāhi mā lam yunazzil bihī sulṭānā, wa ma`wāhumun-nār, wa bi`sa maṡwaẓ-ẓālimīn
3|152|wa laqad ṣadaqakumullāhu wa'dah<b>ū</b> iż taḥussụnahum bi`iżnih, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iżā fasyiltum wa tanāza'tum fil-amri wa 'aṣaitum mim ba'di m<b>ā</b> arākum mā tuḥibbụn, mingkum may yurīdud-dun-yā wa mingkum may yurīdul-ākhirah, ṡumma ṣarafakum 'an-hum liyabtaliyakum, wa laqad 'afā 'angkum, wallāhu żụ faḍlin 'alal-mu`minīn
3|153|iż tuṣ'idụna wa lā talwụna 'al<b>ā</b> aḥadiw war-rasụlu yad'ụkum f<b>ī</b> ukhrākum fa aṡābakum gammam bigammil likai lā taḥzanụ 'alā mā fātakum wa lā m<b>ā</b> aṣābakum, wallāhu khabīrum bimā ta'malụn
3|154|ṡumma anzala 'alaikum mim ba'dil-gammi amanatan nu'āsay yagsyā ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatam mingkum wa ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatung qad ahammat-hum anfusuhum yaẓunnụna billāhi gairal-ḥaqqi ẓannal-jāhiliyyah, yaqụlụna hal lanā minal-amri min syaī`, qul innal-amra kullahụ lillāh, yukhfụna f<b>ī</b> anfusihim mā lā yubdụna lak, yaqụlụna lau kāna lanā minal-amri syai`um mā qutilnā hāhunā, qul lau kuntum fī buyụtikum labarazallażīna kutiba 'alaihimul-qatlu ilā maḍāji'ihim, wa liyabtaliyallāhu mā fī ṣudụrikum wa liyumaḥḥiṣa mā fī qulụbikum, wallāhu 'alīmum biżātiṣ-ṣudụr
3|155|innallażīna tawallau mingkum yaumaltaqal-jam'āni innamastazallahumusy-syaiṭānu biba'ḍi mā kasabụ, wa laqad 'afallāhu 'an-hum, innallāha gafụrun ḥalīm
3|156|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ lā takụnụ kallażīna kafarụ wa qālụ li`ikhwānihim iżā ḍarabụ fil-arḍi au kānụ guzzal lau kānụ 'indanā mā mātụ wa mā qutilụ, liyaj'alallāhu żālika ḥasratan fī qulụbihim, wallāhu yuḥyī wa yumīt, wallāhu bimā ta'malụna baṣīr
3|157|wa la`ing qutiltum fī sabīlillāhi au muttum lamagfiratum minallāhi wa raḥmatun khairum mimmā yajma'ụn
3|158|wa la`im muttum au qutiltum la`ilallāhi tuḥsyarụn
3|159|fa bimā raḥmatim minallāhi linta lahum, walau kunta faẓẓan galīẓal-qalbi lanfaḍḍụ min ḥaulika fa'fu 'an-hum wastagfir lahum wa syāwir-hum fil-amr, fa iżā 'azamta fa tawakkal 'alallāh, innallāha yuḥibbul-mutawakkilīn
3|160|iy yanṣurkumullāhu fa lā gāliba lakum, wa iy yakhżulkum fa man żallażī yanṣurukum mim ba'dih, wa 'alallāhi falyatawakkalil-mu`minụn
3|161|wa mā kāna linabiyyin ay yagull, wa may yaglul ya`ti bimā galla yaumal-qiyāmah, ṡumma tuwaffā kullu nafsim mā kasabat wa hum lā yuẓlamụn
3|162|a fa manittaba'a riḍwānallāhi kamam b<b>ā</b>`a bisakhaṭim minallāhi wa ma`wāhu jahannam, wa bi`sal-maṣīr
3|163|hum darajātun 'indallāh, wallāhu baṣīrum bimā ya'malụn
3|164|laqad mannallāhu 'alal-mu`minīna iż ba'aṡa fīhim rasụlam min anfusihim yatlụ 'alaihim āyātihī wa yuzakkīhim wa yu'allimuhumul-kitāba wal-ḥikmah, wa ing kānụ ming qablu lafī ḍalālim mubīn
3|165|a wa lamm<b>ā</b> aṣābatkum muṣībatung qad aṣabtum miṡlaihā qultum annā hāżā, qul huwa min 'indi anfusikum, innallāha 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
3|166|wa m<b>ā</b> aṣābakum yaumaltaqal-jam'āni fa bi`iżnillāhi wa liya'lamal-mu`minīn
3|167|wa liya'lamallażīna nāfaqụ wa qīla lahum ta'ālau qātilụ fī sabīlillāhi awidfa'ụ, qālụ lau na'lamu qitālal lattaba'nākum, hum lil-kufri yauma`iżin aqrabu min-hum lil-īmān, yaqụlụna bi`afwāhihim mā laisa fī qulụbihim, wallāhu a'lamu bimā yaktumụn
3|168|allażīna qālụ li`ikhwānihim wa qa'adụ lau aṭā'ụnā mā qutilụ, qul fadra`ụ 'an anfusikumul-mauta ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
3|169|wa lā taḥsabannallażīna qutilụ fī sabīlillāhi amwātā, bal aḥy<b>ā</b>`un 'inda rabbihim yurzaqụn
3|170|fariḥīna bim<b>ā</b> ātāhumullāhu min faḍlihī wa yastabsyirụna billażīna lam yal-ḥaqụ bihim min khalfihim allā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
3|171|yastabsyirụna bini'matim minallāhi wa faḍl, wa annallāha lā yuḍī'u ajral-mu`minīn
3|172|allażīnastajābụ lillāhi war-rasụli mim ba'di m<b>ā</b> aṣābahumul-qar-ḥu lillażīna aḥsanụ min-hum wattaqau ajrun 'aẓīm
3|173|allażīna qāla lahumun-nāsu innan-nāsa qad jama'ụ lakum fakhsyauhum fa zādahum īmānaw wa qālụ ḥasbunallāhu wa ni'mal-wakīl
3|174|fangqalabụ bini'matim minallāhi wa faḍlil lam yamsas-hum s<b>ū</b>`uw wattaba'ụ riḍwānallāh, wallāhu żụ faḍlin 'aẓīm
3|175|innamā żālikumusy-syaiṭānu yukhawwifu auliy<b>ā</b>`ahụ fa lā takhāfụhum wa khāfụni ing kuntum mu`minīn
3|176|wa lā yaḥzungkallażīna yusāri'ụna fil-kufr, innahum lay yaḍurrullāha syai`ā, yurīdullāhu allā yaj'ala lahum ḥaẓẓan fil-ākhirati wa lahum 'ażābun 'aẓīm
3|177|innallażīnasytarawul-kufra bil-īmāni lay yaḍurrullāha syai`ā, wa lahum 'ażābun alīm
3|178|wa lā yaḥsabannallażīna kafar<b>ū</b> annamā numlī lahum khairul li`anfusihim, innamā numlī lahum liyazdād<b>ū</b> iṡmā, wa lahum 'ażābum muhīn
3|179|mā kānallāhu liyażaral-mu`minīna 'alā m<b>ā</b> antum 'alaihi ḥattā yamīzal-khabīṡa minaṭ-ṭayyib, wa mā kānallāhu liyuṭli'akum 'alal-gaibi wa lākinnallāha yajtabī mir rusulihī may yasy<b>ā</b>`u fa āminụ billāhi wa rusulih, wa in tu`minụ wa tattaqụ fa lakum ajrun 'aẓīm
3|180|wa lā yaḥsabannallażīna yabkhalụna bim<b>ā</b> ātāhumullāhu min faḍlihī huwa khairal lahum, bal huwa syarrul lahum, sayuṭawwaqụna mā bakhilụ bihī yaumal-qiyāmah, wa lillāhi mīrāṡus-samāwāti wal-arḍ, wallāhu bimā ta'malụna khabīr
3|181|laqad sami'allāhu qaulallażīna qāl<b>ū</b> innallāha faqīruw wa naḥnu agniy<b>ā</b>`, sanaktubu mā qālụ wa qatlahumul-ambiy<b>ā</b>`a bigairi ḥaqqiw wa naqụlu żụqụ 'ażābal-ḥarīq
3|182|żālika bimā qaddamat aidīkum wa annallāha laisa biẓallāmil lil-'abīd
3|183|allażīna qāl<b>ū</b> innallāha 'ahida ilain<b>ā</b> allā nu`mina lirasụlin ḥattā ya`tiyanā biqurbānin ta`kuluhun-nār, qul qad j<b>ā</b>`akum rusulum ming qablī bil-bayyināti wa billażī qultum fa lima qataltumụhum ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
3|184|fa ing każżabụka fa qad kużżiba rusulum ming qablika j<b>ā</b>`ụ bil-bayyināti waz-zuburi wal-kitābil-munīr
3|185|kullu nafsin ż<b>ā</b>`iqatul maụt, wa innamā tuwaffauna ujụrakum yaumal-qiyāmah, fa man zuḥziḥa 'anin-nāri wa udkhilal-jannata fa qad fāz, wa mal-ḥayātud-dun-y<b>ā</b> illā matā'ul-gurụr
3|186|latublawunna f<b>ī</b> amwālikum wa anfusikum, wa latasma'unna minallażīna ụtul-kitāba ming qablikum wa minallażīna asyrak<b>ū</b> ażang kaṡīrā, wa in taṣbirụ wa tattaqụ fa inna żālika min 'azmil-umụr
3|187|wa iż akhażallāhu mīṡāqallażīna ụtul-kitāba latubayyinunnahụ lin-nāsi wa lā taktumụnahụ fa nabażụhu war<b>ā</b>`a ẓuhụrihim wasytarau bihī ṡamanang qalīlā, fa bi`sa mā yasytarụn
3|188|lā taḥsabannallażīna yafraḥụna bim<b>ā</b> ataw wa yuḥibbụna ay yuḥmadụ bimā lam yaf'alụ fa lā taḥsabannahum bimafāzatim minal-'ażāb, wa lahum 'ażābun alīm
3|189|wa lillāhi mulkus-samāwāti wal-arḍ, wallāhu 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
3|190|inna fī khalqis-samāwāti wal-arḍi wakhtilāfil-laili wan-nahāri la`āyātil li`ulil-albāb
3|191|allażīna yażkurụnallāha qiyāmaw wa qu'ụdaw wa 'alā junụbihim wa yatafakkarụna fī khalqis-samāwāti wal-arḍ, rabbanā mā khalaqta hāżā bāṭilā, sub-ḥānaka fa qinā 'ażāban-nār
3|192|rabban<b>ā</b> innaka man tudkhilin-nāra fa qad akhzaitah, wa mā liẓ-ẓālimīna min anṣār
3|193|rabban<b>ā</b> innanā sami'nā munādiyay yunādī lil-īmāni an āminụ birabbikum fa āmannā rabbanā fagfir lanā żunụbanā wa kaffir 'annā sayyi`ātinā wa tawaffanā ma'al-abrār
3|194|rabbanā wa ātinā mā wa'attanā 'alā rusulika wa lā tukhzinā yaumal-qiyāmah, innaka lā tukhliful-mī'ād
3|195|fastajāba lahum rabbuhum annī l<b>ā</b> uḍī'u 'amala 'āmilim mingkum min żakarin au unṡā, ba'ḍukum mim ba'ḍ, fallażīna hājarụ wa ukhrijụ min diyārihim wa ụżụ fī sabīlī wa qātalụ wa qutilụ la`ukaffiranna 'an-hum sayyi`ātihim wa la`udkhilannahum jannātin tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hār, ṡawābam min 'indillāh, wallāhu 'indahụ ḥusnuṡ-ṡawāb
3|196|lā yagurrannaka taqallubullażīna kafarụ fil-bilād
3|197|matā'ung qalīl, ṡumma ma`wāhum jahannam, wa bi`sal-mihād
3|198|lākinillażīnattaqau rabbahum lahum jannātun tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hāru khālidīna fīhā nuzulam min 'indillāh, wa mā 'indallāhi khairul lil-abrār
3|199|wa inna min ahlil-kitābi lamay yu`minu billāhi wa m<b>ā</b> unzila ilaikum wa m<b>ā</b> unzila ilaihim khāsyi'īna lillāhi lā yasytarụna bi`āyātillāhi ṡamanang qalīlā, ul<b>ā</b>`ika lahum ajruhum 'inda rabbihim, innallāha sarī'ul-ḥisāb
3|200|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanuṣbirụ wa ṣābirụ wa rābiṭụ, wattaqullāha la'allakum tufliḥụn
4|1|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsuttaqụ rabbakumullażī khalaqakum min nafsiw wāḥidatiw wa khalaqa min-hā zaujahā wa baṡṡa min-humā rijālang kaṡīraw wa nis<b>ā</b>`ā, wattaqullāhallażī tas<b>ā</b>`alụna bihī wal-ar-ḥām, innallāha kāna 'alaikum raqībā
4|2|wa ātul-yatām<b>ā</b> amwālahum wa lā tatabaddalul-khabīṡa biṭ-ṭayyibi wa lā ta`kul<b>ū</b> amwālahum il<b>ā</b> amwālikum, innahụ kāna ḥụbang kabīrā
4|3|wa in khiftum allā tuqsiṭụ fil-yatāmā fangkiḥụ mā ṭāba lakum minan-nis<b>ā</b>`i maṡnā wa ṡulāṡa wa rubā', fa in khiftum allā ta'dilụ fa wāḥidatan au mā malakat aimānukum, żālika adn<b>ā</b> allā ta'ụlụ
4|4|wa ātun-nis<b>ā</b>`a ṣaduqātihinna niḥlah, fa in ṭibna lakum 'an syai`im min-hu nafsan fa kulụhu han<b>ī</b>`am mar<b>ī</b>`ā
4|5|wa lā tu`tus-sufah<b>ā</b>`a amwālakumullatī ja'alallāhu lakum qiyāmaw warzuqụhum fīhā waksụhum wa qụlụ lahum qaulam ma'rụfā
4|6|wabtalul-yatāmā ḥatt<b>ā</b> iżā balagun-nikāḥ, fa in ānastum min-hum rusydan fadfa'<b>ū</b> ilaihim amwālahum, wa lā ta`kulụh<b>ā</b> isrāfaw wa bidāran ay yakbarụ, wa mang kāna ganiyyan falyasta'fif, wa mang kāna faqīran falya`kul bil-ma'rụf, fa iżā dafa'tum ilaihim amwālahum fa asy-hidụ 'alaihim, wa kafā billāhi ḥasībā
