7|23|qālā rabbanā ẓalamn<b>ā</b> anfusana wa il lam tagfir lanā wa tar-ḥamnā lanakụnanna minal-khāsirīn
7|24|qālahbiṭụ ba'ḍukum liba'ḍin 'aduww, wa lakum fil-arḍi mustaqarruw wa matā'un ilā ḥīn
7|25|qāla fīhā taḥyauna wa fīhā tamụtụna wa min-hā tukhrajụn
7|26|yā ban<b>ī</b> ādama qad anzalnā 'alaikum libāsay yuwārī sau`ātikum warīsyā, wa libāsut-taqwā żālika khaīr, żālika min āyātillāhi la'allahum yażżakkarụn
7|27|yā ban<b>ī</b> ādama lā yaftinannakumusy-syaiṭānu kam<b>ā</b> akhraja abawaikum minal-jannati yanzi'u 'an-humā libāsahumā liyuriyahumā sau`ātihimā, innahụ yarākum huwa wa qabīluhụ min ḥaiṡu lā taraunahum, innā ja'alnasy-syayāṭīna auliy<b>ā</b>`a lillażīna lā yu`minụn
7|28|wa iżā fa'alụ fāḥisyatang qālụ wajadnā 'alaih<b>ā</b> āb<b>ā</b>`anā wallāhu amaranā bihā, qul innallāha lā ya`muru bil-faḥsy<b>ā</b>`, a taqụlụna 'alallāhi mā lā ta'lamụn
7|29|qul amara rabbī bil-qisṭ, wa aqīmụ wujụhakum 'inda kulli masjidiw wad'ụhu mukhliṣīna lahud-dīn, kamā bada`akum ta'ụdụn
7|30|farīqan hadā wa farīqan ḥaqqa 'alaihimuḍ-ḍalālah, innahumuttakhażusy-syayāṭīna auliy<b>ā</b>`a min dụnillāhi wa yaḥsabụna annahum muhtadụn
7|31|yā ban<b>ī</b> ādama khużụ zīnatakum 'inda kulli masjidiw wa kulụ wasyrabụ wa lā tusrifụ, innahụ lā yuḥibbul-musrifīn
7|32|qul man ḥarrama zīnatallāhillat<b>ī</b> akhraja li'ibādihī waṭ-ṭayyibāti minar-rizq, qul hiya lillażīna āmanụ fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā khāliṣatay yaumal-qiyāmah, każālika nufaṣṣilul-āyāti liqaumiy ya'lamụn
7|33|qul innamā ḥarrama rabbiyal-fawāḥisya mā ẓahara min-hā wa mā baṭana wal-iṡma wal-bagya bigairil-ḥaqqi wa an tusyrikụ billāhi mā lam yunazzil bihī sulṭānaw wa an taqụlụ 'alallāhi mā lā ta'lamụn
7|34|wa likulli ummatin ajal, fa iżā j<b>ā</b>`a ajaluhum lā yasta`khirụna sā'ataw wa lā yastaqdimụn
7|35|yā ban<b>ī</b> ādama immā ya`tiyannakum rusulum mingkum yaquṣṣụna 'alaikum āyātī fa manittaqā wa aṣlaḥa fa lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
7|36|wallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā wastakbarụ 'an-h<b>ā</b> ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
7|37|fa man aẓlamu mim maniftarā 'alallāhi każiban au każżaba bi`āyātih, ul<b>ā</b>`ika yanaluhum naṣībuhum minal-kitāb, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iżā j<b>ā</b>`at-hum rusulunā yatawaffaunahum qāl<b>ū</b> aina mā kuntum tad'ụna min dụnillāh, qālụ ḍallụ 'annā wa syahidụ 'al<b>ā</b> anfusihim annahum kānụ kāfirīn
7|38|qāladkhulụ f<b>ī</b> umaming qad khalat ming qablikum minal-jinni wal-insi fin-nāri kullamā dakhalat ummatul la'anat ukhtahā, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iżad dārakụ fīhā jamī'ang qālat ukhrāhum li`ụlāhum rabbanā h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`i aḍallụnā fa ātihim 'ażāban ḍi'fam minan-nār, qāla likullin ḍi'fuw wa lākil lā ta'lamụn
7|39|wa qālat ụlāhum li`ukhrāhum fa mā kāna lakum 'alainā min faḍlin fa żụqul-'ażāba bimā kuntum taksibụn
7|40|innallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā wastakbarụ 'an-hā lā tufattaḥu lahum abwābus-sam<b>ā</b>`i wa lā yadkhulụnal-jannata ḥattā yalijal-jamalu fī sammil-khiyāṭ, wa każālika najzil-mujrimīn
7|41|lahum min jahannama mihāduw wa min fauqihim gawāsy, wa każālika najziẓ-ẓālimīn
7|42|wallażīna āmanụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāti lā nukallifu nafsan illā wus'ah<b>ā</b> ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābul-jannah, hum fīhā khālidụn
7|43|wa naza'nā mā fī ṣudụrihim min gillin tajrī min taḥtihimul-an-hār, wa qālul-ḥamdu lillāhillażī hadānā lihāżā, wa mā kunnā linahtadiya lau l<b>ā</b> an hadānallāh, laqad j<b>ā</b>`at rusulu rabbinā bil-ḥaqq, wa nụd<b>ū</b> an tilkumul-jannatu ụriṡtumụhā bimā kuntum ta'malụn
7|44|wa nād<b>ā</b> aṣ-ḥābul-jannati aṣ-ḥāban-nāri ang qad wajadnā mā wa'adanā rabbunā ḥaqqan fa hal wajattum mā wa'ada rabbukum ḥaqqā, qālụ na'am, fa ażżana mu`ażżinum bainahum al la'natullāhi 'alaẓ-ẓālimīn
7|45|allażīna yaṣuddụna 'an sabīlillāhi wa yabgụnahā 'iwajā, wa hum bil-ākhirati kāfirụn
7|46|wa bainahumā ḥijāb, wa 'alal-a'rāfi rijāluy ya'rifụna kullam bisīmāhum, wa nādau aṣ-ḥābal-jannati an salāmun 'alaikum, lam yadkhulụhā wa hum yaṭma'ụn
7|47|wa iżā ṣurifat abṣāruhum tilq<b>ā</b>`a aṣ-ḥābin-nāri qālụ rabbanā lā taj'alnā ma'al-qaumiẓ-ẓālimīn
7|48|wa nād<b>ā</b> aṣ-ḥābul-a'rāfi rijālay ya'rifụnahum bisīmāhum qālụ m<b>ā</b> agnā 'angkum jam'ukum wa mā kuntum tastakbirụn
7|49|a h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`illażīna aqsamtum lā yanaluhumullāhu biraḥmah, udkhulul-jannata lā khaufun 'alaikum wa l<b>ā</b> antum taḥzanụn
7|50|wa nād<b>ā</b> aṣ-ḥābun-nāri aṣ-ḥābal-jannati an afīḍụ 'alainā minal-m<b>ā</b>`i au mimmā razaqakumullāh, qāl<b>ū</b> innallāha ḥarramahumā 'alal-kāfirīn
7|51|allażīnattakhażụ dīnahum lahwaw wa la'ibaw wa garrat-humul-ḥayātud-dun-yā, fal-yauma nansāhum kamā nasụ liq<b>ā</b>`a yaumihim hāżā wa mā kānụ bi`āyātinā yaj-ḥadụn
7|52|wa laqad ji`nāhum bikitābin faṣṣalnāhu 'alā 'ilmin hudaw wa raḥmatal liqaumiy yu`minụn
7|53|hal yanẓurụna illā ta`wīlah, yauma ya`tī ta`wīluhụ yaqụlullażīna nasụhu ming qablu qad j<b>ā</b>`at rusulu rabbinā bil-ḥaqq, fa hal lanā min syufa'<b>ā</b>`a fa yasyfa'ụ lan<b>ā</b> au nuraddu fa na'mala gairallażī kunnā na'mal, qad khasir<b>ū</b> anfusahum wa ḍalla 'an-hum mā kānụ yaftarụn
7|54|inna rabbakumullāhullażī khalaqas-samāwāti wal-arḍa fī sittati ayyāmin ṡummastawā 'alal-'arsy, yugsyil-lailan-nahāra yaṭlubuhụ ḥaṡīṡaw wasy-syamsa wal-qamara wan-nujụma musakhkharātim bi`amrih<b>ī</b> alā lahul-khalqu wal-amr, tabārakallāhu rabbul-'ālamīn
7|55|ud'ụ rabbakum taḍarru'aw wa khufyah, innahụ lā yuḥibbul-mu'tadīn
7|56|wa lā tufsidụ fil-arḍi ba'da iṣlāḥihā wad'ụhu khaufaw wa ṭama'ā, inna raḥmatallāhi qarībum minal-muḥsinīn
7|57|wa huwallażī yursilur-riyāḥa busyram baina yadai raḥmatih, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iż<b>ā</b> aqallat saḥāban ṡiqālan suqnāhu libaladim mayyitin fa anzalnā bihil-m<b>ā</b>`a fa akhrajnā bihī ming kulliṡ-ṡamarāt, każālika nukhrijul-mautā la'allakum tażakkarụn
7|58|wal-baladuṭ-ṭayyibu yakhruju nabātuhụ bi`iżni rabbih, wallażī khabuṡa lā yakhruju illā nakidā, każālika nuṣarriful-āyāti liqaumiy yasykurụn
7|59|laqad arsalnā nụḥan ilā qaumihī fa qāla yā qaumi'budullāha mā lakum min ilāhin gairuh, inn<b>ī</b> akhāfu 'alaikum 'ażāba yaumin 'aẓīm
7|60|qālal-mala`u ming qaumih<b>ī</b> innā lanarāka fī ḍalālim mubīn
7|61|qāla yā qaumi laisa bī ḍalālatuw wa lākinnī rasụlum mir rabbil-'ālamīn
7|62|uballigukum risālāti rabbī wa anṣaḥu lakum wa a'lamu minallāhi mā lā ta'lamụn
7|63|a wa 'ajibtum an j<b>ā</b>`akum żikrum mir rabbikum 'alā rajulim mingkum liyunżirakum wa litattaqụ wa la'allakum tur-ḥamụn
7|64|fa każżabụhu fa anjaināhu wallażīna ma'ahụ fil-fulki wa agraqnallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā, innahum kānụ qauman 'amīn
7|65|wa ilā 'ādin akhāhum hụdā, qāla yā qaumi'budullāha mā lakum min ilāhin gairuh, a fa lā tattaqụn
7|66|qālal-mala`ullażīna kafarụ ming qaumih<b>ī</b> innā lanarāka fī safāhatiw wa innā lanaẓunnuka minal-kāżibīn
7|67|qāla yā qaumi laisa bī safāhatuw wa lākinnī rasụlum mir rabbil-'ālamīn
7|68|uballigukum risālāti rabbī wa ana lakum nāṣiḥun amīn
7|69|a wa 'ajibtum an j<b>ā</b>`akum żikrum mir rabbikum 'alā rajulim mingkum liyunżirakum, ważkur<b>ū</b> iż ja'alakum khulaf<b>ā</b>`a mim ba'di qaumi nụḥiw wa zādakum fil-khalqi baṣṭah, fażkur<b>ū</b> āl<b>ā</b>`allāhi la'allakum tufliḥụn
7|70|qāl<b>ū</b> a ji`tanā lina'budallāha waḥdahụ wa nażara mā kāna ya'budu āb<b>ā</b>`unā, fa`tinā bimā ta'idun<b>ā</b> ing kunta minaṣ-ṣādiqīn
7|71|qāla qad waqa'a 'alaikum mir rabbikum rijsuw wa gaḍab, a tujādilụnanī f<b>ī</b> asm<b>ā</b>`in sammaitumụh<b>ā</b> antum wa āb<b>ā</b>`ukum mā nazzalallāhu bihā min sulṭān, fantaẓir<b>ū</b> innī ma'akum minal-muntaẓirīn
7|72|fa anjaināhu wallażīna ma'ahụ biraḥmatim minnā wa qaṭa'nā dābirallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā wa mā kānụ mu`minīn
7|73|wa ilā ṡamụda akhāhum ṣāliḥā, qāla yā qaumi'budullāha mā lakum min ilāhin gairuh, qad j<b>ā</b>`atkum bayyinatum mir rabbikum, hāżihī nāqatullāhi lakum āyatan fa żarụhā ta`kul f<b>ī</b> arḍillāhi wa lā tamassụhā bis<b>ū</b>`in fa ya`khużakum 'ażābun alīm
7|74|ważkur<b>ū</b> iż ja'alakum khulaf<b>ā</b>`a mim ba'di 'ādiw wa bawwa`akum fil-arḍi tattakhiżụna min suhụlihā quṣụraw wa tan-ḥitụnal-jibāla buyụtā, fażkur<b>ū</b> āl<b>ā</b>`allāhi wa lā ta'ṡau fil-arḍi mufsidīn
7|75|qālal-mala`ullażīnastakbarụ ming qaumihī lillażīnastuḍ'ifụ liman āmana min-hum a ta'lamụna anna ṣāliḥam mursalum mir rabbih, qāl<b>ū</b> innā bim<b>ā</b> ursila bihī mu`minụn
7|76|qālallażīnastakbar<b>ū</b> innā billaż<b>ī</b> āmantum bihī kāfirụn
7|77|fa 'aqarun-nāqata wa 'atau 'an amri rabbihim wa qālụ yā ṣāliḥu`tinā bimā ta'idun<b>ā</b> ing kunta minal-mursalīn
7|78|fa akhażat-humur-rajfatu fa aṣbaḥụ fī dārihim jāṡimīn
7|79|fa tawallā 'an-hum wa qāla yā qaumi laqad ablagtukum risālata rabbī wa naṣaḥtu lakum wa lākil lā tuḥibbụnan-nāṣiḥīn
7|80|wa lụṭan iż qāla liqaumih<b>ī</b> a ta`tụnal-fāḥisyata mā sabaqakum bihā min aḥadim minal-'ālamīn
7|81|innakum lata`tụnar-rijāla syahwatam min dụnin-nis<b>ā</b>`, bal antum qaumum musrifụn
7|82|wa mā kāna jawāba qaumih<b>ī</b> ill<b>ā</b> ang qāl<b>ū</b> akhrijụhum ming qaryatikum, innahum unāsuy yataṭahharụn
7|83|fa anjaināhu wa ahlah<b>ū</b> illamra`atahụ kānat minal-gābirīn
7|84|wa amṭarnā 'alaihim maṭarā, fanẓur kaifa kāna 'āqibatul-mujrimīn
7|85|wa ilā madyana akhāhum syu'aibā, qāla yā qaumi'budullāha mā lakum min ilāhin gairuh, qad j<b>ā</b>`atkum bayyinatum mir rabbikum fa auful-kaila wal mīzāna wa lā tabkhasun-nāsa asy-y<b>ā</b>`ahum wa lā tufsidụ fil-arḍi ba'da iṣlāḥihā, żālikum khairul lakum ing kuntum mu`minīn
7|86|wa lā taq'udụ bikulli ṣirāṭin tụ'idụna wa taṣuddụna 'an sabīlillāhi man āmana bihī wa tabgụnahā 'iwajā, ważkur<b>ū</b> iż kuntum qalīlan fa kaṡṡarakum wanẓurụ kaifa kāna 'āqibatul-mufsidīn
7|87|wa ing kāna ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatum mingkum āmanụ billaż<b>ī</b> ursiltu bihī wa ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatul lam yu`minụ faṣbirụ ḥattā yaḥkumallāhu bainanā, wa huwa khairul-ḥākimīn
7|88|qālal-mala`ullażīnastakbarụ ming qaumihī lanukhrijannaka yā syu'aibu wallażīna āmanụ ma'aka ming qaryatin<b>ā</b> au lata'ụdunna fī millatinā, qāla a walau kunnā kārihīn
7|89|qadiftarainā 'alallāhi każiban in 'udnā fī millatikum ba'da iż najjānallāhu min-hā, wa mā yakụnu lan<b>ā</b> an na'ụda fīh<b>ā</b> ill<b>ā</b> ay yasy<b>ā</b>`allāhu rabbunā, wasi'a rabbunā kulla syai`in 'ilmā, 'alallāhi tawakkalnā, rabbanaftaḥ bainanā wa baina qauminā bil-ḥaqqi wa anta khairul-fātiḥīn
7|90|wa qālal-mala`ullażīna kafarụ ming qaumihī la`inittaba'tum syu'aiban innakum iżal lakhāsirụn
7|91|fa akhażat-humur-rajfatu fa aṣbaḥụ fī dārihim jāṡimīn
7|92|allażīna każżabụ syu'aibang ka`al lam yagnau fīhā, allażīna każżabụ syu'aibang kānụ humul-khāsirīn
7|93|fa tawallā 'an-hum wa qāla yā qaumi laqad ablagtukum risālāti rabbī wa naṣaḥtu lakum, fa kaifa āsā 'alā qauming kāfirīn
7|94|wa m<b>ā</b> arsalnā fī qaryatim min nabiyyin ill<b>ā</b> akhażn<b>ā</b> ahlahā bil-ba`s<b>ā</b>`i waḍ-ḍarr<b>ā</b>`i la'allahum yaḍḍarra'ụn
7|95|ṡumma baddalnā makānas-sayyi`atil-ḥasanata ḥattā 'afaw wa qālụ qad massa āb<b>ā</b>`anaḍ-ḍarr<b>ā</b>`u was-sarr<b>ā</b>`u fa akhażnāhum bagtataw wa hum lā yasy'urụn
7|96|walau anna ahlal-qur<b>ā</b> āmanụ wattaqau lafataḥnā 'alaihim barakātim minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i wal-arḍi wa lāking każżabụ fa akhażnāhum bimā kānụ yaksibụn
7|97|a fa amina ahlul-qur<b>ā</b> ay ya`tiyahum ba`sunā bayātaw wa hum n<b>ā</b>`imụn
7|98|a wa amina ahlul-qur<b>ā</b> ay ya`tiyahum ba`sunā ḍuḥaw wa hum yal'abụn
7|99|a fa aminụ makrallāh, fa lā ya`manu makrallāhi illal-qaumul-khāsirụn
7|100|a wa lam yahdi lillażīna yariṡụnal-arḍa mim ba'di ahlih<b>ā</b> al lau nasy<b>ā</b>`u aṣabnāhum biżunụbihim, wa naṭba'u 'alā qulụbihim fa hum lā yasma'ụn
7|101|tilkal-qurā naquṣṣu 'alaika min amb<b>ā</b>`ihā, wa laqad j<b>ā</b>`at-hum rusuluhum bil-bayyināt, fa mā kānụ liyu`minụ bimā każżabụ ming qabl, każālika yaṭba'ullāhu 'alā qulụbil-kāfirīn
7|102|wa mā wajadnā li`akṡarihim min 'ahd, wa iw wajadn<b>ā</b> akṡarahum lafāsiqīn
7|103|ṡumma ba'aṡnā mim ba'dihim mụsā bi`āyātin<b>ā</b> ilā fir'auna wa mala`ihī fa ẓalamụ bihā, fanẓur kaifa kāna 'āqibatul-mufsidīn
7|104|wa qāla mụsā yā fir'aunu innī rasụlum mir rabbil-'ālamīn
7|105|ḥaqīqun 'al<b>ā</b> al l<b>ā</b> aqụla 'alallāhi illal-ḥaqq, qad ji`tukum bibayyinatim mir rabbikum fa arsil ma'iya ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īl
7|106|qāla ing kunta ji`ta bi`āyatin fa`ti bih<b>ā</b> ing kunta minaṣ-ṣādiqīn
7|107|fa alqā 'aṣāhu fa iżā hiya ṡu'bānum mubīn
7|108|wa naza'a yadahụ fa iżā hiya baiḍ<b>ā</b>`u lin-nāẓirīn
7|109|qālal-mala`u ming qaumi fir'auna inna hāżā lasāḥirun 'alīm
7|110|yurīdu ay yukhrijakum min arḍikum, fa māżā ta`murụn
7|111|qāl<b>ū</b> arjih wa akhāhu wa arsil fil-mad<b>ā</b>`ini ḥāsyirīn
7|112|ya`tụka bikulli sāḥirin 'alīm
7|113|wa j<b>ā</b>`as-saḥaratu fir'auna qāl<b>ū</b> inna lanā la`ajran ing kunnā naḥnul-gālibīn
7|114|qāla na'am wa innakum laminal-muqarrabīn
7|115|qālụ yā mụs<b>ā</b> imm<b>ā</b> an tulqiya wa imm<b>ā</b> an nakụna naḥnul-mulqīn
7|116|qāla alqụ, fa lamm<b>ā</b> alqau saḥar<b>ū</b> a'yunan-nāsi wastar-habụhum wa j<b>ā</b>`ụ bisiḥrin 'aẓīm
7|117|wa auḥain<b>ā</b> ilā mụs<b>ā</b> an alqi 'aṣāk, fa iżā hiya talqafu mā ya`fikụn
7|118|fa waqa'al-ḥaqqu wa baṭala mā kānụ ya'malụn
7|119|fa gulibụ hunālika wangqalabụ ṣāgirīn
7|120|wa ulqiyas-saḥaratu sājidīn
7|121|qāl<b>ū</b> āmannā birabbil-'ālamīn
7|122|rabbi mụsā wa hārụn
7|123|qāla fir'aunu āmantum bihī qabla an āżana lakum, inna hāżā lamakrum makartumụhu fil-madīnati litukhrijụ min-h<b>ā</b> ahlahā, fa saufa ta'lamụn
7|124|la`uqaṭṭi'anna aidiyakum wa arjulakum min khilāfin ṡumma la`uṣallibannakum ajma'īn
7|125|qāl<b>ū</b> inn<b>ā</b> ilā rabbinā mungqalibụn
7|126|wa mā tangqimu minn<b>ā</b> ill<b>ā</b> an āmannā bi`āyāti rabbinā lammā j<b>ā</b>`atnā, rabban<b>ā</b> afrig 'alainā ṣabraw wa tawaffanā muslimīn
7|127|wa qālal-mala`u ming qaumi fir'auna a tażaru mụsā wa qaumahụ liyufsidụ fil-arḍi wa yażaraka wa ālihatak, qāla sanuqattilu abn<b>ā</b>`ahum wa nastaḥyī nis<b>ā</b>`ahum, wa innā fauqahum qāhirụn
7|128|qāla mụsā liqaumihista'īnụ billāhi waṣbirụ, innal-arḍa lillāh, yụriṡuhā may yasy<b>ā</b>`u min 'ibādih, wal-'āqibatu lil-muttaqīn
7|129|qāl<b>ū</b> ụżīnā ming qabli an ta`tiyana wa mim ba'di mā ji`tana, qāla 'asā rabbukum ay yuhlika 'aduwwakum wa yastakhlifakum fil-arḍi fa yanẓura kaifa ta'malụn
7|130|wa laqad akhażn<b>ā</b> āla fir'auna bis-sinīna wa naqṣim minaṡ-ṡamarāti la'allahum yażżakkarụn
7|131|fa iżā j<b>ā</b>`at-humul-ḥasanatu qālụ lanā hāżih, wa in tuṣib-hum sayyi`atuy yaṭṭayyarụ bimụsā wa mam ma'ah, al<b>ā</b> innamā ṭ<b>ā</b>`iruhum 'indallāhi wa lākinna akṡarahum lā ya'lamụn
7|132|wa qālụ mahmā ta`tinā bihī min āyatil litas-ḥaranā bihā fa mā naḥnu laka bimu`minīn
7|133|fa arsalnā 'alaihimuṭ-ṭụfāna wal-jarāda wal-qummala waḍ-ḍafādi'a wad-dama āyātim mufaṣṣalāt, fastakbarụ wa kānụ qaumam mujrimīn
7|134|wa lammā waqa'a 'alaihimur-rijzu qālụ yā mụsad'u lanā rabbaka bimā 'ahida 'indak, la`ing kasyafta 'annar-rijza lanu`minanna laka wa lanursilanna ma'aka ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īl
7|135|fa lammā kasyafnā 'an-humur-rijza il<b>ā</b> ajalin hum bāligụhu iżā hum yangkuṡụn
7|136|fantaqamnā min-hum fa agraqnāhum fil-yammi bi`annahum każżabụ bi`āyātinā wa kānụ 'an-hā gāfilīn
7|137|wa auraṡnal-qaumallażīna kānụ yustaḍ'afụna masyāriqal-arḍi wa magāribahallatī bāraknā fīhā, wa tammat kalimatu rabbikal-ḥusnā 'alā ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla bimā ṣabarụ, wa dammarnā mā kāna yaṣna'u fir'aunu wa qaumuhụ wa mā kānụ ya'risyụn
7|138|wa jāwaznā biban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īlal-baḥra fa atau 'alā qaumiy ya'kufụna 'al<b>ā</b> aṣnāmil lahum, qālụ yā mụsaj'al lan<b>ā</b> ilāhang kamā lahum ālihah, qāla innakum qaumun taj-halụn
7|139|inna h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`i mutabbarum mā hum fīhi wa bāṭilum mā kānụ ya'malụn
7|140|qāla a gairallāhi abgīkum ilāhaw wa huwa faḍḍalakum 'alal-'ālamīn
7|141|wa iż anjainākum min āli fir'auna yasụmụnakum s<b>ū</b>`al-'ażāb, yuqattilụna abn<b>ā</b>`akum wa yastaḥyụna nis<b>ā</b>`akum, wa fī żālikum bal<b>ā</b>`um mir rabbikum 'aẓīm
7|142|wa wā'adnā mụsā ṡalāṡīna lailataw wa atmamnāhā bi'asyrin fa tamma mīqātu rabbih<b>ī</b> arba'īna lailah, wa qāla mụsā li`akhīhi hārụnakhlufnī fī qaumī wa aṣliḥ wa lā tattabi' sabīlal-mufsidīn
7|143|wa lammā j<b>ā</b>`a mụsā limīqātinā wa kallamahụ rabbuhụ qāla rabbi arin<b>ī</b> anẓur ilaīk, qāla lan tarānī wa lākininẓur ilal-jabali fa inistaqarra makānahụ fa saufa tarānī, fa lammā tajallā rabbuhụ lil-jabali ja'alahụ dakkaw wa kharra mụsā ṣa'iqā, fa lamm<b>ā</b> afāqa qāla sub-ḥānaka tubtu ilaika wa ana awwalul-mu`minīn
7|144|qāla yā mụs<b>ā</b> inniṣṭafaituka 'alan-nāsi birisālātī wa bikalāmī fa khuż m<b>ā</b> ātaituka wa kum minasy-syākirīn
7|145|wa katabnā lahụ fil-alwāḥi ming kulli syai`im mau'iẓataw wa tafṣīlal likulli syaī`, fa khuż-hā biquwwatiw wa`mur qaumaka ya`khużụ bi`aḥsanihā, sa`urīkum dāral-fāsiqīn
7|146|sa aṣrifu 'an āyātiyallażīna yatakabbarụna fil-arḍi bigairil-ḥaqq, wa iy yarau kulla āyatil lā yu`minụ bihā, wa iy yarau sabīlar-rusydi lā yattakhiżụhu sabīlā, wa iy yarau sabīlal-gayyi yattakhiżụhu sabīlā, żālika bi`annahum każżabụ bi`āyātinā wa kānụ 'an-hā gāfilīn
7|147|wallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā wa liq<b>ā</b>`il-ākhirati ḥabiṭat a'māluhum, hal yujzauna illā mā kānụ ya'malụn
7|148|wattakhaża qaumu mụsā mim ba'dihī min ḥuliyyihim 'ijlan jasadal lahụ khuwār, a lam yarau annahụ lā yukallimuhum wa lā yahdīhim sabīlā, ittakhażụhu wa kānụ ẓālimīn
7|149|wa lammā suqiṭa f<b>ī</b> aidīhim wa ra`au annahum qad ḍallụ qālụ la`il lam yar-ḥamnā rabbunā wa yagfir lanā lanakụnanna minal-khāsirīn
7|150|wa lammā raja'a mụs<b>ā</b> ilā qaumihī gaḍbāna asifang qāla bi`samā khalaftumụnī mim ba'dī, a 'ajiltum amra rabbikum, wa alqal-alwāḥa wa akhaża bira`si akhīhi yajurruh<b>ū</b> ilaīh, qālabna umma innal-qaumastaḍ'afụnī wa kādụ yaqtulụnanī fa lā tusymit biyal-a'd<b>ā</b>`a wa lā taj'alnī ma'al qaumiẓ-ẓālimīn
7|151|qāla rabbigfir lī wa li`akhī wa adkhilnā fī raḥmatika wa anta ar-ḥamur-rāḥimīn
7|152|innallażīnattakhażul-'ijla sayanāluhum gaḍabum mir rabbihim wa żillatun fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā, wa każālika najzil-muftarīn
7|153|wallażīna 'amilus-sayyi`āti ṡumma tābụ mim ba'dihā wa āman<b>ū</b> inna rabbaka mim ba'dihā lagafụrur raḥīm
7|154|wa lammā sakata 'am mụsal-gaḍabu akhażal-alwāḥa wa fī nuskhatihā hudaw wa raḥmatul lillażīna hum lirabbihim yar-habụn
7|155|wakhtāra mụsā qaumahụ sab'īna rajulal limīqātinā, fa lamm<b>ā</b> akhażat-humur-rajfatu qāla rabbi lau syi`ta ahlaktahum ming qablu wa iyyāy, a tuhlikunā bimā fa'alas-sufah<b>ā</b>`u minnā, in hiya illā fitnatuk, tuḍillu bihā man tasy<b>ā</b>`u wa tahdī man tasy<b>ā</b>`, anta waliyyunā fagfir lanā war-ḥamnā wa anta khairul-gāfirīn
7|156|waktub lana fī hāżihid-dun-yā ḥasanataw wa fil-ākhirati innā hudn<b>ā</b> ilaīk, qāla 'ażāb<b>ī</b> uṣību bihī man asy<b>ā</b>`, wa raḥmatī wasi'at kulla syaī`, fa sa`aktubuhā lillażīna yattaqụna wa yu`tụnaz-zakāta wallażīna hum bi`āyātinā yu`minụn
7|157|allażīna yattabi'ụnar-rasụlan-nabiyyal-ummiyyallażī yajidụnahụ maktụban 'indahum fit-taurāti wal-injīli ya`muruhum bil-ma'rụfi wa yan-hāhum 'anil-mungkari wa yuḥillu lahumuṭ-ṭayyibāti wa yuḥarrimu 'alaihimul-khab<b>ā</b>`iṡa wa yaḍa'u 'an-hum iṣrahum wal-aglālallatī kānat 'alaihim, fallażīna āmanụ bihī wa 'azzarụhu wa naṣarụhu wattaba'un-nụrallaż<b>ī</b> unzila ma'ah<b>ū</b> ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-mufliḥụn
7|158|qul y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsu innī rasụlullāhi ilaikum jamī'anillażī lahụ mulkus-samāwāti wal-arḍ, l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huwa yuḥyī wa yumītu fa āminụ billāhi wa rasụlihin-nabiyyil-ummiyyillażī yu`minu billāhi wa kalimātihī wattabi'ụhu la'allakum tahtadụn
7|159|wa ming qaumi mụs<b>ā</b> ummatuy yahdụna bil-ḥaqqi wa bihī ya'dilụn
7|160|wa qaṭṭa'nāhumuṡnatai 'asyrata asbāṭan umamā, wa auḥain<b>ā</b> ilā mụs<b>ā</b> iżistasqāhu qaumuh<b>ū</b> aniḍrib bi'aṣākal-ḥajar, fambajasat min-huṡnatā 'asyrata 'ainā, qad 'alima kullu unāsim masyrabahum, wa ẓallalnā 'alaihimul-gamāma wa anzalnā 'alaihimul-manna was-salwā, kulụ min ṭayyibāti mā razaqnākum, wa mā ẓalamụnā wa lāking kān<b>ū</b> anfusahum yaẓlimụn
7|161|wa iż qīla lahumuskunụ hāżihil-qaryata wa kulụ min-hā ḥaiṡu syi`tum wa qụlụ hiṭṭatuw wadkhulul-bāba sujjadan nagfir lakum khaṭ<b>ī</b>`ātikum, sanazīdul-muḥsinīn
7|162|fa baddalallażīna ẓalamụ min-hum qaulan gairallażī qīla lahum fa arsalnā 'alaihim rijzam minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i bimā kānụ yaẓlimụn
7|163|was`al-hum 'anil-qaryatillatī kānat hāḍiratal-baḥr, iż ya'dụna fis-sabti iż ta`tīhim ḥītānuhum yauma sabtihim syurra'aw wa yauma lā yasbitụna lā ta`tīhim, każālika nablụhum bimā kānụ yafsuqụn
7|164|wa iż qālat ummatum min-hum lima ta'iẓụna qaumanillāhu muhlikuhum au mu'ażżibuhum 'ażāban syadīdā, qālụ ma'żiratan ilā rabbikum wa la'allahum yattaqụn
7|165|fa lammā nasụ mā żukkirụ bih<b>ī</b> anjainallażīna yan-hauna 'anis-s<b>ū</b>`i wa akhażnallażīna ẓalamụ bi'ażābim ba`īsim bimā kānụ yafsuqụn
7|166|fa lammā 'atau 'am mā nuhụ 'an-hu qulnā lahum kụnụ qiradatan khāsi`īn
7|167|wa iż ta`ażżana rabbuka layab'aṡanna 'alaihim ilā yaumil-qiyāmati may yasụmuhum s<b>ū</b>`al-'ażāb, inna rabbaka lasarī'ul-'iqābi wa innahụ lagafụrur raḥīm
7|168|wa qaṭṭa'nāhum fil-arḍi umamā, min-humuṣ-ṣāliḥụna wa min-hum dụna żālika wa balaunāhum bil-ḥasanāti was-sayyi`āti la'allahum yarji'ụn
7|169|fa khalafa mim ba'dihim khalfuw wariṡul-kitāba ya`khużụna 'araḍa hāżal-adnā wa yaqụlụna sayugfaru lanā, wa iy ya`tihim 'araḍum miṡluhụ ya`khużụh, a lam yu`khaż 'alaihim mīṡāqul-kitābi al lā yaqụlụ 'alallāhi illal-ḥaqqa wa darasụ mā fīh, wad-dārul-ākhiratu khairul lillażīna yattaqụn, a fa lā ta'qilụn
7|170|wallażīna yumassikụna bil-kitābi wa aqāmuṣ-ṣalāh, innā lā nuḍī'u ajral-muṣliḥīn
7|171|wa iż nataqnal-jabala fauqahum ka`annahụ ẓullatuw wa ẓann<b>ū</b> annahụ wāqi'um bihim, khużụ m<b>ā</b> ātainākum biquwwatiw ważkurụ mā fīhi la'allakum tattaqụn
7|172|wa iż akhaża rabbuka mim ban<b>ī</b> ādama min ẓuhụrihim żurriyyatahum wa asy-hadahum 'al<b>ā</b> anfusihim, a lastu birabbikum, qālụ balā syahidnā, an taqụlụ yaumal-qiyāmati innā kunnā 'an hāżā gāfilīn
7|173|au taqụl<b>ū</b> innam<b>ā</b> asyraka āb<b>ā</b>`unā ming qablu wa kunnā żurriyyatam mim ba'dihim, a fa tuhlikunā bimā fa'alal-mubṭilụn
7|174|wa każālika nufaṣṣilul-āyāti wa la'allahum yarji'ụn
7|175|watlu 'alaihim naba`allaż<b>ī</b> ātaināhu āyātinā fansalakha min-hā fa atba'ahusy-syaiṭānu fa kāna minal-gāwīn
7|176|walau syi`nā larafa'nāhu bihā wa lākinnah<b>ū</b> akhlada ilal-arḍi wattaba'a hawāh, fa maṡaluhụ kamaṡalil-kalb, in taḥmil 'alaihi yal-haṡ au tatruk-hu yal-haṡ, żālika maṡalul-qaumillażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā, faqṣuṣil-qaṣaṣa la'allahum yatafakkarụn
7|177|s<b>ā</b>`a maṡalanil-qaumullażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā wa anfusahum kānụ yaẓlimụn
7|178|may yahdillāhu fa huwal-muhtadī, wa may yuḍlil fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-khāsirụn
7|179|wa laqad żara`nā lijahannama kaṡīram minal-jinni wal-insi lahum qulụbul lā yafqahụna bihā wa lahum a'yunul lā yubṣirụna bihā wa lahum āżānul lā yasma'ụna bihā, ul<b>ā</b>`ika kal-an'āmi bal hum aḍall, ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-gāfilụn
7|180|wa lillāhil-asm<b>ā</b>`ul-ḥusnā fad'ụhu bihā wa żarullażīna yul-ḥidụna f<b>ī</b> asm<b>ā</b>`ih, sayujzauna mā kānụ ya'malụn
7|181|wa mim man khalaqn<b>ā</b> ummatuy yahdụna bil-ḥaqqi wa bihī ya'dilụn
7|182|wallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā sanastadrijuhum min ḥaiṡu lā ya'lamụn
7|183|wa umlī lahum, inna kaidī matīn
7|184|a wa lam yatafakkarụ mā biṣāḥibihim min jinnah, in huwa illā nażīrum mubīn
7|185|a wa lam yanẓurụ fī malakụtis-samāwāti wal-arḍi wa mā khalaqallāhu min syai`iw wa an 'as<b>ā</b> ay yakụna qadiqtaraba ajaluhum fa bi`ayyi ḥadīṡim ba'dahụ yu`minụn
7|186|may yuḍlilillāhu fa lā hādiya lahụ wa yażaruhum fī ṭugyānihim ya'mahụn
7|187|yas`alụnaka 'anis-sā'ati ayyāna mursāhā, qul innamā 'ilmuhā 'inda rabbī, lā yujallīhā liwaqtih<b>ā</b> illā huw, ṡaqulat fis-samāwāti wal-arḍ, lā ta`tīkum illā bagtah, yas`alụnaka ka`annaka ḥafiyyun 'an-hā, qul innamā 'ilmuhā 'indallāhi wa lākinna akṡaran-nāsi lā ya'lamụn
7|188|qul l<b>ā</b> amliku linafsī naf'aw wa lā ḍarran illā mā sy<b>ā</b>`allāh, walau kuntu a'lamul-gaiba lastakṡartu minal-khaīr, wa mā massaniyas-s<b>ū</b>`u in ana illā nażīruw wa basyīrul liqaumiy yu`minụn
7|189|huwallażī khalaqakum min nafsiw wāḥidatiw wa ja'ala min-hā zaujahā liyaskuna ilaihā, fa lammā tagasysyāhā ḥamalat ḥamlan khafīfan fa marrat bih, fa lamm<b>ā</b> aṡqalad da'awallāha rabbahumā la`in ātaitanā ṣāliḥal lanakụnanna minasy-syākirīn
7|190|fa lamm<b>ā</b> ātāhumā ṣāliḥan ja'alā lahụ syurak<b>ā</b>`a fīm<b>ā</b> ātāhumā, fa ta'ālallāhu 'ammā yusyrikụn
7|191|a yusyrikụna mā lā yakhluqu syai`aw wa hum yukhlaqụn
7|192|wa lā yastaṭī'ụna lahum naṣraw wa l<b>ā</b> anfusahum yanṣurụn
7|193|wa in tad'ụhum ilal-hudā lā yattabi'ụkum, saw<b>ā</b>`un 'alaikum a da'autumụhum am antum ṣāmitụn
7|194|innallażīna tad'ụna min dụnillāhi 'ibādun amṡālukum fad'ụhum falyastajībụ lakum ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
7|195|a lahum arjuluy yamsyụna bih<b>ā</b> am lahum aidiy yabṭisyụna bih<b>ā</b> am lahum a'yunuy yubṣirụna bih<b>ā</b> am lahum āżānuy yasma'ụna bihā, qulid'ụ syurak<b>ā</b>`akum ṡumma kīdụni fa lā tunẓirụn
7|196|inna waliyyiyallāhullażī nazzalal-kitāba wa huwa yatawallaṣ-ṣāliḥīn
7|197|wallażīna tad'ụna min dụnihī lā yastaṭī'ụna naṣrakum wa l<b>ā</b> anfusahum yanṣurụn
7|198|wa in tad'ụhum ilal-hudā lā yasma'ụ, wa tarāhum yanẓurụna ilaika wa hum lā yubṣirụn
7|199|khużil-'afwa wa`mur bil-'urfi wa a'riḍ 'anil-jāhilīn
7|200|wa immā yanzagannaka minasy-syaiṭāni nazgun fasta'iż billāh, innahụ samī'un 'alīm
7|201|innallażīnattaqau iżā massahum ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifum minasy-syaiṭāni tażakkarụ fa iżā hum mubṣirụn
7|202|wa ikhwānuhum yamuddụnahum fil-gayyi ṡumma lā yuqṣirụn
7|203|wa iżā lam ta`tihim bi`āyating qālụ lau lajtabaitahā, qul innam<b>ā</b> attabi'u mā yụḥ<b>ā</b> ilayya mir rabbī, hāżā baṣ<b>ā</b>`iru mir rabbikum wa hudaw wa raḥmatul liqaumiy yu`minụn
7|204|wa iżā quri`al-qur`ānu fastami'ụ lahụ wa anṣitụ la'allakum tur-ḥamụn
7|205|ważkur rabbaka fī nafsika taḍarru'aw wa khīfataw wa dụnal-jahri minal-qauli bil-guduwwi wal-āṣāli wa lā takum minal-gāfilīn
7|206|innallażīna 'inda rabbika lā yastakbirụna 'an 'ibādatihī wa yusabbiḥụnahụ wa lahụ yasjudụn
8|1|yas`alụnaka 'anil-anfāl, qulil-anfālu lillāhi war-rasụl, fattaqullāha wa aṣliḥụ żāta bainikum wa aṭī'ullāha wa rasụlah<b>ū</b> ing kuntum mu`minīn
8|2|innamal-mu`minụnallażīna iżā żukirallāhu wajilat qulụbuhum wa iżā tuliyat 'alaihim āyātuhụ zādat-hum īmānaw wa 'alā rabbihim yatawakkalụn
8|3|allażīna yuqīmụnaṣ-ṣalāta wa mimmā razaqnāhum yunfiqụn
8|4|ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-mu`minụna ḥaqqā, lahum darajātun 'inda rabbihim wa magfiratuw wa rizqung karīm
8|5|kam<b>ā</b> akhrajaka rabbuka mim baitika bil-ḥaqqi wa inna farīqam minal-mu`minīna lakārihụn
8|6|yujādilụnaka fil-ḥaqqi ba'da mā tabayyana ka`annamā yusāqụna ilal-mauti wa hum yanẓurụn
8|7|wa iż ya'idukumullāhu iḥdaṭ-ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifataini annahā lakum wa tawaddụna anna gaira żātisy-syaukati takụnu lakum wa yurīdullāhu ay yuḥiqqal-ḥaqqa bikalimātihī wa yaqṭa'a dābiral-kāfirīn
8|8|liyuḥiqqal-ḥaqqa wa yubṭilal-bāṭila walau karihal-mujrimụn
8|9|iż tastagīṡụna rabbakum fastajāba lakum annī mumiddukum bi`alfim minal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati murdifīn
8|10|wa mā ja'alahullāhu illā busyrā wa litaṭma`inna bihī qulụbukum, wa man-naṣru illā min 'indillāh, innallāha 'azīzun ḥakīm
8|11|iż yugasysyīkumun-nu'āsa amanatam min-hu wa yunazzilu 'alaikum minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i m<b>ā</b>`al liyuṭahhirakum bihī wa yuż-hiba 'angkum rijzasy-syaiṭāni wa liyarbiṭa 'alā qulụbikum wa yuṡabbita bihil-aqdām
8|12|iż yụḥī rabbuka ilal-mal<b>ā</b>`ikati annī ma'akum fa ṡabbitullażīna āmanụ, sa`ulqī fī qulụbillażīna kafarur-ru'ba faḍribụ fauqal-a'nāqi waḍribụ min-hum kulla banān
8|13|żālika bi`annahum sy<b>ā</b>qqullāha wa rasụlah, wa may yusyāqiqillāha wa rasụlahụ fa innallāha syadīdul-'iqāb
8|14|żālikum fa żụqụhu wa anna lil-kāfirīna 'ażāban-nār
8|15|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> iżā laqītumullażīna kafarụ zaḥfan fa lā tuwallụhumul-adbār
8|16|wa may yuwallihim yauma`iżin duburah<b>ū</b> illā mutaḥarrifal liqitālin au mutaḥayyizan ilā fi`atin fa qad b<b>ā</b>`a bigaḍabim minallāhi wa ma`wāhu jahannam, wa bi`sal-maṣīr
8|17|fa lam taqtulụhum wa lākinnallāha qatalahum wa mā ramaita iż ramaita wa lākinnallāha ramā, wa liyubliyal-mu`minīna min-hu bal<b>ā</b>`an ḥasanā, innallāha samī'un 'alīm
8|18|żālikum wa annallāha mụhinu kaidil-kāfirīn
8|19|in tastaftiḥụ fa qad j<b>ā</b>`akumul-fat-ḥ, wa in tantahụ fa huwa khairul lakum, wa in ta'ụdụ na'ud, wa lan tugniya 'angkum fi`atukum syai`aw walau kaṡurat wa annallāha ma'al-mu`minīn
8|20|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> aṭī'ullāha wa rasụlahụ wa lā tawallau 'an-hu wa antum tasma'ụn
8|21|wa lā takụnụ kallażīna qālụ sami'nā wa hum lā yasma'ụn
8|22|inna syarrad-daw<b>ā</b>bbi 'indallāhiṣ-ṣummul-bukmullażīna lā ya'qilụn
8|23|walau 'alimallāhu fīhim khairal la`asma'ahum, walau asma'ahum latawallaw wa hum mu'riḍụn
8|24|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanustajībụ lillāhi wa lir-rasụli iżā da'ākum limā yuḥyīkum, wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha yaḥụlu bainal-mar`i wa qalbihī wa annah<b>ū</b> ilaihi tuḥsyarụn
8|25|wattaqụ fitnatal lā tuṣībannallażīna ẓalamụ mingkum kh<b>ā</b>ṣṣah, wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha syadīdul-'iqāb
8|26|ważkur<b>ū</b> iż antum qalīlum mustaḍ'afụna fil-arḍi takhāfụna ay yatakhaṭṭafakumun-nāsu fa āwākum wa ayyadakum binaṣrihī wa razaqakum minaṭ-ṭayyibāti la'allakum tasykurụn
8|27|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ lā takhụnullāha war-rasụla wa takhụn<b>ū</b> amānātikum wa antum ta'lamụn
8|28|wa'lam<b>ū</b> annam<b>ā</b> amwālukum wa aulādukum fitnatuw wa annallāha 'indah<b>ū</b> ajrun 'aẓīm
8|29|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> in tattaqullāha yaj'al lakum furqānaw wa yukaffir 'angkum sayyi`ātikum wa yagfir lakum, wallāhu żul-faḍlil-'aẓīm
8|30|wa iż yamkuru bikallażīna kafarụ liyuṡbitụka au yaqtulụka au yukhrijụk, wa yamkurụna wa yamkurullāh, wallāhu khairul-mākirīn
8|31|wa iżā tutlā 'alaihim āyātunā qālụ qad sami'nā lau nasy<b>ā</b>`u laqulnā miṡla hāż<b>ā</b> in hāż<b>ā</b> ill<b>ā</b> asāṭīrul-awwalīn
8|32|wa iż qālullāhumma ing kāna hāżā huwal-ḥaqqa min 'indika fa amṭir 'alainā ḥijāratam minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i awi`tinā bi'ażābin alīm
8|33|wa mā kānallāhu liyu'ażżibahum wa anta fīhim, wa mā kānallāhu mu'ażżibahum wa hum yastagfirụn
8|34|wa mā lahum allā yu'ażżibahumullāhu wa hum yaṣuddụna 'anil-masjidil-ḥarāmi wa mā kān<b>ū</b> auliy<b>ā</b>`ah, in auliy<b>ā</b>`uh<b>ū</b> illal-muttaqụna wa lākinna akṡarahum lā ya'lamụn
8|35|wa mā kāna ṣalātuhum 'indal-baiti illā muk<b>ā</b>`aw wa taṣdiyah, fa żụqul-'ażāba bimā kuntum takfurụn
8|36|innallażīna kafarụ yunfiqụna amwālahum liyaṣuddụ 'an sabīlillāh, fa sayunfiqụnahā ṡumma takụnu 'alaihim ḥasratan ṡumma yuglabụn, wallażīna kafar<b>ū</b> ilā jahannama yuḥsyarụn
8|37|liyamīzallāhul-khabīṡa minaṭ-ṭayyibi wa yaj'alal-khabīṡa ba'ḍahụ 'alā ba'ḍin fa yarkumahụ jamī'an fa yaj'alahụ fī jahannam, ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-khāsirụn
8|38|qul lillażīna kafar<b>ū</b> iy yantahụ yugfar lahum mā qad salaf, wa iy ya'ụdụ fa qad maḍat sunnatul-awwalīn
8|39|wa qātilụhum ḥattā lā takụna fitnatuw wa yakụnad-dīnu kulluhụ lillāh, fa inintahau fa innallāha bimā ya'malụna baṣīr
8|40|wa in tawallau fa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha maulākum, ni'mal-maulā wa ni'man-naṣīr
8|41|wa'lam<b>ū</b> annamā ganimtum min syai`in fa anna lillāhi khumusahụ wa lir-rasụli wa liżil-qurbā wal-yatāmā wal-masākīni wabnis-sabīli ing kuntum āmantum billāhi wa m<b>ā</b> anzalnā 'alā 'abdinā yaumal-furqāni yaumaltaqal jam'ān, wallāhu 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
8|42|iż antum bil-'udwatid-dun-yā wa hum bil-'udwatil-quṣwā war-rakbu asfala mingkum, walau tawā'attum lakhtalaftum fil-mī'ādi wa lākil liyaqḍiyallāhu amrang kāna maf'ụlal liyahlika man halaka 'am bayyinatiw wa yaḥyā man ḥayya 'am bayyinah, wa innallāha lasamī'un 'alīm
8|43|iż yurīkahumullāhu fī manāmika qalīlā, walau arākahum kaṡīral lafasyiltum wa latanāza'tum fil-amri wa lākinnallāha sallam, innahụ 'alīmum biżātiṣ-ṣudụr
8|44|wa iż yurīkumụhum iżiltaqaitum f<b>ī</b> a'yunikum qalīlaw wa yuqallilukum f<b>ī</b> a'yunihim liyaqḍiyallāhu amrang kāna maf'ụlā, wa ilallāhi turja'ul-umụr
8|45|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> iżā laqītum fi`atan faṡbutụ ważkurullāha kaṡīral la'allakum tufliḥụn
8|46|wa aṭī'ullāha wa rasụlahụ wa lā tanāza'ụ fa tafsyalụ wa taż-haba rīḥukum waṣbirụ, innallāha ma'aṣ-ṣābirīn
8|47|wa lā takụnụ kallażīna kharajụ min diyārihim baṭaraw wa ri`<b>ā</b>`an-nāsi wa yaṣuddụna 'an sabīlillāh, wallāhu bimā ya'malụna muḥīṭ
8|48|wa iż zayyana lahumusy-syaiṭānu a'mālahum wa qāla lā gāliba lakumul-yauma minan-nāsi wa innī jārul lakum, fa lammā tar<b>ā</b>`atil-fi`atāni nakaṣa 'alā 'aqibaihi wa qāla innī bar<b>ī</b>`um mingkum inn<b>ī</b> arā mā lā tarauna inn<b>ī</b> akhāfullāh, wallāhu syadīdul-'iqāb
8|49|iż yaqụlul-munāfiqụna wallażīna fī qulụbihim maraḍun garra h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`i dīnuhum, wa may yatawakkal 'alallāhi fa innallāha 'azīzun ḥakīm
8|50|walau tar<b>ā</b> iż yatawaffallażīna kafarul-mal<b>ā</b>`ikatu yaḍribụna wujụhahum wa adbārahum, wa żụqụ 'ażābal-ḥarīq
8|51|żālika bimā qaddamat aidīkum wa annallāha laisa biẓallāmil lil-'abīd
8|52|kada`bi āli fir'auna wallażīna ming qablihim, kafarụ bi`āyātillāhi fa akhażahumullāhu biżunụbihim, innallāha qawiyyun syadīdul-'iqāb
8|53|żālika bi`annallāha lam yaku mugayyiran ni'matan an'amahā 'alā qaumin ḥattā yugayyirụ mā bi`anfusihim wa annallāha samī'un 'alīm
8|54|kada`bi āli fir'auna wallażīna ming qablihim, każżabụ bi`āyāti rabbihim fa ahlaknāhum biżunụbihim wa agraqn<b>ā</b> āla fir'aụn, wa kullung kānụ ẓālimīn
8|55|inna syarrad-daw<b>ā</b>bbi 'indallāhillażīna kafarụ fa hum lā yu`minụn
8|56|allażīna 'āhatta min-hum ṡumma yangquḍụna 'ahdahum fī kulli marratiw wa hum lā yattaqụn
8|57|fa immā taṡqafannahum fil-ḥarbi fa syarrid bihim man khalfahum la'allahum yażżakkarụn
8|58|wa immā takhāfanna ming qaumin khiyānatan fambiż ilaihim 'alā saw<b>ā</b>`, innallāha lā yuḥibbul-kh<b>ā</b>`inīn
8|59|wa lā yaḥsabannallażīna kafarụ sabaqụ, innahum lā yu'jizụn
8|60|wa a'iddụ lahum mastaṭa'tum ming quwwatiw wa mir ribāṭil-khaili tur-hibụna bihī 'aduwwallāhi wa 'aduwwakum wa ākharīna min dụnihim, lā ta'lamụnahum, allāhu ya'lamuhum, wa mā tunfiqụ min syai`in fī sabīlillāhi yuwaffa ilaikum wa antum lā tuẓlamụn
8|61|wa in janaḥụ lis-salmi fajnaḥ lahā wa tawakkal 'alallāh, innahụ huwas-samī'ul-'alīm
8|62|wa iy yurīd<b>ū</b> ay yakhda'ụka fa inna ḥasbakallāh, huwallaż<b>ī</b> ayyadaka binaṣrihī wa bil-mu`minīn
8|63|wa allafa baina qulụbihim, lau anfaqta mā fil-arḍi jamī'am m<b>ā</b> allafta baina qulụbihim wa lākinnallāha allafa bainahum, innahụ 'azīzun ḥakīm
8|64|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nabiyyu ḥasbukallāhu wa manittaba'aka minal-mu`minīn
8|65|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nabiyyu ḥarriḍil-mu`minīna 'alal-qitāl, iy yakum mingkum 'isyrụna ṣābirụna yaglibụ mi`ataīn, wa iy yakum mingkum mi`atuy yaglib<b>ū</b> alfam minallażīna kafarụ bi`annahum qaumul lā yafqahụn
8|66|al-āna khaffafallāhu 'angkum wa 'alima anna fīkum ḍa'fā, fa iy yakum mingkum mi`atun ṣābiratuy yaglibụ mi`ataīn, wa iy yakum mingkum alfuy yaglib<b>ū</b> alfaini bi`iżnillāh, wallāhu ma'aṣ-ṣābirīn
8|67|mā kāna linabiyyin ay yakụna lah<b>ū</b> asrā ḥattā yuṡkhina fil-arḍ, turīdụna 'araḍad-dun-yā wallāhu yurīdul-ākhirah, wallāhu 'azīzun ḥakīm
8|68|lau lā kitābum minallāhi sabaqa lamassakum fīm<b>ā</b> akhażtum 'ażābun 'aẓīm
8|69|fa kulụ mimmā ganimtum ḥalālan ṭayyibaw wattaqullāh, innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
8|70|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nabiyyu qul liman f<b>ī</b> aidīkum minal-asr<b>ā</b> iy ya'lamillāhu fī qulụbikum khairay yu`tikum khairam mimm<b>ā</b> ukhiża mingkum wa yagfir lakum, wallāhu gafụrur raḥīm
8|71|wa iy yurīdụ khiyānataka fa qad khānullāha ming qablu fa amkana min-hum wallāhu 'alīmun ḥakīm
8|72|innallażīna āmanụ wa hājarụ wa jāhadụ bi`amwālihim wa anfusihim fī sabīlillāhi wallażīna āwaw wa naṣar<b>ū</b> ul<b>ā</b>`ika ba'ḍuhum auliy<b>ā</b>`u ba'ḍ, wallażīna āmanụ wa lam yuhājirụ mā lakum miw walāyatihim min syai`in ḥattā yuhājirụ, wa inistanṣarụkum fid-dīni fa 'alaikumun-naṣru illā 'alā qaumim bainakum wa bainahum mīṡāq, wallāhu bimā ta'malụna baṣīr
8|73|wallażīna kafarụ ba'ḍuhum auliy<b>ā</b>`u ba'ḍ, illā taf'alụhu takun fitnatun fil-arḍi wa fasādung kabīr
8|74|wallażīna āmanụ wa hājarụ wa jāhadụ fī sabīlillāhi wallażīna āwaw wa naṣar<b>ū</b> ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-mu`minụna ḥaqqā, lahum magfiratuw wa rizqung karīm
8|75|wallażīna āmanụ mim ba'du wa hājarụ wa jāhadụ ma'akum fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika mingkum, wa ulul-ar-ḥāmi ba'ḍuhum aulā biba'ḍin fī kitābillāh, innallāha bikulli syai`in 'alīm
9|1|bar<b>ā</b>`atum minallāhi wa rasụlih<b>ī</b> ilallażīna 'āhattum minal-musyrikīn
9|2|fa sīḥụ fil-arḍi arba'ata asy-huriw wa'lam<b>ū</b> annakum gairu mu'jizillāhi wa annallāha mukhzil-kāfirīn
9|3|wa ażānum minallāhi wa rasụlih<b>ī</b> ilan-nāsi yaumal-ḥajjil-akbari annallāha bar<b>ī</b>`um minal-musyrikīna wa rasụluh, fa in tubtum fa huwa khairul lakum, wa in tawallaitum fa'lam<b>ū</b> annakum gairu mu'jizillāh, wa basysyirillażīna kafarụ bi'ażābin alīm
9|4|illallażīna 'āhattum minal-musyrikīna ṡumma lam yangquṣụkum syai`aw wa lam yuẓāhirụ 'alaikum aḥadan fa atimm<b>ū</b> ilaihim 'ahdahum ilā muddatihim, innallāha yuḥibbul muttaqīn
9|5|fa iżansalakhal-asy-hurul-ḥurumu faqtulul-musyrikīna ḥaiṡu wajattumụhum wa khużụhum waḥṣurụhum waq'udụ lahum kulla marṣad, fa in tābụ wa aqāmuṣ-ṣalāta wa ātawuz-zakāta fa khallụ sabīlahum, innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
9|6|wa in aḥadum minal-musyrikīnastajāraka fa ajir-hu ḥattā yasma'a kalāmallāhi ṡumma ablig-hu ma`manah, żālika bi`annahum qaumul lā ya'lamụn
9|7|kaifa yakụnu lil-musyrikīna 'ahdun 'indallāhi wa 'inda rasụlih<b>ī</b> illallażīna 'āhattum 'indal-masjidil-ḥarām, famastaqāmụ lakum fastaqīmụ lahum, innallāha yuḥibbul-muttaqīn
9|8|kaifa wa iy yaẓ-harụ 'alaikum lā yarqubụ fīkum illaw wa lā żimmah, yurḍụnakum bi`afwāhihim wa ta`bā qulụbuhum, wa akṡaruhum fāsiqụn
9|9|isytarau bi`āyātillāhi ṡamanang qalīlan fa ṣaddụ 'an sabīlih, innahum s<b>ā</b>`a mā kānụ ya'malụn
9|10|lā yarqubụna fī mu`minin illaw wa lā żimmah, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-mu'tadụn
9|11|fa in tābụ wa aqāmuṣ-ṣalāta wa ātawuz-zakāta fa ikhwānukum fid-dīn, wa nufaṣṣilul-āyāti liqaumiy ya'lamụn
9|12|wa in nakaṡ<b>ū</b> aimānahum mim ba'di 'ahdihim wa ṭa'anụ fī dīnikum fa qātil<b>ū</b> a`immatal-kufri innahum l<b>ā</b> aimāna lahum la'allahum yantahụn
9|13|alā tuqātilụna qauman nakaṡ<b>ū</b> aimānahum wa hammụ bi`ikhrājir-rasụli wa hum bada`ụkum awwala marrah, a takhsyaunahum, fallāhu aḥaqqu an takhsyauhu ing kuntum mu`minīn
9|14|qātilụhum yu'ażżib-humullāhu bi`aidīkum wa yukhzihim wa yanṣurkum 'alaihim wa yasyfi ṣudụra qaumim mu`minīn
9|15|wa yuż-hib gaiẓa qulụbihim, wa yatụbullāhu 'alā may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu 'alīmun ḥakīm
9|16|am ḥasibtum an tutrakụ wa lammā ya'lamillāhullażīna jāhadụ mingkum wa lam yattakhiżụ min dụnillāhi wa lā rasụlihī wa lal-mu`minīna walījah, wallāhu khabīrum bimā ta'malụn
9|17|mā kāna lil-musyrikīna ay ya'murụ masājidallāhi syāhidīna 'al<b>ā</b> anfusihim bil-kufr, ul<b>ā</b>`ika ḥabiṭat a'māluhum, wa fin-nāri hum khālidụn
9|18|innamā ya'muru masājidallāhi man āmana billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri wa aqāmaṣ-ṣalāta wa ātaz-zakāta wa lam yakhsya illallāh, fa 'as<b>ā</b> ul<b>ā</b>`ika ay yakụnụ minal-muhtadīn
9|19|a ja'altum siqāyatal-ḥ<b>ā</b>jji wa 'imāratal-masjidil-ḥarāmi kaman āmana billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri wa jāhada fī sabīlillāh, lā yastawụna 'indallāh, wallāhu lā yahdil-qaumaẓ-ẓālimīn
9|20|allażīna āmanụ wa hājarụ wa jāhadụ fī sabīlillāhi bi`amwālihim wa anfusihim a'ẓamu darajatan 'indallāh, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-f<b>ā</b>`izụn
9|21|yubasysyiruhum rabbuhum biraḥmatim min-hu wa riḍwāniw wa jannātil lahum fīhā na'īmum muqīm
9|22|khālidīna fīh<b>ā</b> abadā, innallāha 'indah<b>ū</b> ajrun 'aẓīm
9|23|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ lā tattakhiż<b>ū</b> āb<b>ā</b>`akum wa ikhwānakum auliy<b>ā</b>`a inistaḥabbul-kufra 'alal-īmān, wa may yatawallahum mingkum fa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humuẓ-ẓālimụn
9|24|qul ing kāna āb<b>ā</b>`ukum wa abn<b>ā</b>`ukum wa ikhwānukum wa azwājukum wa 'asyīratukum wa amwāluniqtaraftumụhā wa tijāratun takhsyauna kasādahā wa masākinu tarḍaunah<b>ā</b> aḥabba ilaikum minallāhi wa rasụlihī wa jihādin fī sabīlihī fa tarabbaṣụ ḥattā ya`tiyallāhu bi`amrih, wallāhu lā yahdil-qaumal-fāsiqīn
9|25|laqad naṣarakumullāhu fī mawāṭina kaṡīratiw wa yauma ḥunainin iż a'jabatkum kaṡratukum fa lam tugni 'angkum syai`aw wa ḍāqat 'alaikumul-arḍu bimā raḥubat ṡumma wallaitum mudbirīn
9|26|ṡumma anzalallāhu sakīnatahụ 'alā rasụlihī wa 'alal-mu`minīna wa anzala junụdal lam tarauhā wa 'ażżaballażīna kafarụ, wa żālika jaz<b>ā</b>`ul-kāfirīn
9|27|ṡumma yatụbullāhu mim ba'di żālika 'alā may yasy<b>ā</b>`, wallāhu gafụrur raḥīm
9|28|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> innamal-musyrikụna najasun fa lā yaqrabul-masjidal-ḥarāma ba'da 'āmihim hāżā, wa in khiftum 'ailatan fa saufa yugnīkumullāhu min faḍlih<b>ī</b> in sy<b>ā</b>`, innallāha 'alīmun ḥakīm
9|29|qātilullażīna lā yu`minụna billāhi wa lā bil-yaumil-ākhiri wa lā yuḥarrimụna mā ḥarramallāhu wa rasụluhụ wa lā yadīnụna dīnal-ḥaqqi minallażīna ụtul-kitāba ḥattā yu'ṭul-jizyata 'ay yadiw wa hum ṣāgirụn
9|30|wa qālatil-yahụdu 'uzairunibnullāhi wa qālatin-naṣāral-masīḥubnullāh, żālika qauluhum bi`afwāhihim, yuḍāhi`ụna qaulallażīna kafarụ ming qabl, qātalahumullāh, annā yu`fakụn
9|31|ittakhaż<b>ū</b> aḥbārahum wa ruhbānahum arbābam min dụnillāhi wal-masīḥabna maryam, wa m<b>ā</b> umir<b>ū</b> illā liya'bud<b>ū</b> ilāhaw wāḥidā, l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huw, sub-ḥānahụ 'ammā yusyrikụn
9|32|yurīdụna ay yuṭfi`ụ nụrallāhi bi`afwāhihim wa ya`ballāhu ill<b>ā</b> ay yutimma nụrahụ walau karihal-kāfirụn
9|33|huwallaż<b>ī</b> arsala rasụlahụ bil-hudā wa dīnil-ḥaqqi liyuẓ-hirahụ 'alad-dīni kullihī walau karihal-musyrikụn
9|34|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āman<b>ū</b> inna kaṡīram minal-aḥbāri war-ruhbāni laya`kulụna amwālan-nāsi bil-bāṭili wa yaṣuddụna 'an sabīlillāh, wallażīna yaknizụnaż-żahaba wal-fiḍḍata wa lā yunfiqụnahā fī sabīlillāhi fa basysyir-hum bi'ażābin alīm
9|35|yauma yuḥmā 'alaihā fī nāri jahannama fa tukwā bihā jibāhuhum wa junụbuhum wa ẓuhụruhum, hāżā mā kanaztum li`anfusikum fa żụqụ mā kuntum taknizụn
9|36|inna 'iddatasy-syuhụri 'indallāhiṡnā 'asyara syahran fī kitābillāhi yauma khalaqas-samāwāti wal-arḍa min-h<b>ā</b> arba'atun ḥurum, żālikad-dīnul-qayyimu fa lā taẓlimụ fīhinna anfusakum wa qātilul-musyrikīna k<b>ā</b>ffatang kamā yuqātilụnakum k<b>ā</b>ffah, wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha ma'al-muttaqīn
9|37|innaman-nas<b>ī</b>`u ziyādatun fil-kufri yuḍallu bihillażīna kafarụ yuḥillụnahụ 'āmaw wa yuḥarrimụnahụ 'āmal liyuwāṭi`ụ 'iddata mā ḥarramallāhu fa yuḥillụ mā ḥarramallāh, zuyyina lahum s<b>ū</b>`u a'mālihim, wallāhu lā yahdil-qaumal-kāfirīn
9|38|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ mā lakum iżā qīla lakumunfirụ fī sabīlillāhiṡ ṡāqaltum ilal-arḍ, a raḍītum bil-ḥayātid-dun-yā minal-ākhirah, fa mā matā'ul-ḥayātid-dun-yā fil-ākhirati illā qalīl
9|39|illā tanfirụ yu'ażżibkum 'ażāban alīmaw wa yastabdil qauman gairakum wa lā taḍurrụhu syai`ā, wallāhu 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
9|40|illā tanṣurụhu fa qad naṣarahullāhu iż akhrajahullażīna kafarụ ṡāniyaṡnaini iż humā fil-gāri iż yaqụlu liṣāḥibihī lā taḥzan innallāha ma'anā, fa anzalallāhu sakīnatahụ 'alaihi wa ayyadahụ bijunụdil lam tarauhā wa ja'ala kalimatallażīna kafarus-suflā, wa kalimatullāhi hiyal-'ulyā, wallāhu 'azīzun ḥakīm
9|41|infirụ khifāfaw wa ṡiqālaw wa jāhidụ bi`amwālikum wa anfusikum fī sabīlillāh, żālikum khairul lakum ing kuntum ta'lamụn
9|42|lau kāna 'araḍang qarībaw wa safarang qāṣidal lattaba'ụka wa lākim ba'udat 'alaihimusy-syuqqah, wa sayaḥlifụna billāhi lawistaṭa'nā lakharajnā ma'akum, yuhlikụna anfusahum, wallāhu ya'lamu innahum lakāżibụn
9|43|'afallāhu 'angk, lima ażinta lahum ḥattā yatabayyana lakallażīna ṣadaqụ wa ta'lamal-kāżibīn
9|44|lā yasta`żinukallażīna yu`minụna billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri ay yujāhidụ bi`amwālihim wa anfusihim, wallāhu 'alīmum bil-muttaqīn
9|45|innamā yasta`żinukallażīna lā yu`minụna billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri wartābat qulụbuhum fa hum fī raibihim yataraddadụn
9|46|walau arādul-khurụja la`a'addụ lahụ 'uddataw wa lāking karihallāhumbi'āṡahum fa ṡabbaṭahum wa qīlaq'udụ ma'al-qā'idīn
9|47|lau kharajụ fīkum mā zādụkum illā khabālaw wa la`auḍa'ụ khilālakum yabgụnakumul-fitnah, wa fīkum sammā'ụna lahum, wallāhu 'alīmum biẓ-ẓālimīn
9|48|laqadibtagawul-fitnata ming qablu wa qallabụ lakal-umụra ḥattā j<b>ā</b>`al-ḥaqqu wa ẓahara amrullāhi wa hum kārihụn
9|49|wa min-hum may yaqụlu`żal lī wa lā taftinnī, alā fil-fitnati saqaṭụ, wa inna jahannama lamuḥīṭatum bil-kāfirīn
9|50|in tuṣibka ḥasanatun tasu`hum, wa in tuṣibka muṣībatuy yaqụlụ qad akhażn<b>ā</b> amranā ming qablu wa yatawallaw wa hum fariḥụn
9|51|qul lay yuṣīban<b>ā</b> illā mā kataballāhu lanā, huwa maulānā wa 'alallāhi falyatawakkalil-mu`minụn
9|52|qul hal tarabbaṣụna bin<b>ā</b> ill<b>ā</b> iḥdal-ḥusnayaīn, wa naḥnu natarabbaṣu bikum ay yuṣībakumullāhu bi'ażābim min 'indih<b>ī</b> au bi`aidīnā fa tarabbaṣ<b>ū</b> innā ma'akum mutarabbiṣụn
9|53|qul anfiqụ ṭau'an au kar-hal lay yutaqabbala mingkum, innakum kuntum qauman fāsiqīn
9|54|wa mā mana'ahum an tuqbala min-hum nafaqātuhum ill<b>ā</b> annahum kafarụ billāhi wa birasụlihī wa lā ya`tụnaṣ-ṣalāta illā wa hum kusālā wa lā yunfiqụna illā wa hum kārihụn
9|55|fa lā tu'jibka amwāluhum wa l<b>ā</b> aulāduhum, innamā yurīdullāhu liyu'ażżibahum bihā fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā wa taz-haqa anfusuhum wa hum kāfirụn
9|56|wa yaḥlifụna billāhi innahum lamingkum, wa mā hum mingkum wa lākinnahum qaumuy yafraqụn
9|57|lau yajidụna malja`an au magārātin au muddakhalal lawallau ilaihi wa hum yajmaḥụn
9|58|wa min-hum may yalmizuka fiṣ-ṣadaqāt, fa in u'ṭụ min-hā raḍụ wa il lam yu'ṭau min-h<b>ā</b> iżā hum yaskhaṭụn
9|59|walau annahum raḍụ m<b>ā</b> ātāhumullāhu wa rasụluhụ wa qālụ ḥasbunallāhu sayu`tīnallāhu min faḍlihī wa rasụluhụ inn<b>ā</b> ilallāhi rāgibụn
9|60|innamaṣ-ṣadaqātu lil-fuqar<b>ā</b>`i wal-masākīni wal-'āmilīna 'alaihā wal-mu`allafati qulụbuhum wa fir-riqābi wal-gārimīna wa fī sabīlillāhi wabnis-sabīl, farīḍatam minallāh, wallāhu 'alīmun ḥakīm
9|61|wa min-humullażīna yu`żụnan-nabiyya wa yaqụlụna huwa użun, qul użunu khairil lakum yu`minu billāhi wa yu`minu lil-mu`minīna wa raḥmatul lillażīna āmanụ mingkum, wallażīna yu`żụna rasụlallāhi lahum 'ażābun alīm
9|62|yaḥlifụna billāhi lakum liyurḍụkum wallāhu wa rasụluh<b>ū</b> aḥaqqu ay yurḍụhu ing kānụ mu`minīn
9|63|a lam ya'lam<b>ū</b> annahụ may yuḥādidillāha wa rasụlahụ fa anna lahụ nāra jahannama khālidan fīhā, żālikal-khizyul-'aẓīm
9|64|yaḥżarul-munāfiqụna an tunazzala 'alaihim sụratun tunabbi`uhum bimā fī qulụbihim, qulistahzi`ụ, innallāha mukhrijum mā taḥżarụn
9|65|wa la`in sa`altahum layaqụlunna innamā kunnā nakhụḍu wa nal'ab, qul a billāhi wa āyātihī wa rasụlihī kuntum tastahzi`ụn
9|66|lā ta'tażirụ qad kafartum ba'da īmānikum, in na'fu 'an ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatim mingkum nu'ażżib ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatam bi`annahum kānụ mujrimīn
9|67|al-munāfiqụna wal-munāfiqātu ba'ḍuhum mim ba'ḍ, ya`murụna bil-mungkari wa yan-hauna 'anil-ma'rụfi wa yaqbiḍụna aidiyahum, nasullāha fa nasiyahum, innal-munāfiqīna humul-fāsiqụn
9|68|wa'adallāhul-munāfiqīna wal-munāfiqāti wal-kuffāra nāra jahannama khālidīna fīhā, hiya ḥasbuhum, wa la'anahumullāh, wa lahum 'ażābum muqīm
9|69|kallażīna ming qablikum kān<b>ū</b> asyadda mingkum quwwataw wa akṡara amwālaw wa aulādā, fastamta'ụ bikhalāqihim fastamta'tum bikhalāqikum kamastamta'allażīna ming qablikum bikhalāqihim wa khuḍtum kallażī khāḍụ, ul<b>ā</b>`ika ḥabiṭat a'māluhum fid-dun-yā wal-ākhirah, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-khāsirụn
9|70|a lam ya`tihim naba`ullażīna ming qablihim qaumi nụḥiw wa 'ādiw wa ṡamụda wa qaumi ibrāhīma wa aṣ-ḥābi madyana wal-mu`tafikāt, atat-hum rusuluhum bil-bayyināt, fa mā kānallāhu liyaẓlimahum wa lāking kān<b>ū</b> anfusahum yaẓlimụn
9|71|wal-mu`minụna wal-mu`minātu ba'ḍuhum auliy<b>ā</b>`u ba'ḍ, ya`murụna bil-ma'rụfi wa yan-hauna 'anil-mungkari wa yuqīmụnaṣ-ṣalāta wa yu`tụnaz-zakāta wa yuṭī'ụnallāha wa rasụlah, ul<b>ā</b>`ika sayar-ḥamuhumullāh, innallāha 'azīzun ḥakīm
9|72|wa'adallāhul-mu`minīna wal-mu`mināti jannātin tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hāru khālidīna fīhā wa masākina ṭayyibatan fī jannāti 'adn, wa riḍwānum minallāhi akbar, żālika huwal-fauzul-'aẓīm
9|73|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nabiyyu jāhidil-kuffāra wal-munāfiqīna wagluẓ 'alaihim, wa ma`wāhum jahannamu wa bi`sal-maṣīr
9|74|yaḥlifụna billāhi mā qālụ, wa laqad qālụ kalimatal-kufri wa kafarụ ba'da islāmihim wa hammụ bimā lam yanalụ, wa mā naqam<b>ū</b> ill<b>ā</b> an agnāhumullāhu wa rasụluhụ min faḍlih, fa iy yatụbụ yaku khairal lahum, wa iy yatawallau yu'ażżib-humullāhu 'ażāban alīman fid-dun-yā wal-ākhirah, wa mā lahum fil-arḍi miw waliyyiw wa lā naṣīr
9|75|wa min-hum man 'āhadallāha la`in ātānā min faḍlihī lanaṣṣaddaqanna wa lanakụnanna minaṣ-ṣāliḥīn
9|76|fa lamm<b>ā</b> ātāhum min faḍlihī bakhilụ bihī wa tawallaw wa hum mu'riḍụn
9|77|fa a'qabahum nifāqan fī qulụbihim ilā yaumi yalqaunahụ bim<b>ā</b> akhlafullāha mā wa'adụhu wa bimā kānụ yakżibụn
9|78|a lam ya'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha ya'lamu sirrahum wa najwāhum wa annallāha 'allāmul-guyụb
9|79|allażīna yalmizụnal-muṭṭawwi'īna minal-mu`minīna fiṣ-ṣadaqāti wallażīna lā yajidụna illā juhdahum fa yaskharụna min-hum, sakhirallāhu min-hum wa lahum 'ażābun alīm
9|80|istagfir lahum au lā tastagfir lahum, in tastagfir lahum sab'īna marratan fa lay yagfirallāhu lahum, żālika bi`annahum kafarụ billāhi wa rasụlih, wallāhu lā yahdil-qaumal-fāsiqīn
9|81|fariḥal-mukhallafụna bimaq'adihim khilāfa rasụlillāhi wa karih<b>ū</b> ay yujāhidụ bi`amwālihim wa anfusihim fī sabīlillāhi wa qālụ lā tanfirụ fil-ḥarr, qul nāru jahannama asyaddu ḥarrā, lau kānụ yafqahụn
9|82|falyaḍ-ḥakụ qalīlaw walyabkụ kaṡīrā, jaz<b>ā</b>`am bimā kānụ yaksibụn
9|83|fa ir raja'akallāhu ilā ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatim min-hum fasta`żanụka lil-khurụji fa qul lan takhrujụ ma'iya abadaw wa lan tuqātilụ ma'iya 'aduwwā, innakum raḍītum bil-qu'ụdi awwala marrah, faq'udụ ma'al-khālifīn
9|84|wa lā tuṣalli 'al<b>ā</b> aḥadim min-hum māta abadaw wa lā taqum 'alā qabrih, innahum kafarụ billāhi wa rasụlihī wa mātụ wa hum fāsiqụn
9|85|wa lā tu'jibka amwāluhum wa aulāduhum, innamā yurīdullāhu ay yu'ażżibahum bihā fid-dun-yā wa taz-haqa anfusuhum wa hum kāfirụn
9|86|wa iż<b>ā</b> unzilat sụratun an āminụ billāhi wa jāhidụ ma'a rasụlihista`żanaka uluṭ-ṭauli min-hum wa qālụ żarnā nakum ma'al-qā'idīn
9|87|raḍụ bi`ay yakụnụ ma'al-khawālifi wa ṭubi'a 'alā qulụbihim fa hum lā yafqahụn
9|88|lākinir-rasụlu wallażīna āmanụ ma'ahụ jāhadụ bi`amwālihim wa anfusihim, wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika lahumul-khairātu wa ul<b>ā</b>`ika humul-mufliḥụn
9|89|a'addallāhu lahum jannātin tajrī min taḥtihal-an-hāru khālidīna fīhā, żālikal-fauzul-'aẓīm
9|90|wa j<b>ā</b>`al-mu'ażżirụna minal-a'rābi liyu`żana lahum wa qa'adallażīna każabullāha wa rasụlah, sayuṣībullażīna kafarụ min-hum 'ażābun alīm
9|91|laisa 'alaḍ-ḍu'af<b>ā</b>`i wa lā 'alal-marḍā wa lā 'alallażīna lā yajidụna mā yunfiqụna ḥarajun iżā naṣaḥụ lillāhi wa rasụlih, mā 'alal-muḥsinīna min sabīl, wallāhu gafụrur raḥīm
9|92|wa lā 'alallażīna iżā m<b>ā</b> atauka litaḥmilahum qulta l<b>ā</b> ajidu m<b>ā</b> aḥmilukum 'alaihi tawallaw wa a'yunuhum tafīḍu minad-dam'i ḥazanan allā yajidụ mā yunfiqụn
9|93|innamas-sabīlu 'alallażīna yasta`żinụnaka wa hum agniy<b>ā</b>`, raḍụ bi`ay yakụnụ ma'al-khawālifi wa ṭaba'allāhu 'alā qulụbihim fa hum lā ya'lamụn
9|94|ya'tażirụna ilaikum iżā raja'tum ilaihim, qul lā ta'tażirụ lan nu`mina lakum qad nabba`anallāhu min akhbārikum wa sayarallāhu 'amalakum wa rasụluhụ ṡumma turaddụna ilā 'ālimil-gaibi wasy-syahādati fa yunabbi`ukum bimā kuntum ta'malụn
9|95|sayaḥlifụna billāhi lakum iżangqalabtum ilaihim litu'riḍụ 'an-hum, fa a'riḍụ 'an-hum, innahum rijsuw wa ma`wāhum jahannamu jaz<b>ā</b>`am bimā kānụ yaksibụn
9|96|yaḥlifụna lakum litarḍau 'an-hum, fa in tarḍau 'an-hum fa innallāha lā yarḍā 'anil-qaumil-fāsiqīn
9|97|al-a'rābu asyaddu kufraw wa nifāqaw wa ajdaru allā ya'lamụ ḥudụda m<b>ā</b> anzalallāhu 'alā rasụlih, wallāhu 'alīmun ḥakīm
9|98|wa minal-a'rābi may yattakhiżu mā yunfiqu magramaw wa yatarabbaṣu bikumud-daw<b>ā</b>`ir, 'alaihim d<b>ā</b>`iratus-saụ`, wallāhu samī'un 'alīm
9|99|wa minal-a'rābi may yu`minu billāhi wal-yaumil-ākhiri wa yattakhiżu mā yunfiqu qurubātin 'indallāhi wa ṣalawātir-rasụl, al<b>ā</b> innahā qurbatul lahum, sayudkhiluhumullāhu fī raḥmatih, innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
9|100|was-sābiqụnal-awwalụna minal-muhājirīna wal-anṣāri wallażīnattaba'ụhum bi`iḥsānir raḍiyallāhu 'an-hum wa raḍụ 'an-hu wa a'adda lahum jannātin tajrī taḥtahal-an-hāru khālidīna fīh<b>ā</b> abadā, żālikal-fauzul-'aẓīm
9|101|wa mim man ḥaulakum minal-a'rābi munāfiqụn, wa min ahlil-madīnati maradụ 'alan-nifāq, lā ta'lamuhum, naḥnu na'lamuhum, sanu'ażżibuhum marrataini ṡumma yuraddụna ilā 'ażābin 'aẓīm
9|102|wa ākharụna'tarafụ biżunụbihim khalaṭụ 'amalan ṣāliḥaw wa ākhara sayyi`ā, 'asallāhu ay yatụba 'alaihim, innallāha gafụrur raḥīm
9|103|khuż min amwālihim ṣadaqatan tuṭahhiruhum wa tuzakkīhim bihā wa ṣalli 'alaihim, inna ṣalātaka sakanul lahum, wallāhu samī'un 'alīm
9|104|a lam ya'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha huwa yaqbalut-taubata 'an 'ibādihī wa ya`khużuṣ-ṣadaqāti wa annallāha huwat-tawwābur-raḥīm
9|105|wa quli'malụ fa sayarallāhu 'amalakum wa rasụluhụ wal-mu`minụn, wa saturaddụna ilā 'ālimil-gaibi wasy-syahādati fa yunabbi`ukum bimā kuntum ta'malụn
9|106|wa ākharụna murjauna li`amrillāhi immā yu'ażżibuhum wa immā yatụbu 'alaihim, wallāhu 'alīmun ḥakīm
9|107|wallażīnattakhażụ masjidan ḍirāraw wa kufraw wa tafrīqam bainal-mu`minīna wa irṣādal liman ḥāraballāha wa rasụlahụ ming qabl, wa layaḥlifunna in aradn<b>ā</b> illal-ḥusnā, wallāhu yasy-hadu innahum lakāżibụn
9|108|lā taqum fīhi abadā, lamasjidun ussisa 'alat-taqwā min awwali yaumin aḥaqqu an taqụma fīh, fīhi rijāluy yuḥibbụna ay yataṭahharụ, wallāhu yuḥibbul-muṭṭahhirīn
9|109|a fa man assasa bun-yānahụ 'alā taqwā minallāhi wa riḍwānin khairun am man assasa bun-yānahụ 'alā syafā jurufin hārin fan-hāra bihī fī nāri jahannam, wallāhu lā yahdil qaumaẓ-ẓālimīn
9|110|lā yazālu bun-yānuhumullażī banau rībatan fī qulụbihim ill<b>ā</b> an taqaṭṭa'a qulụbuhum, wallāhu 'alīmun ḥakīm
9|111|innallāhasytarā minal-mu`minīna anfusahum wa amwālahum bi`anna lahumul-jannah, yuqātilụna fī sabīlillāhi fa yaqtulụna wa yuqtalụna wa'dan 'alaihi ḥaqqan fit-taurāti wal-injīli wal-qur`ān, wa man aufā bi'ahdihī minallāhi fastabsyirụ bibai'ikumullażī bāya'tum bih, wa żālika huwal-fauzul-'aẓīm
9|112|att<b>ā</b>`ibụnal-'ābidụnal-ḥāmidụnas-s<b>ā</b>`iḥụnar-rāki'ụnas-sājidụnal-āmirụna bil-ma'rụfi wan-nāhụna 'anil-mungkari wal-ḥāfiẓụna liḥudụdillāh, wa basysyiril-mu`minīn
9|113|mā kāna lin-nabiyyi wallażīna āman<b>ū</b> ay yastagfirụ lil-musyrikīna walau kān<b>ū</b> ulī qurbā mim ba'di mā tabayyana lahum annahum aṣ-ḥābul-jaḥīm
9|114|wa mā kānastigfāru ibrāhīma li`abīhi illā 'am mau'idatiw wa'adah<b>ā</b> iyyāh, fa lammā tabayyana lah<b>ū</b> annahụ 'aduwwul lillāhi tabarra`a min-h, inna ibrāhīma la`awwāhun ḥalīm
9|115|wa mā kānallāhu liyuḍilla qaumam ba'da iż hadāhum ḥattā yubayyina lahum mā yattaqụn, innallāha bikulli syai`in 'alīm
9|116|innallāha lahụ mulkus-samāwāti wal-arḍ, yuḥyī wa yumīt, wa mā lakum min dụnillāhi miw waliyyiw wa lā naṣīr
9|117|laqat tāballāhu 'alan-nabiyyi wal-muhājirīna wal-anṣārillażīnattaba'ụhu fī sā'atil-'usrati mim ba'di mā kāda yazīgu qulụbu farīqim min-hum ṡumma tāba 'alaihim, innahụ bihim ra`ụfur raḥīm
9|118|wa 'alaṡ-ṡalāṡatillażīna khullifụ, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iżā ḍāqat 'alaihimul-arḍu bimā raḥubat wa ḍāqat 'alaihim anfusuhum wa ẓann<b>ū</b> al lā malja`a minallāhi ill<b>ā</b> ilaīh, ṡumma tāba 'alaihim liyatụbụ, innallāha huwat-tawwābur-raḥīm
9|119|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanuttaqullāha wa kụnụ ma'aṣ-ṣādiqīn
9|120|mā kāna li`ahlil-madīnati wa man ḥaulahum minal-a'rābi ay yatakhallafụ 'ar rasụlillāhi wa lā yargabụ bi`anfusihim 'an nafsih, żālika bi`annahum lā yuṣībuhum ẓama`uw wa lā naṣabuw wa lā makhmaṣatun fī sabīlillāhi wa lā yaṭa`ụna mauṭi`ay yagīẓul-kuffāra wa lā yanalụna min 'aduwwin nailan illā kutiba lahum bihī 'amalun ṣāliḥ, innallāha lā yuḍī'u ajral-muḥsinīn
9|121|wa lā yunfiqụna nafaqatan ṣagīrataw wa lā kabīrataw wa lā yaqṭa'ụna wādiyan illā kutiba lahum liyajziyahumullāhu aḥsana mā kānụ ya'malụn
9|122|wa mā kānal-mu`minụna liyanfirụ k<b>ā</b>ffah, falau lā nafara ming kulli firqatim min-hum ṭ<b>ā</b>`ifatul liyatafaqqahụ fid-dīni wa liyunżirụ qaumahum iżā raja'<b>ū</b> ilaihim la'allahum yaḥżarụn
9|123|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhallażīna āmanụ qātilullażīna yalụnakum minal-kuffāri walyajidụ fīkum gilẓah, wa'lam<b>ū</b> annallāha ma'al-muttaqīn
9|124|wa iżā m<b>ā</b> unzilat sụratun fa min-hum may yaqụlu ayyukum zādat-hu hāżih<b>ī</b> īmānā, fa ammallażīna āmanụ fa zādat-hum īmānaw wa hum yastabsyirụn
9|125|wa ammallażīna fī qulụbihim maraḍun fa zādat-hum rijsan ilā rijsihim wa mātụ wa hum kāfirụn
9|126|a wa lā yarauna annahum yuftanụna fī kulli 'āmim marratan au marrataini ṡumma lā yatụbụna wa lā hum yażżakkarụn
9|127|wa iżā m<b>ā</b> unzilat sụratun naẓara ba'ḍuhum ilā ba'ḍ, hal yarākum min aḥadin ṡummanṣarafụ, ṣarafallāhu qulụbahum bi`annahum qaumul lā yafqahụn
9|128|laqad j<b>ā</b>`akum rasụlum min anfusikum 'azīzun 'alaihi mā 'anittum ḥarīṣun 'alaikum bil-mu`minīna ra`ụfur raḥīm
9|129|fa in tawallau fa qul ḥasbiyallāhu l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huw, 'alaihi tawakkaltu wa huwa rabbul-'arsyil-'aẓīm
10|1|alif l<b>ā</b>m rā, tilka āyātul-kitābil-ḥakīm
10|2|a kāna lin-nāsi 'ajaban an auḥain<b>ā</b> ilā rajulim min-hum an anżirin-nāsa wa basysyirillażīna āman<b>ū</b> anna lahum qadama ṣidqin 'inda rabbihim, qālal-kāfirụna inna hāżā lasāḥirum mubīn
10|3|inna rabbakumullāhullażī khalaqas-samāwāti wal-arḍa fī sittati ayyāmin ṡummastawā 'alal-'arsyi yudabbirul-amr, mā min syafī'in illā mim ba'di iżnih, żālikumullāhu rabbukum fa'budụh, a fa lā tażakkarụn
10|4|ilaihi marji'ukum jamī'ā, wa'dallāhi ḥaqqā, innahụ yabda`ul-khalqa ṡumma yu'īduhụ liyajziyallażīna āmanụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāti bil-qisṭ, wallażīna kafarụ lahum syarābum min ḥamīmiw wa 'ażābun alīmum bimā kānụ yakfurụn
10|5|huwallażī ja'alasy-syamsa ḍiy<b>ā</b>`aw wal-qamara nụraw wa qaddarahụ manāzila lita'lamụ 'adadas-sinīna wal-ḥisāb, mā khalaqallāhu żālika illā bil-ḥaqq, yufaṣṣilul-āyāti liqaumiy ya'lamụn
10|6|inna fikhtilāfil-laili wan-nahāri wa mā khalaqallāhu fis-samāwāti wal-arḍi la`āyātil liqaumiy yattaqụn
10|7|innallażīna lā yarjụna liq<b>ā</b>`ana wa raḍụ bil-ḥayātid-dun-yā waṭma`annụ bihā wallażīna hum 'an āyātinā gāfilụn
10|8|ul<b>ā</b>`ika ma`wāhumun-nāru bimā kānụ yaksibụn
10|9|innallażīna āmanụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāti yahdīhim rabbuhum bi`īmānihim, tajrī min taḥtihimul-an-hāru fī jannātin-na'īm
10|10|da'wāhum fīhā sub-ḥānakallāhumma wa taḥiyyatuhum fīhā salām, wa ākhiru da'wāhum anil-ḥamdu lillāhi rabbil 'ālamīn
10|11|walau yu'ajjilullāhu lin-nāsisy-syarrasti'jālahum bil-khairi laquḍiya ilaihim ajaluhum, fa nażarullażīna lā yarjụna liq<b>ā</b>`anā fī ṭugyānihim ya'mahụn
10|12|wa iżā massal-insānaḍ-ḍurru da'ānā lijambih<b>ī</b> au qā'idan au q<b>ā</b>`imā, fa lammā kasyafnā 'an-hu ḍurrahụ marra ka`al lam yad'un<b>ā</b> ilā ḍurrim massah, każālika zuyyina lil-musrifīna mā kānụ ya'malụn
10|13|wa laqad ahlaknal-qurụna ming qablikum lammā ẓalamụ wa j<b>ā</b>`at-hum rusuluhum bil-bayyināti wa mā kānụ liyu`minụ, każālika najzil-qaumal-mujrimīn
10|14|ṡumma ja'alnākum khal<b>ā</b>`ifa fil-arḍi mim ba'dihim linanẓura kaifa ta'malụn
10|15|wa iżā tutlā 'alaihim āyātunā bayyināting qālallażīna lā yarjụna liq<b>ā</b>`ana`ti biqur`ānin gairi hāż<b>ā</b> au baddil-h, qul mā yakụnu l<b>ī</b> an ubaddilahụ min tilq<b>ā</b>`i nafsī, in attabi'u illā mā yụḥ<b>ā</b> ilayy, inn<b>ī</b> akhāfu in 'aṣaitu rabbī 'ażāba yaumin 'aẓīm
10|16|qul lau sy<b>ā</b>`allāhu mā talautuhụ 'alaikum wa l<b>ā</b> adrākum bihī fa qad labiṡtu fīkum 'umuram ming qablih, a fa lā ta'qilụn
10|17|fa man aẓlamu mim maniftarā 'alallāhi każiban au każżaba bi`āyātih, innahụ lā yufliḥul-mujrimụn
10|18|wa ya'budụna min dụnillāhi mā lā yaḍurruhum wa lā yanfa'uhum wa yaqụlụna h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`i syufa'<b>ā</b>`unā 'indallāh, qul a tunabbi`ụnallāha bimā lā ya'lamu fis-samāwāti wa lā fil-arḍ, sub-ḥānahụ wa ta'ālā 'ammā yusyrikụn
10|19|wa mā kānan-nāsu ill<b>ā</b> ummataw wāḥidatan fakhtalafụ, walau lā kalimatun sabaqat mir rabbika laquḍiya bainahum fīmā fīhi yakhtalifụn
10|20|wa yaqụlụna lau l<b>ā</b> unzila 'alaihi āyatum mir rabbih, fa qul innamal-gaibu lillāhi fantaẓirụ, innī ma'akum minal-muntaẓirīn
10|21|wa iż<b>ā</b> ażaqnan-nāsa raḥmatam mim ba'di ḍarr<b>ā</b>`a massat-hum iżā lahum makrun f<b>ī</b> āyātinā, qulillāhu asra'u makrā, inna rusulana yaktubụna mā tamkurụn
10|22|huwallażī yusayyirukum fil-barri wal-baḥr, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iżā kuntum fil-fulk, wa jaraina bihim birīḥin ṭayyibatiw wa fariḥụ bihā j<b>ā</b>`at-hā rīḥun 'āṣifuw wa j<b>ā</b>`ahumul-mauju ming kulli makāniw wa ẓann<b>ū</b> annahum uḥīṭa bihim da'awullāha mukhliṣīna lahud-dīn, la`in anjaitanā min hāżihī lanakụnanna minasy-syākirīn
10|23|fa lamm<b>ā</b> anjāhum iżā hum yabgụna fil-arḍi bigairil-ḥaqq, y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsu innamā bagyukum 'al<b>ā</b> anfusikum matā'al-ḥayātid-dun-yā ṡumma ilainā marji'ukum fa nunabbi`ukum bimā kuntum ta'malụn
10|24|innamā maṡalul-ḥayātid-dun-yā kam<b>ā</b>`in anzalnāhu minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i fakhtalaṭa bihī nabātul-arḍi mimmā ya`kulun-nāsu wal-an'ām, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iż<b>ā</b> akhażatil-arḍu zukhrufahā wazzayyanat wa ẓanna ahluh<b>ā</b> annahum qādirụna 'alaih<b>ā</b> atāh<b>ā</b> amrunā lailan au nahāran fa ja'alnāhā ḥaṣīdang ka`al lam tagna bil-ams, każālika nufaṣṣilul-āyāti liqaumiy yatafakkarụn
10|25|wallāhu yad'<b>ū</b> ilā dāris-salām, wa yahdī may yasy<b>ā</b>`u ilā ṣirāṭim mustaqīm
10|26|lillażīna aḥsanul-ḥusnā wa ziyādah, wa lā yar-haqu wujụhahum qataruw wa lā żillah, ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābul-jannati hum fīhā khālidụn
10|27|wallażīna kasabus-sayyi`āti jaz<b>ā</b>`u sayyi`atim bimiṡlihā wa tar-haquhum żillah, mā lahum minallāhi min 'āṣim, ka`annam<b>ā</b> ugsyiyat wujụhuhum qiṭa'am minal-laili muẓlimā, ul<b>ā</b>`ika aṣ-ḥābun-nār, hum fīhā khālidụn
10|28|wa yauma naḥsyuruhum jamī'an ṡumma naqụlu lillażīna asyrakụ makānakum antum wa syurak<b>ā</b>`ukum, fa zayyalnā bainahum wa qāla syurak<b>ā</b>`uhum mā kuntum iyyānā ta'budụn
10|29|fa kafā billāhi syahīdam bainanā wa bainakum ing kunnā 'an 'ibādatikum lagāfilīn
10|30|hunālika tablụ kullu nafsim m<b>ā</b> aslafat wa rudd<b>ū</b> ilallāhi maulāhumul-ḥaqqi wa ḍalla 'an-hum mā kānụ yaftarụn
10|31|qul may yarzuqukum minas-sam<b>ā</b>`i wal-arḍi am may yamlikus-sam'a wal-abṣāra wa may yukhrijul-ḥayya minal-mayyiti wa yukhrijul-mayyita minal-ḥayyi wa may yudabbirul-amr, fa sayaqụlụnallāh, fa qul a fa lā tattaqụn
10|32|fa żālikumullāhu rabbukumul-ḥaqq, fa māżā ba'dal-ḥaqqi illaḍ-ḍalālu fa annā tuṣrafụn
10|33|każālika ḥaqqat kalimatu rabbika 'alallażīna fasaq<b>ū</b> annahum lā yu`minụn
10|34|qul hal min syurak<b>ā</b>`ikum may yabda`ul-khalqa ṡumma yu'īduh, qulillāhu yabda`ul-khalqa ṡumma yu'īduhụ fa annā tu`fakụn
10|35|qul hal min syurak<b>ā</b>`ikum may yahd<b>ī</b> ilal-ḥaqq, qulillāhu yahdī lil-ḥaqq, a fa may yahd<b>ī</b> ilal-ḥaqqi aḥaqqu ay yuttaba'a am mal lā yahidd<b>ī</b> ill<b>ā</b> ay yuhdā, fa mā lakum, kaifa taḥkumụn
10|36|wa mā yattabi'u akṡaruhum illā ẓannā, innaẓ-ẓanna lā yugnī minal-ḥaqqi syai`ā, innallāha 'alīmum bimā yaf'alụn
10|37|wa mā kāna hāżal-qur`ānu ay yuftarā min dụnillāhi wa lākin taṣdīqallażī baina yadaihi wa tafṣīlal-kitābi lā raiba fīhi mir rabbil-'ālamīn
10|38|am yaqụlụnaftarāh, qul fa`tụ bisụratim miṡlihī wad'ụ manistaṭa'tum min dụnillāhi ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
10|39|bal każżabụ bimā lam yuḥīṭụ bi'ilmihī wa lammā ya`tihim ta`wīluh, każālika każżaballażīna ming qablihim fanẓur kaifa kāna 'āqibatuẓ-ẓālimīn
10|40|wa min-hum may yu`minu bihī wa min-hum mal lā yu`minu bih, wa rabbuka a'lamu bil-mufsidīn
10|41|wa ing każżabụka fa qul lī 'amalī wa lakum 'amalukum, antum bar<b>ī</b>`ụna mimm<b>ā</b> a'malu wa ana bar<b>ī</b>`um mimmā ta'malụn
10|42|wa min-hum may yastami'ụna ilaīk, a fa anta tusmi'uṣ-ṣumma walau kānụ lā ya'qilụn
10|43|wa min-hum may yanẓuru ilaīk, a fa anta tahdil-'umya walau kānụ lā yubṣirụn
10|44|innallāha lā yaẓlimun-nāsa syai`aw wa lākinnan-nāsa anfusahum yaẓlimụn
10|45|wa yauma yaḥsyuruhum ka`al lam yalbaṡ<b>ū</b> illā sā'atam minan-nahāri yata'ārafụna bainahum, qad khasirallażīna każżabụ biliq<b>ā</b>`illāhi wa mā kānụ muhtadīn
10|46|wa immā nuriyannaka ba'ḍallażī na'iduhum au natawaffayannaka fa ilainā marji'uhum ṡummallāhu syahīdun 'alā mā yaf'alụn
10|47|wa likulli ummatir rasụl, fa iżā j<b>ā</b>`a rasụluhum quḍiya bainahum bil-qisṭi wa hum lā yuẓlamụn
10|48|wa yaqụlụna matā hāżal-wa'du ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
10|49|qul l<b>ā</b> amliku linafsī ḍarraw wa lā naf'an illā mā sy<b>ā</b>`allāh, likulli ummatin ajal, iżā j<b>ā</b>`a ajaluhum fa lā yasta`khirụna sā'ataw wa lā yastaqdimụn
10|50|qul a ra`aitum in atākum 'ażābuhụ bayātan au nahāram māżā yasta'jilu min-hul-mujrimụn
10|51|a ṡumma iżā mā waqa'a āmantum bih, <b>ā</b>l-āna waqad kuntum bihī tasta'jilụn
10|52|ṡumma qīla lillażīna ẓalamụ żụqụ 'ażābal-khuld, hal tujzauna illā bimā kuntum taksibụn
10|53|wa yastambi`ụnaka aḥaqqun huw, qul ī wa rabb<b>ī</b> innahụ laḥaqq, wa m<b>ā</b> antum bimu'jizīn
10|54|walau anna likulli nafsin ẓalamat mā fil-arḍi laftadat bih, wa asarrun-nadāmata lammā ra`awul-'ażāb, wa quḍiya bainahum bil-qisṭi wa hum lā yuẓlamụn
10|55|al<b>ā</b> inna lillāhi mā fis-samāwāti wal-arḍ, al<b>ā</b> inna wa'dallāhi ḥaqquw wa lākinna akṡarahum lā ya'lamụn
10|56|huwa yuḥyī wa yumītu wa ilaihi turja'ụn
10|57|y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsu qad j<b>ā</b>`atkum mau'iẓatum mir rabbikum wa syif<b>ā</b>`ul limā fiṣ-ṣudụri wa hudaw wa raḥmatul lil-mu`minīn
10|58|qul bifaḍlillāhi wa biraḥmatihī fa biżālika falyafraḥụ, huwa khairum mimmā yajma'ụn
10|59|qul a ra`aitum m<b>ā</b> anzalallāhu lakum mir rizqin fa ja'altum min-hu ḥarāmaw wa halālā, qul <b>ā</b>llāhu ażina lakum am 'alallāhi taftarụn
10|60|wa mā ẓannullażīna yaftarụna 'alallāhil-każiba yaumal-qiyāmah, innallāha lażụ faḍlin 'alan-nāsi wa lākinna akṡarahum lā yasykurụn
10|61|wa mā takụnu fī sya`niw wa mā tatlụ min-hu ming qur`āniw wa lā ta'malụna min 'amalin illā kunnā 'alaikum syuhụdan iż tufīḍụna fīh, wa mā ya'zubu 'ar rabbika mim miṡqāli żarratin fil-arḍi wa lā fis-sam<b>ā</b>`i wa l<b>ā</b> aṣgara min żālika wa l<b>ā</b> akbara illā fī kitābim mubīn
10|62|al<b>ā</b> inna auliy<b>ā</b>`allāhi lā khaufun 'alaihim wa lā hum yaḥzanụn
10|63|allażīna āmanụ wa kānụ yattaqụn
10|64|lahumul-busyrā fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā wa fil-ākhirah, lā tabdīla likalimātillāh, żālika huwal-fauzul-'aẓīm
10|65|wa lā yaḥzungka qauluhum, innal-'izzata lillāhi jamī'ā, huwas-samī'ul-'alīm
10|66|al<b>ā</b> inna lillāhi man fis-samāwāti wa man fil-arḍ, wa mā yattabi'ullażīna yad'ụna min dụnillāhi syurak<b>ā</b>`, iy yattabi'ụna illaẓ-ẓanna wa in hum illā yakhruṣụn
10|67|huwallażī ja'ala lakumul-laila litaskunụ fīhi wan-nahāra mubṣirā, inna fī żālika la`āyātil liqaumiy yasma'ụn
10|68|qāluttakhażallāhu waladan sub-ḥānah, huwal-ganiyy, lahụ mā fis-samāwāti wa mā fil-arḍ, in 'indakum min sulṭānim bihāżā, a taqụlụna 'alallāhi mā lā ta'lamụn
10|69|qul innallażīna yaftarụna 'alallāhil-każiba lā yufliḥụn
10|70|matā'un fid-dun-yā ṡumma ilainā marji'uhum ṡumma nużīquhumul-'ażābasy-syadīda bimā kānụ yakfurụn
10|71|watlu 'alaihim naba`a nụḥ, iż qāla liqaumihī yā qaumi ing kāna kabura 'alaikum maqāmī wa tażkīrī bi`āyātillāhi fa 'alallāhi tawakkaltu fa ajmi'<b>ū</b> amrakum wa syurak<b>ā</b>`akum ṡumma lā yakun amrukum 'alaikum gummatan ṡummaqḍ<b>ū</b> ilayya wa lā tunẓirụn
10|72|fa in tawallaitum fa mā sa`altukum min ajr, in ajriya illā 'alallāhi wa umirtu an akụna minal-muslimīn
10|73|fa każżabụhu fa najjaināhu wa mam ma'ahụ fil-fulki wa ja'alnāhum khal<b>ā</b>`ifa wa agraqnallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātinā, fanẓur kaifa kāna 'āqibatul-munżarīn
10|74|ṡumma ba'aṡnā mim ba'dihī rusulan ilā qaumihim fa j<b>ā</b>`ụhum bil-bayyināti fa mā kānụ liyu`minụ bimā każżabụ bihī ming qabl, każālika naṭba'u 'alā qulụbil-mu'tadīn
10|75|ṡumma ba'aṡnā mim ba'dihim mụsā wa hārụna ilā fir'auna wa mala`ihī bi`āyātinā fastakbarụ wa kānụ qaumam mujrimīn
10|76|fa lammā j<b>ā</b>`ahumul-ḥaqqu min 'indinā qāl<b>ū</b> inna hāżā lasiḥrum mubīn
10|77|qāla mụs<b>ā</b> a taqụlụna lil-ḥaqqi lammā j<b>ā</b>`akum, a siḥrun hāżā, wa lā yufliḥus-sāḥirụn
10|78|qāl<b>ū</b> a ji`tanā litalfitanā 'ammā wajadnā 'alaihi āb<b>ā</b>`anā wa takụna lakumal-kibriy<b>ā</b>`u fil-arḍ, wa mā naḥnu lakumā bimu`minīn
10|79|wa qāla fir'aunu`tụnī bikulli sāḥirin 'alīm
10|80|fa lammā j<b>ā</b>`as-saḥaratu qāla lahum mụs<b>ā</b> alqụ m<b>ā</b> antum mulqụn
10|81|fa lamm<b>ā</b> alqau qāla mụsā mā ji`tum bihis-siḥr, innallāha sayubṭiluh, innallāha lā yuṣliḥu 'amalal-mufsidīn
10|82|wa yuḥiqqullāhul-ḥaqqa bikalimātihī walau karihal-mujrimụn
10|83|fa m<b>ā</b> āmana limụs<b>ā</b> illā żurriyyatum ming qaumihī 'alā khaufim min fir'auna wa mala`ihim ay yaftinahum, wa inna fir'auna la'ālin fil-arḍ, wa innahụ laminal-musrifīn
10|84|wa qāla mụsā yā qaumi ing kuntum āmantum billāhi fa 'alaihi tawakkal<b>ū</b> ing kuntum muslimīn

10|86|wa najjinā biraḥmatika minal-qaumil-kāfirīn
10|87|wa auḥain<b>ā</b> ilā mụsā wa akhīhi an tabawwa`ā liqaumikumā bimiṣra buyụtaw waj'alụ buyụtakum qiblataw wa aqīmuṣ-ṣalāh, wa basysyiril-mu`minīn
10|88|wa qāla mụsā rabban<b>ā</b> innaka ātaita fir'auna wa mala`ahụ zīnataw wa amwālan fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā, rabbanā liyuḍillụ 'an sabīlik, rabbanaṭmis 'al<b>ā</b> amwālihim wasydud 'alā qulụbihim fa lā yu`minụ ḥattā yarawul-'ażābal-alīm
10|89|qāla qad ujībad da'watukumā fastaqīmā wa lā tattabi'<b>ā</b>nni sabīlallażīna lā ya'lamụn
10|90|wa jāwaznā biban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īlal-baḥra fa atba'ahum fir'aunu wa junụduhụ bagyaw wa 'adwā, ḥatt<b>ā</b> iż<b>ā</b> adrakahul-garaqu qāla āmantu annahụ l<b>ā</b> ilāha illallaż<b>ī</b> āmanat bihī ban<b>ū</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla wa ana minal-muslimīn
10|91|<b>ā</b>l-āna wa qad 'aṣaita qablu wa kunta minal-mufsidīn
10|92|fal-yauma nunajjīka bibadanika litakụna liman khalfaka āyah, wa inna kaṡīram minan-nāsi 'an āyātinā lagāfilụn
10|93|wa laqad bawwa`nā ban<b>ī</b> isr<b>ā</b>`īla mubawwa`a ṣidqiw wa razaqnāhum minaṭ-ṭayyibāt, famakhtalafụ ḥattā j<b>ā</b>`ahumul-'ilm, inna rabbaka yaqḍī bainahum yaumal-qiyāmati fīmā kānụ fīhi yakhtalifụn
10|94|fa ing kunta fī syakkim mimm<b>ā</b> anzaln<b>ā</b> ilaika fas`alillażīna yaqra`ụnal-kitāba ming qablik, laqad j<b>ā</b>`akal-ḥaqqu mir rabbika fa lā takụnanna minal-mumtarīn
10|95|wa lā takụnanna minallażīna każżabụ bi`āyātillāhi fa takụna minal-khāsirīn

10|97|walau j<b>ā</b>`at-hum kullu āyatin ḥattā yarawul-'ażābal-alīm
10|98|falau lā kānat qaryatun āmanat fa nafa'ah<b>ā</b> īmānuh<b>ā</b> illā qauma yụnus, lamm<b>ā</b> āmanụ kasyafnā 'an-hum 'ażābal-khizyi fil-ḥayātid-dun-yā wa matta'nāhum ilā ḥīn
10|99|walau sy<b>ā</b>`a rabbuka la`āmana man fil-arḍi kulluhum jamī'ā, a fa anta tukrihun-nāsa ḥattā yakụnụ mu`minīn
10|100|wa mā kāna linafsin an tu`mina illā bi`iżnillāh, wa yaj'alur-rijsa 'alallażīna lā ya'qilụn
10|101|qulinẓurụ māżā fis-samāwāti wal-arḍ, wa mā tugnil-āyātu wan-nużuru 'ang qaumil lā yu`minụn
10|102|fa hal yantaẓirụna illā miṡla ayyāmillażīna khalau ming qablihim, qul fantaẓir<b>ū</b> innī ma'akum minal-muntaẓirīn
10|103|ṡumma nunajjī rusulana wallażīna āmanụ każālik, ḥaqqan 'alainā nunjil-mu`minīn
10|104|qul y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsu ing kuntum fī syakkim min dīnī fa l<b>ā</b> a'budullażīna ta'budụna min dụnillāhi wa lākin a'budullāhallażī yatawaffākum wa umirtu an akụna minal-mu`minīn
10|105|wa an aqim waj-haka lid-dīni ḥanīfā, wa lā takụnanna minal-musyrikīn
10|106|wa lā tad'u min dụnillāhi mā lā yanfa'uka wa lā yaḍurruk, fa in fa'alta fa innaka iżam minaẓ-ẓālimīn
10|107|wa iy yamsaskallāhu biḍurrin fa lā kāsyifa lah<b>ū</b> illā huw, wa iy yuridka bikhairin fa lā r<b>ā</b>dda lifaḍlih, yuṣību bihī may yasy<b>ā</b>`u min 'ibādih, wa huwal-gafụrur-raḥīm
10|108|qul y<b>ā</b> ayyuhan-nāsu qad j<b>ā</b>`akumul-ḥaqqu mir rabbikum, fa manihtadā fa innamā yahtadī linafsih, wa man ḍalla fa innamā yaḍillu 'alaihā, wa m<b>ā</b> ana 'alaikum biwakīl
10|109|wattabi' mā yụḥ<b>ā</b> ilaika waṣbir ḥattā yaḥkumallāh, wa huwa khairul-ḥākimīn
11|1|alif l<b>ā</b>m rā, kitābun uḥkimat āyātuhụ ṡumma fuṣṣilat mil ladun ḥakīmin khabīr
11|2|allā ta'bud<b>ū</b> illallāh, innanī lakum min-hu nażīruw wa basyīr
11|3|wa anistagfirụ rabbakum ṡumma tụb<b>ū</b> ilaihi yumatti'kum matā'an ḥasanan il<b>ā</b> ajalim musamman wa yu`ti kulla żī faḍlin faḍlah, wa in tawallau fa inn<b>ī</b> akhāfu 'alaikum 'ażāba yauming kabīr
11|4|ilallāhi marji'ukum, wa huwa 'alā kulli syai`ing qadīr
11|5|al<b>ā</b> innahum yaṡnụna ṣudụrahum liyastakhfụ min-h, alā ḥīna yastagsyụna ṡiyābahum ya'lamu mā yusirrụna wa mā yu'linụn, innahụ 'alīmum biżātiṣ-ṣudụr
11|6|wa mā min d<b>ā</b>bbatin fil-arḍi illā 'alallāhi rizquhā wa ya'lamu mustaqarrahā wa mustauda'ahā, kullun fī kitābim mubīn
11|7|wa huwallażī khalaqas-samāwāti wal-arḍa fī sittati ayyāmiw wa kāna 'arsyuhụ 'alal-m<b>ā</b>`i liyabluwakum ayyukum aḥsanu 'amalā, wa la`ing qulta innakum mab'ụṡụna mim ba'dil-mauti layaqụlannallażīna kafar<b>ū</b> in hāż<b>ā</b> illā siḥrum mubīn
11|8|wa la`in akhkharnā 'an-humul-'ażāba il<b>ā</b> ummatim ma'dụdatil layaqụlunna mā yaḥbisuh, alā yauma ya`tīhim laisa maṣrụfan 'an-hum wa ḥāqa bihim mā kānụ bihī yastahzi`ụn
11|9|wa la`in ażaqnal-insāna minnā raḥmatan ṡumma naza'nāhā min-h, innahụ laya`ụsung kafụr
11|10|wa la`in ażaqnāhu na'm<b>ā</b>`a ba'da ḍarr<b>ā</b>`a massat-hu layaqụlanna żahabas-sayyi`ātu 'annī, innahụ lafariḥun fakhụr
11|11|illallażīna ṣabarụ wa 'amiluṣ-ṣāliḥāt, ul<b>ā</b>`ika lahum magfiratuw wa ajrung kabīr
11|12|fa la'allaka tārikum ba'ḍa mā yụḥ<b>ā</b> ilaika wa ḍ<b>ā</b>`iqum bihī ṣadruka ay yaqụlụ lau l<b>ā</b> unzila 'alaihi kanzun au j<b>ā</b>`a ma'ahụ malak, innam<b>ā</b> anta nażīr, wallāhu 'alā kulli syai`iw wakīl
11|13|am yaqụlụnaftarāh, qul fa`tụ bi'asyri suwarim miṡlihī muftarayātiw wad'ụ manistaṭa'tum min dụnillāhi ing kuntum ṣādiqīn
11|14|fa il lam yastajībụ lakum fa'lam<b>ū</b> annam<b>ā</b> unzila bi'ilmillāhi wa al l<b>ā</b> ilāha illā huw, fa hal antum muslimụn
11|15|mang kāna yurīdul-ḥayātad-dun-yā wa zīnatahā nuwaffi ilaihim a'mālahum fīhā wa hum fīhā lā yubkhasụn
11|16|ul<b>ā</b>`ikallażīna laisa lahum fil-ākhirati illan-nāru wa ḥabiṭa mā ṣana'ụ fīhā wa bāṭilum mā kānụ ya'malụn
11|17|a fa mang kāna 'alā bayyinatim mir rabbihī wa yatlụhu syāhidum min-hu wa ming qablihī kitābu mụs<b>ā</b> imāmaw wa raḥmah, ul<b>ā</b>`ika yu`minụna bih, wa may yakfur bihī minal-aḥzābi fan-nāru mau'iduhụ fa lā taku fī miryatim min-hu innahul-ḥaqqu mir rabbika wa lākinna akṡaran-nāsi lā yu`minụn
11|18|wa man aẓlamu mim maniftarā 'alallāhi każibā, ul<b>ā</b>`ika yu'raḍụna 'alā rabbihim wa yaqụlul-asy-hādu h<b>ā</b>`ul<b>ā</b>`illażīna każabụ 'alā rabbihim, alā la'natullāhi 'alaẓ-ẓālimīn
11|19|allażīna yaṣuddụna 'an sabīlillāhi wa yabgụnahā 'iwajā, wa hum bil-ākhirati hum kāfirụn

11|21|ul<b>ā</b>`ikallażīna khasir<b>ū</b> anfusahum wa ḍalla 'an-hum mā kānụ yaftarụn

11|24|maṡalul-farīqaini kal-a'mā wal-aṣammi wal-baṣīri was-samī', hal yastawiyāni maṡalā, a fa lā tażakkarụn

11|28|qāla yā qaumi a ra`aitum ing kuntu 'alā bayyinatim mir rabbī wa ātānī raḥmatam min 'indihī fa 'ummiyat 'alaikum, a nulzimukumụhā wa antum lahā kārihụn
11|29|wa yā qaumi l<b>ā</b> as`alukum 'alaihi mālā, in ajriya illā 'alallāhi wa m<b>ā</b> ana biṭāridillażīna āmanụ, innahum mulāqụ rabbihim wa lākinn<b>ī</b> arākum qauman taj-halụn

11|32|qālụ yā nụḥu qad jādaltana fa akṡarta jidālana fa`tinā bimā ta'idun<b>ā</b> ing kunta minaṣ-ṣādiqīn

11|43|qāla sa`āw<b>ī</b> ilā jabaliy ya'ṣimunī minal-m<b>ā</b>`, qāla lā 'āṣimal-yauma min amrillāhi illā mar raḥim, wa ḥāla bainahumal-mauju fa kāna minal-mugraqīn
11|44|wa qīla y<b>ā</b> arḍubla'ī m<b>ā</b>`aki wa yā sam<b>ā</b>`u aqli'ī wa gīḍal-m<b>ā</b>`u wa quḍiyal-amru wastawat 'alal-jụdiyyi wa qīla bu'dal lil-qaumiẓ-ẓālimīn

11|47|qāla rabbi inn<b>ī</b> a'ụżu bika an as`alaka mā laisa lī bihī 'ilm, wa illā tagfir lī wa tar-ḥamn<b>ī</b> akum minal-khāsirīn
11|48|qīla yā nụḥuhbiṭ bisalāmim minnā wa barakātin 'alaika wa 'al<b>ā</b> umamim mim mam ma'ak, wa umamun sanumatti'uhum ṡumma yamassuhum minnā 'ażābun alīm
11|49|tilka min amb<b>ā</b>`il-gaibi nụḥīh<b>ā</b> ilaīk, mā kunta ta'lamuh<b>ā</b> anta wa lā qaumuka ming qabli hāżā, faṣbir, innal-'āqibata lil-muttaqīn

11|58|wa lammā j<b>ā</b>`a amrunā najjainā hụdaw wallażīna āmanụ ma'ahụ biraḥmatim minnā, wa najjaināhum min 'ażābin galīẓ
11|59|wa tilka 'ādun jaḥadụ bi`āyāti rabbihim wa 'aṣau rusulahụ wattaba'<b>ū</b> amra kulli jabbārin 'anīd
